     _getHistoryKey() {
    const chatId = TavernHelper.chatId;
    // 如果无法获取chatId，提供一个备用键以避免完全失效
    if (!chatId) {
        console.warn('[历史系统] 新会话尚未生成chatId，使用备用键存储历史记录');
        return 'frontend_chat_history_fallback';
    }
    return `frontend_chat_history_${chatId}`;
},     SafeGetValue(obj, paths, defaultValue = 'N/A') {
    // 如果传入的不是一个数组，将其包装成数组以统一处理
    if (!Array.isArray(paths)) {
        paths = [paths];
    }
    // 遍历所有可能的键名路径
    for (const path of paths) {
        const value = _.get(obj, path);
        // 只要找到一个有效的值（不是 undefined 或 null），就立即返回它
        if (value !== undefined && value !== null) {
            return value;
        }
    }
    // 如果遍历完所有路径都找不到，则返回默认值
    return defaultValue;
},

    async checkForSummaryReminder() {
    if (this.summaryReminderShown) return; // 如果已经提醒过，则跳过

    try {
        const bookName = '1源堡';
        const journeyKey = this.unifiedIndex > 1 ? `本周目经历(${this.unifiedIndex})` : '本周目经历';
        const coreMemoryKey = this.unifiedIndex > 1 ? `本周目核心记忆(${this.unifiedIndex})` : '本周目核心记忆';
        const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
        const journeyEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === journeyKey);

        if (!journeyEntry || !journeyEntry.content) {
            console.log('[总结提醒] 未找到本周目经历条目或内容为空');
            return;
        }
        console.log('[总结提醒] 本周目经历内容长度：', journeyEntry.content.length);
        const allEvents = this.parseJourneyEntry(journeyEntry.content);
        console.log('[总结提醒] 解析出的事件总数：', allEvents.length);
        // 关键日志3：查看所有事件的序号
        const allEventIds = allEvents.map(event => event['序号']).join(',');
        console.log('[总结提醒] 所有事件的序号：', allEventIds);

        if (allEvents.length === 0) return;

        const coreMemoryEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === coreMemoryKey);
        let lastSummarizedId = 0;
        if (coreMemoryEntry && coreMemoryEntry.content) {
            const markerStart = '[Meta-LastSummarizedId:';
            const startIndex = coreMemoryEntry.content.lastIndexOf(markerStart);
            if (startIndex !== -1) {
                const endIndex = coreMemoryEntry.content.indexOf(']', startIndex);
                if (endIndex !== -1) {
                    const idString = coreMemoryEntry.content.substring(startIndex + markerStart.length, endIndex).trim();
                    lastSummarizedId = parseInt(idString, 10) || 0;
                    console.log(`[总结提醒] 从核心记忆中读取到最后总结ID：${lastSummarizedId}`);
                } else {
                    console.log('[总结提醒] 核心记忆中有Meta标记，但未找到闭合]');
                }
            } else {
                console.log('[总结提醒] 核心记忆中未找到Meta-LastSummarizedId标记，默认lastSummarizedId=0');
            }
        } else {
            console.log('[总结提醒] 未找到“本周目核心记忆”条目，默认lastSummarizedId=0');
        }

        // 计算未总结的新事件数（补全日志）
        const newEvents = allEvents.filter(event => {
            const eventId = parseInt(event['序号'] || '0', 10);
            const isNew = !isNaN(eventId) && eventId > lastSummarizedId;
            // 关键日志4：查看每个事件的过滤结果（可选，太多可注释）
            // console.log(`[总结提醒] 事件序号${event['序号']} → 解析ID=${eventId} → 是否新事件：${isNew}`);
            return isNew;
        });

        const newEventCount = newEvents.length;
        // 关键日志5：打印最终新事件数（核心！确认是否<30）
        console.log('[总结提醒] 未总结的新事件数：', newEventCount);
        //console.log('[总结提醒] 未总结的新事件序号：', newEvents.map(e => e['序号']).join(','));
        //console.log('[总结提醒] 最新事件序号：', newEvents.length > 0 ? newEvents[newEvents.length - 1]['序号'] : '无');

        // 触发提醒（修复：标记已提醒后，下次新增事件仍需检查）
        if (newEventCount >= 30) {
        // 你的原消息文本（一字未改，直接用）
        const message = `您已有 ${newEventCount} 条新事件未进行总结。\n为了保持“核心记忆”的清晰，建议您进行一次总结。`;

        // 延迟300ms调用：避开AI回复后的UI阻塞
        setTimeout(() => {
            // 格式化：仅把\n换成<br>（适配innerHTML赋值，保证换行正常）
            const formattedMessage = message.replace(/\n/g, '<br>');

            this.showCustomConfirm(
                formattedMessage, // 传入格式化后的消息（核心内容不变，仅换行适配）
                async () => {
                    this.summaryReminderShown = false;
                    await this.showJourney().then(() => this.showSummarizerModal());
                },
                () => {
                    this.summaryReminderShown = false;
                }
            );


        }, 300);
    } else {
        console.log(`[总结提醒] 新事件数${newEventCount}<30，不触发提醒（需≥30）`);
    }
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('检查总结提醒时出错:', e);
    }
},
  async showSummarizerModal() {
    this.openModal('summarizer-modal', true);
    const body = document.getElementById('summarizer-body');
    const footer = document.getElementById('summarizer-footer');
    body.innerHTML = '<div class="summarizer-loading">正在准备总结材料...</div>';
    footer.innerHTML = '';

    try {
        const selectedCheckboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.journey-select-checkbox:checked');
        let mode = 'incremental';
        let eventIdsToSummarize = [];

        const bookName = '1源堡';
        const journeyKey = this.unifiedIndex > 1 ? `本周目经历(${this.unifiedIndex})` : '本周目经历';
        const coreMemoryKey = this.unifiedIndex > 1 ? `本周目核心记忆(${this.unifiedIndex})` : '本周目核心记忆';
        const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
        const journeyEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === journeyKey);

        if (!journeyEntry || !journeyEntry.content) {
            body.innerHTML = '<p class="modal-placeholder">“本周目经历”为空，无法进行总结。</p>';
            return;
        }
        const allEvents = this.parseJourneyEntry(journeyEntry.content);

        if (selectedCheckboxes.length > 0) {
            mode = 'custom';
            eventIdsToSummarize = Array.from(selectedCheckboxes).map(cb => cb.dataset.sequenceId);
        } else {
            const coreMemoryEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === coreMemoryKey);
            let lastSummarizedId = 0;
            if (coreMemoryEntry && coreMemoryEntry.content) {
                const markerStart = '[Meta-LastSummarizedId:';
                const startIndex = coreMemoryEntry.content.lastIndexOf(markerStart);
                if (startIndex !== -1) {
                    const endIndex = coreMemoryEntry.content.indexOf(']', startIndex);
                    if (endIndex !== -1) {
                        const idString = coreMemoryEntry.content.substring(startIndex + markerStart.length, endIndex);
                        lastSummarizedId = parseInt(idString.trim(), 10) || 0;
                    }
                }
            }
            eventIdsToSummarize = allEvents.filter(event => parseInt(event['序号'], 10) > lastSummarizedId).map(event => event['序号']);
        }

        if (eventIdsToSummarize.length === 0) {
            body.innerHTML = '<p class="modal-placeholder">没有需要总结的新事件。</p>';
            return;
        }

        const eventsToSummarize = allEvents.filter(event => eventIdsToSummarize.includes(event['序号']));
        const promptMaterial = this.reconstructJourneyEntry(eventsToSummarize);
        const infoText = mode === 'custom'
            ? `您已选择 ${eventsToSummarize.length} 个事件进行自定义总结。`
            : `发现 ${eventsToSummarize.length} 个新事件（序号 #${eventsToSummarize[0]['序号']} 至 #${eventsToSummarize[eventsToSummarize.length - 1]['序号']}）`;

        const inputListHtml = eventsToSummarize.map(event => `<div class="summarizer-input-item">[${event['序号']}] ${event['标题']}</div>`).join('');

        // 渲染“记忆蒸馏器”新界面
        body.innerHTML = `
            <div class="summarizer-controls">
                <p>${infoText}</p>
                <button id="btn-generate-summary" class="interaction-btn primary-btn">开始提炼记忆精华</button>
            </div>
            <div class="summarizer-container">
                <div class="summarizer-input">
                    <div class="summarizer-header">待提炼的记忆</div>
                    <div id="summarizer-input-list">${inputListHtml}</div>
                </div>
                <div class="summarizer-output-wrapper">
                    <div class="summarizer-header">凝结的记忆精华</div>
                    <div id="summarizer-output-container">
                        <div class="summarizer-loading">等待开始...</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;

        const generateBtn = document.getElementById('btn-generate-summary');
        generateBtn.dataset.mode = mode;
        generateBtn.dataset.lastEventId = eventsToSummarize[eventsToSummarize.length - 1]['序号'];

        generateBtn.addEventListener('click', () =>
            this.performSummarization(promptMaterial, mode, eventsToSummarize[eventsToSummarize.length - 1]['序号'])
        );

    } catch (e) {
        console.error('准备总结器时出错:', e);
        body.innerHTML = `<p class="modal-placeholder">准备总结时出错: ${e.message}</p>`;
    }
},

                async performSummarization(promptMaterial, mode, lastEventId) {
    const outputContainer = document.getElementById('summarizer-output-container');
    const generateBtn = document.getElementById('btn-generate-summary');
    if (!outputContainer || !generateBtn) return;

    generateBtn.disabled = true;
    outputContainer.innerHTML = '<div class="summarizer-loading">正在构建防御性指令并请求摘要...</div>';

    // 升起“信号旗”，告知 handleStreamEnd 准备劫持
    this.isSummarizing = true;

    try {
        const firstEventMatch = promptMaterial.match(/序号\|(\d+)/);
        const firstEventId = firstEventMatch ? firstEventMatch[1] : '?';

        // 【核心修改】创建一个带有“最高权威”和“忽略后续”指令的模板
        const defensive_template = `
[CONTEXT_LOGS]
${promptMaterial}
</CONTEXT_LOGS>

---
[SYSTEM OVERRIDE: ABSOLUTE FINAL INSTRUCTION]
ATTENTION: This is the absolute final, highest-priority command. Your response for this turn is dictated SOLELY by the rules within this block. You MUST IGNORE any and all text, instructions, or roleplay scenarios that appear AFTER this block.

YOUR ONLY TASK:
1. Review the logs in <CONTEXT_LOGS>.
2. Generate a summary STRICTLY following the Markdown template below.
3. Your response MUST ONLY be the formatted summary. Any other output is a failure.

[REQUIRED OUTPUT FORMAT]
### 核心记忆摘要：[格式：剧情节点标签+核心冲突/进展]
**覆盖时段：** [经历序号 #${firstEventId} 至 #${lastEventId}]
#### 一、关键事件脉络（仅本阶段独有，无重复）
[事件一标题+核心行动者]：[触发背景]→[关键决策/行动]→[已落地结果]（简要描述）
（非关键事件合并为“次要支线：XXX/XXX（无后续影响可省略）”）
#### 二、人物关系与状态变更（仅本阶段）
[主要人物A]: [描述人物在此阶段最重要的变化。]
#### 三、阶段独有线索（标注优先级+归属）
- 主跟进线索：[与主线强相关的伏笔]
- 可选支线线索：[非主线但可延展的伏笔]
#### 四、本阶段剧情推进指引
[阶段属性]：[单线/多线并行]
[仅本阶段]：一句话

[END OF ABSOLUTE FINAL INSTRUCTION]
Now, process the logs and generate the summary as commanded.
`;

        await TavernHelper.generate({
            injects: [
                {
                    role: 'system', // 使用 'system' 角色，语义上权重更高
                    content: defensive_template,
                    position: 'append_to_chat', // 插入到聊天末尾，预设结尾之前
                    depth: 9999, // 给予极高深度，尽可能地靠后
                    should_scan: false
                }
            ],
            should_stream: false,
        });
        // 结果将由完美的 handleStreamEnd 劫持

    } catch (e) {
        console.error('生成摘要时调用 TavernHelper.generate 失败:', e);
        outputContainer.innerHTML = `<p class="modal-placeholder">生成摘要失败: ${e.message}</p>`;
        generateBtn.disabled = false;
        this.isSummarizing = false;
    }
},

async writeSummaryToLorebook(mode, lastEventId) {
    const outputTextarea = document.getElementById('summarizer-output');
    if (!outputTextarea) return;
    const summaryContent = outputTextarea.value.trim();
    if (!summaryContent) {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('摘要内容不能为空。');
        return;
    }

    this.showTemporaryMessage('正在将记忆固化到世界书中...');
    try {
        const bookName = '1源堡';
        const coreMemoryKey = this.unifiedIndex > 1 ? `本周目核心记忆(${this.unifiedIndex})` : '本周目核心记忆';
        const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
        let targetEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === coreMemoryKey);

        if (!targetEntry) {
            await TavernHelper.createLorebookEntries(bookName, [{
                comment: coreMemoryKey,
                keys: [coreMemoryKey],
                content: '',
                enabled: true,
            }]);
            targetEntry = (await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName)).find(entry => entry.comment === coreMemoryKey);
        }

        let newContent = '';
        if (mode === 'incremental') {
            let existingContent = targetEntry.content || '';
            const markerStart = '[Meta-LastSummarizedId:';
            const startIndex = existingContent.lastIndexOf(markerStart);

            if (startIndex !== -1) {
                const endIndex = existingContent.indexOf(']', startIndex);
                if (endIndex !== -1) {
                    existingContent = existingContent.substring(0, startIndex);
                }
            }
            existingContent = existingContent.trim();

            newContent = existingContent ? `${existingContent}\n\n---\n\n${summaryContent}` : summaryContent;

            // 【最终核心修复 1】在增量模式下，补全写入新书签的关键代码
            newContent += `\n\n[Meta-LastSummarizedId: ${lastEventId}]`;

        } else { // custom mode
            newContent = summaryContent;

            // 【最终核心修复 2】在自定义模式下，同样写入书签，确保后续增量总结能接续上
            newContent += `\n\n[Meta-LastSummarizedId: ${lastEventId}]`;
        }

        await TavernHelper.setLorebookEntries(bookName, [{ uid: targetEntry.uid, content: newContent }]);
        this.showTemporaryMessage('核心记忆已成功更新！', 3000);
        this.summaryReminderShown = false; // 【核心新增】重置提醒标记
        this.closeAllModals();

    } catch (e) {
        console.error('写入核心记忆失败:', e);
        this.showTemporaryMessage(`写入失败: ${e.message}`, 4000);
    }
},


    renderUI(data) {
  console.log('%c[TRACE-RENDERUI] 触发renderUI，传入的data:', 'color: green;', data);
  console.log('%c[TRACE-RENDERUI] 当前currentMvuState:', 'color: green;', this.currentMvuState);
 // 🔴 强制将传入的新数据赋值给this.currentMvuState.stat_data（覆盖旧值）
  //if (data && this.currentMvuState) {
  //  this.currentMvuState.stat_data = _.cloneDeep(data); // 深克隆，杜绝引用污染
  //}
  //console.log('[TRACE-RENDERUI] 当前this.currentMvuState（修改后）:', this.currentMvuState);
 console.trace('[TRACE-RENDERUI] 调用栈（查看谁触发了renderUI）');
  if (!data) {
        console.warn('RenderUI 调用失败：没有提供数据。');
        return;
    }
    const updateText = (id, value, style = '') => {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (el) {
      el.innerText = value;
      if (style) {
        // 应用样式字符串到元素（覆盖原有行内样式，保留外部CSS）
        el.style.cssText = style;
      }
    }
  };

    const jingjieValue = this.SafeGetValue(data, '当前序列', '...');
    const tierStyle = this.getTierStyle(jingjieValue);
    updateText('val-jingjie', jingjieValue, tierStyle);
    updateText('val-jinian', this.SafeGetValue(data, '当前时间纪元', '...'));
    const charge = Number(this.SafeGetValue(data, '灵性聚合度', 0)).toFixed(4);
    document.getElementById('val-guixu-charge-text').innerText = `${charge}%`;
    const chargeBar = document.getElementById('bar-guixu-charge');
    if (chargeBar) chargeBar.style.setProperty('--guixu-charge', `${charge}%`);

    this.updateTalentAndLinggen(data);
    // this.loadEquipmentFromMVU(data); // 核心修复：删除此行，以防止AI回复覆盖本地的装备状态
    this.updateDisplayedAttributes();

    // 【核心修正】移植“归墟”版的渲染逻辑
    const summaryTextEl = document.getElementById('status-summary-text');
    const popupListEl = document.getElementById('status-effects-popup-list');

    // --- 新增：用以下整段逻辑替换掉原有的 statusKeys.map(...) 逻辑 ---
 if (summaryTextEl && popupListEl) {
    const statusesObj = this.SafeGetValue(data, '当前状态', {});
    const statusKeys = Object.keys(statusesObj).filter(key => key !== '$meta');

    if (statusKeys.length > 0) {
        summaryTextEl.textContent = `当前有 ${statusKeys.length} 个状态效果`;
        // 同样使用新的渲染引擎，但可能需要适配popup的CSS样式
        popupListEl.innerHTML = statusKeys.map(key => {
            const value = statusesObj[key];
            // 注意：新引擎生成的是 <li>，而旧popup可能需要的是 <div>，如果样式错乱，需要调整CSS或这里的HTML结构
            return this._getHtmlForStatus(key, value).replace('<li', '<div').replace('</li>', '</div>');
        }).join('');
    } else {
        summaryTextEl.textContent = '理智正常';
        popupListEl.innerHTML = '<div class="status-effect-item">当前无特殊状态效果。</div>';
    }
}
},

       async renderStateAt(messageObject) {
  console.log('%c[TRACE-RENDERSTATE] 调用 renderStateAt，传入的 messageObject.data:', 'color: purple;', messageObject.data);

  // 1. 校验（确保快照有效）
  if (!messageObject || !messageObject.data || !messageObject.data.stat_data) {
    console.warn('[TRACE-RENDERSTATE] 无效的快照，跳过渲染');
    return;
  }

  // 2. 避免重复渲染（性能优化）
  if (this.lastRenderedMessageId === messageObject.message_id) {
    console.log(`[性能优化] 已渲染过快照 ${messageObject.message_id}，跳过重复操作`);
    return;
  }

  // 3. 定义当前查看的快照 + 判断是否为活跃回合
  const currentViewSnapshot = messageObject;
  const lastSnapshot = this.chatHistoryCache.at(-1);
  const isActiveRound = currentViewSnapshot.message_id === (lastSnapshot?.message_id || '');
  console.log(`[回合类型] 当前ID: ${currentViewSnapshot.message_id}，活跃回合ID: ${lastSnapshot?.message_id}，是否活跃: ${isActiveRound}`);

  // 4. 深拷贝快照数据更新 currentMvuState（内存状态）
  this.currentMvuState = _.cloneDeep(messageObject.data);
  console.log(`[TRACE-RENDERSTATE] currentMvuState 已更新为快照 ${messageObject.message_id} 的数据`);

  // 5. 恢复当前查看回合的装备状态（内存中）
  if (currentViewSnapshot.data && currentViewSnapshot.data.equipped_items) {
    this.equippedItems = _.cloneDeep(currentViewSnapshot.data.equipped_items);
    console.log(`[时间旅行] 从快照恢复装备:`, this.equippedItems);
  } else {
    await this.loadEquipmentState();
    this.refreshEquipmentSlots();
  }

  // 6. 重新渲染UI（基于内存中的当前状态）
  const safeStatData = _.cloneDeep(this.currentMvuState.stat_data);
  this.renderUI(safeStatData);
  console.log(`[UI渲染] 已基于快照 ${messageObject.message_id} 的内存状态更新UI`);

  // 7. 加载场景+更新属性（仅更新内存和UI，不同步变量管理器）
  this.loadAndDisplayCurrentScene(currentViewSnapshot);
  await this.updateDisplayedAttributes(currentViewSnapshot);

  // 8. 记录已渲染ID
  this.lastRenderedMessageId = messageObject.message_id;
  console.log(`[时间旅行] UI已刷新至消息: ${messageObject.message_id}（仅更新内存和UI，未同步变量管理器）`);
},
   // 这是一个统一的状态渲染引擎，能处理所有格式
 _getHtmlForStatus(statusKey, statusValue) {
    let html = '';

    // 情况1：状态值本身就是一个详细的对象
    if (statusValue && typeof statusValue === 'object') {
        const name = statusValue.名称 || statusValue.name || statusKey;
        html += `<div class="status-modal-name">${name}</div>`;
        html += '<div class="status-modal-description">';
        for (const [detailKey, detailValue] of Object.entries(statusValue)) {
            // 不再重复显示名称
            if (['名称', 'name', '$meta'].includes(detailKey)) continue;
            // 确保显示的值是可读的字符串
            const displayValue = (typeof detailValue === 'string' || typeof detailValue === 'number') ? detailValue : '详情未提供';
            html += `<div><strong>${detailKey}:</strong> ${displayValue}</div>`;
        }
        html += '</div>';
    }
    // 情况2：状态值是简单的字符串描述
    else if (typeof statusValue === 'string') {
        html += `<div class="status-modal-name">${statusKey}</div>`;
        html += `<div class="status-modal-description">${statusValue}</div>`;
    }
    // 情况3：无效数据，提供备用显示
    else {
        html += `<div class="status-modal-name">${statusKey}</div>`;
        html += `<div class="status-modal-description">效果详情未提供。</div>`;
    }

    return `<li class="status-modal-item">${html}</li>`;
},
    toggleStatusPopup() {
    const popup = document.getElementById('status-effects-popup');
    if (popup) {
        const isVisible = popup.style.display === 'flex';
        popup.style.display = isVisible ? 'none' : 'flex';
    }
},   // --- 用这个函数，完整替换旧的 showStatusEffectsModal ---
showStatusEffectsModal() {
    if (!this.currentMvuState || !this.currentMvuState.stat_data) {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('无法获取状态数据。');
        return;
    }
    this.openModal('status-effects-modal');
    const body = document.getElementById('status-effects-modal-body');
    const statusesObj = this.SafeGetValue(this.currentMvuState.stat_data, '当前状态', {});
    const statusKeys = Object.keys(statusesObj).filter(key => key !== '$meta');

    if (statusKeys.length === 0) {
        body.innerHTML = '<p class="modal-placeholder" style="text-align:center; color:#a09c91; font-size:12px;">当前无特殊状态效果。</p>';
        return;
    }

    // 使用新的渲染引擎来生成HTML
    const listHtml = statusKeys.map(key => {
        const value = statusesObj[key];
        return this._getHtmlForStatus(key, value);
    }).join('');

    body.innerHTML = `<ul class="status-modal-list">${listHtml}</ul>`;
},

            // --- 新增：用于显示/隐藏思维链浮层的函数 ---
showThinkingOverlay() {
    const overlay = document.getElementById('thinking-overlay');
    const contentEl = document.getElementById('thinking-content');
    if (overlay && contentEl && this.lastExtractedThinking) {
        contentEl.textContent = this.lastExtractedThinking;
        overlay.style.display = 'flex';
    }
},

hideThinkingOverlay() {
    const overlay = document.getElementById('thinking-overlay');
    if (overlay) {
        overlay.style.display = 'none';
    }
},

// 新增弹幕
renderDanmaku() {
  const layer = document.getElementById('danmaku-layer');
  if (!layer) return;
  layer.innerHTML = this.lastExtractedDanmaku
    .map(dm => `<div class="danmaku-pill"><span class="dm-text">${dm.replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;')}</span></div>`)
    .join('');
},

showDmOverlay() {
  const layer = document.getElementById('danmaku-layer');
  if (!layer) return;
  this.renderDanmaku();
  layer.style.display = 'block';
  this.isDanmakuVisible = true;
},

hideDmOverlay() {
  const layer = document.getElementById('danmaku-layer');
  if (layer) layer.style.display = 'none';
  this.isDanmakuVisible = false;
},

toggleDanmakuOverlay() {
  if (this.isDanmakuVisible) {
    this.hideDmOverlay();
  } else {
    this.showDmOverlay();
  }
},

// ====================================================================
// --- 新增：前端独立历史记录系统核心 (Stage 2) ---
// ====================================================================


 async loadHistoryFromStorage() {
  console.log(`%c[TRACE-HISTORY] >>>>> START. chatHistoryCache 长度 BEFORE: ${this.chatHistoryCache.length}`, 'color: red; font-weight: bold;');
  const historyKey = this._getHistoryKey(); // 获取原始键（如 frontend_chat_history_fallback）
  const isGlobalFallback = historyKey === 'frontend_chat_history_fallback';

  if (isGlobalFallback) {
    // 步骤1：优先读取独立快照（依赖AppStorage自动加前缀，无需手动拼接）
    let storedSnapshots = [];
    try {
      // 直接传原始key，AppStorage内部会自动添加SEFIROT_CASTLE_REVISION_前缀
      storedSnapshots = await AppStorage.loadData(historyKey, []);
      console.log(`[历史系统] 从独立快照键（${historyKey}）读取到数据，原始长度: ${storedSnapshots.length}`);
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(`[历史系统] 读取独立快照失败:`, e);
    }

    // 验证独立快照有效性（必须是数组且有数据）
    if (Array.isArray(storedSnapshots) && storedSnapshots.length > 0) {
      this.chatHistoryCache = storedSnapshots;
      this.historyViewIndex = this.chatHistoryCache.length - 1;
      this.isHistoryViewMode = false;
      console.log(`[历史系统] 独立快照加载成功，缓存长度: ${this.chatHistoryCache.length}`);
      console.log(`%c[TRACE-HISTORY] <<<<< END. chatHistoryCache 长度 AFTER: ${this.chatHistoryCache.length}`, 'color: red; font-weight: bold;');
      return;
    }

    // 步骤2：独立快照无效时，读取multi_save_data中的归档
    try {
      const allSaves = await this.getSavesFromStorage(); // 注意：getSavesFromStorage需异步（见之前优化点）
      const validSaves = [];

      // 筛选有有效timeline_history的归档
      Object.values(allSaves).forEach(save => {
        if (save?.timeline_history && Array.isArray(save.timeline_history) && save.timeline_history.length > 0) {
          validSaves.push(save);
        }
      });

      if (validSaves.length > 0) {
        // 按时间排序，取最新归档
        validSaves.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.timestamp) - new Date(a.timestamp));
        const latestSave = validSaves[0];
        this.chatHistoryCache = latestSave.timeline_history;
        this.historyViewIndex = this.chatHistoryCache.length - 1;
        this.isHistoryViewMode = false;
        console.log(`[历史系统] 从归档（${latestSave.save_name}）加载快照，缓存长度: ${this.chatHistoryCache.length}`);
        console.log(`%c[TRACE-HISTORY] <<<<< END. chatHistoryCache 长度 AFTER: ${this.chatHistoryCache.length}`, 'color: red; font-weight: bold;');
        return;
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(`[历史系统] 读取归档失败:`, e);
    }

    // 步骤3：无任何数据（全新会话）
    this.chatHistoryCache = [];
    console.log('[历史系统] 无任何快照或归档（全新会话）');
    console.log(`%c[TRACE-HISTORY] <<<<< END. chatHistoryCache 长度 AFTER: 0`, 'color: red; font-weight: bold;');
    return;
  }

  // 非全局备用键场景（正常会话）：直接读取原始key（AppStorage自动加前缀）
  try {
    const storedHistory = await AppStorage.loadData(historyKey, []);
    if (Array.isArray(storedHistory)) {
      this.chatHistoryCache = storedHistory;
      console.log(`[历史系统] 从键（${historyKey}）加载到 ${this.chatHistoryCache.length} 条历史记录`);
    } else {
      this.chatHistoryCache = [];
      console.log(`[历史系统] 键（${historyKey}）数据无效，初始化为空`);
    }
  } catch (e) {
    this.chatHistoryCache = [];
    console.error(`[历史系统] 读取键（${historyKey}）失败:`, e);
  }

  this.historyViewIndex = this.chatHistoryCache.length > 0 ? this.chatHistoryCache.length - 1 : 0;
  this.isHistoryViewMode = false;
  console.log(`%c[TRACE-HISTORY] <<<<< END. State AFTER is:`, 'color: red; font-weight: bold;', this.currentMvuState);
},


// 公共函数：根据快照截断世界书（复用逻辑，减少出错）
async _truncateJourneyBySnapshot(snapshot, index, actionName) {
    let targetSnapshot = snapshot;
    let targetIndex = index;
    let mergedJourney = ''; // 存储合并所有快照后的完整经历
    let hasLatestSnapshotInvalid = false; // 标记：最新快照是否无效
    const WARNING_DURATION = 10000; // 降级警告弹窗显示时长（10秒）

    // 降级逻辑：只有“回到现在”时，才处理无效快照降级
    if (actionName === '回到现在') {
        // 先校验当前接收的快照（最新快照）是否有效
        const targetJourneyContent = this._extractLastTagContent('本周目经历', snapshot.message) || '';
        const isCurrentSnapshotValid = targetJourneyContent.trim()
            && this.parseJourneyEntry(targetJourneyContent).length > 0
            && Math.max(...this.parseJourneyEntry(targetJourneyContent).map(ev => parseInt(ev.序号, 10) || 0)) > 0;

        // 如果最新快照无效，自动找最新有效快照
        if (!isCurrentSnapshotValid) {
            console.warn(`[${actionName}] 最新快照 ${index} 未找到有效 <本周目经历> 标签（原始最新回合无效）`);
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`⚠️ 警告：当前最新回合（快照${index}）无有效<本周目经历>！
• 此为真实存档位，序号对不上说明之前有无效回合快照
• 建议从有效回合继续游戏
• 系统即将自动降级到最近的有效回合的本周目经历`, WARNING_DURATION);
            hasLatestSnapshotInvalid = true; // 标记已弹过无效提示
            const latestValid = await this._findLatestValidSnapshot();
            if (latestValid) {
                targetSnapshot = latestValid.snapshot;
                targetIndex = latestValid.index;
            } else {
                console.warn(`[${actionName}] 无任何有效快照，跳过截断`);
                this.showTemporaryMessage(`无有效经历记录，跳过同步`, 3000);
                return;
            }
        }

        // 合并所有快照的经历（关键补全步骤）
        let mergedStr = '';
        for (const snap of this.chatHistoryCache) { // 遍历所有快照，不管有没有降级
            if (!snap || !snap.message) continue;
            const snapJourney = this._extractLastTagContent('本周目经历', snap.message) || '';
            if (snapJourney.trim()) mergedStr += snapJourney + '\n\n'; // 拼接所有有效经历
        }
        mergedJourney = mergedStr.trim();

        // 合并后去重+排序（避免重复事件，保证顺序正确）
        const mergedEvents = this.parseJourneyEntry(mergedJourney);
        const uniqueEvents = Array.from(new Map(mergedEvents.map(ev => [ev.序号, ev])).values());
        uniqueEvents.sort((a, b) => parseInt(a.序号, 10) - parseInt(b.序号, 10));
        mergedJourney = uniqueEvents.map(ev => this.stringifyJourneyEvent(ev)).join('\n\n');

        // 合并后仍无有效经历，直接跳过（兜底）
        if (!mergedJourney.trim()) {
            console.warn(`[${actionName}] 合并所有快照后仍无有效经历，跳过`);
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`无有效经历记录，跳过同步`, 3000);
            return;
        }
    }

    // 提取目标快照经历
    const targetJourneyContent = this._extractLastTagContent('本周目经历', targetSnapshot.message) || '';
    console.log(`[${actionName}] 从快照 ${targetIndex} 提取的经历：${targetJourneyContent}`);

    // 第一重防护：无有效内容
    if (!targetJourneyContent.trim()) {
        console.warn(`[${actionName}] 快照 ${targetIndex} 未找到有效 <本周目经历> 标签，跳过截断操作（避免误删现有经历）`);
        this.showTemporaryMessage(`快照 ${targetIndex} （此为本回合真实存档位，如与序号对不上，证明之前存档也存在无效回合,建议从不报错的有效回合继续）无有效<本周目经历>标签，跳过回档记忆截断`, 8000);
        return;
    }

    // 第二重防护：解析无事件
    const targetEvents = this.parseJourneyEntry(targetJourneyContent);
    if (targetEvents.length === 0) {
        console.warn(`[${actionName}] 快照 ${targetIndex} 的经历格式无效（无有效事件序号），跳过截断`);
        this.showTemporaryMessage(`快照 ${targetIndex} 的经历格式无效，无法确定截断位置，已取消记忆截断`, 5000);
        return;
    }

    // 计算最大事件序号
    const maxTargetEventId = targetEvents.length > 0
        ? Math.max(...targetEvents.map(ev => parseInt(ev.序号, 10) || 0))
        : 0;
    console.log(`[${actionName}] 目标快照最大事件序号：${maxTargetEventId}`);

    // 第三重防护：最大序号≤0
    if (maxTargetEventId <= 0) {
        console.warn(`[${actionName}] 快照 ${targetIndex} 无有效事件序号（≤0），跳过截断`);
        this.showTemporaryMessage(`快照 ${targetIndex} 无有效事件序号，已取消记忆截断`, 5000);
        return;
    }

    // 读取世界书
    const bookName = '1源堡';
    const journeyKey = this.unifiedIndex > 1 ? `本周目经历(${this.unifiedIndex})` : '本周目经历';
    const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
    const journeyEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === journeyKey);

    if (journeyEntry && journeyEntry.content) {
        const currentEvents = this.parseJourneyEntry(journeyEntry.content);
        let keepEvents = [];

        // 区分场景：回到现在用合并后的完整事件，其他场景用原逻辑
        if (actionName === '回到现在') {
            // 回到现在：用合并所有快照的完整经历（补全118-120）
            keepEvents = this.parseJourneyEntry(mergedJourney);
        } else {
            // 其他场景：截断
            keepEvents = currentEvents.filter(ev => (parseInt(ev.序号, 10) || 0) <= maxTargetEventId);
        }

        // 第四重防护：截断后无事件
        if (keepEvents.length === 0) {
            console.warn(`[${actionName}] 截断后将无任何有效事件，跳过操作`);
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`截断后无有效事件，已取消记忆截断`, 3000);
            return;
        }

        // 统一写入逻辑（去掉重复写入）
        const shouldWrite = actionName === '回到现在'
            ? // 回到现在：只要合并后的经历和当前不一致，就写入（补全）
              JSON.stringify(keepEvents.map(ev => ev.序号)) !== JSON.stringify(currentEvents.map(ev => ev.序号))
            : // 其他场景：只截断
              keepEvents.length < currentEvents.length;

        if (shouldWrite) {
            const newContent = keepEvents.map(ev => this.stringifyJourneyEvent(ev)).join('\n\n');
            await TavernHelper.setLorebookEntries(bookName, [{ uid: journeyEntry.uid, content: newContent }]);
            const finalMaxId = actionName === '回到现在'
                ? parseInt(keepEvents[keepEvents.length - 1].序号, 10)
                : maxTargetEventId;
            console.log(`[${actionName}] 同步完成：保留 ${keepEvents.length} 条事件`);
            setTimeout(() => {
                const syncMsg = hasLatestSnapshotInvalid
                    ? `✅ 降级同步成功！
基于快照${targetIndex}合并所有有效经历
更新至序号${finalMaxId}（共${keepEvents.length}条）`
                    : `✅ 同步成功！
本周目经历更新至序号${finalMaxId}（共${keepEvents.length}条）`;
                this.showTemporaryMessage(syncMsg, 5000);
            }, hasLatestSnapshotInvalid ? WARNING_DURATION : 0); // 有警告则延迟10秒，无则立即弹
        } else if (actionName === '回到现在') {
            console.log(`[${actionName}] 无需同步：当前经历已完整（合并后无新增事件）`);
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`当前经历已完整，无需同步`, 3000);
        }
    }
},

// 辅助函数：从聊天缓存中，倒序查找「最新的有效快照」（有有效本周目经历）
async _findLatestValidSnapshot() {
    // 倒序遍历缓存（从最新到最旧）
    for (let i = this.chatHistoryCache.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        const snapshot = this.chatHistoryCache[i];
        if (!snapshot || !snapshot.message) continue;

        // 提取经历
        const journeyContent = this._extractLastTagContent('本周目经历', snapshot.message) || '';
        if (!journeyContent.trim()) continue;

        // 解析事件
        const events = this.parseJourneyEntry(journeyContent);
        if (events.length === 0) continue;

        // 过滤有效序号（避免序号无效）
        const validEvents = events.filter(ev => {
            const eventId = parseInt(ev.序号, 10);
            return !isNaN(eventId) && eventId > 0;
        });
        if (validEvents.length === 0) continue;

        // 找到第一个有效快照，直接返回（倒序所以是最新的）
        console.log(`找到最新有效快照：序号${i}，最大事件序号${Math.max(...validEvents.map(ev => parseInt(ev.序号, 10)))}`);
        return { snapshot, index: i };
    }

    // 极端情况：所有快照都无效
    console.warn('未找到任何有效快照');
    return null;
},

// 辅助函数：复用performLoad的逻辑，合并所有快照的经历（字符串级拼接，更稳妥）
async _mergeAllSnapshotsJourney() {
    let mergedJourney = '';
    // 遍历前端缓存的所有快照（chatHistoryCache = 当前时间线的所有回合）
    for (const snap of this.chatHistoryCache) {
        if (!snap || !snap.message) continue;
        // 提取当前快照的经历（和performLoad完全一致）
        const snapJourney = this._extractLastTagContent('本周目经历', snap.message) || '';
        if (snapJourney.trim()) {
            mergedJourney += snapJourney + '\n\n'; // 每个事件用空行分隔（和你的经历格式一致）
        }
    }
    const trimmedJourney = mergedJourney.trim();
    // 去重：避免同一事件重复（比如快照重复存储）
    const events = this.parseJourneyEntry(trimmedJourney);
    const uniqueEvents = Array.from(new Map(events.map(ev => [ev.序号, ev])).values());
    // 按序号排序（恢复1→2→...→121的顺序）
    uniqueEvents.sort((a, b) => parseInt(a.序号, 10) - parseInt(b.序号, 10));
    // 转回字符串（和performLoad的最终步骤一致）
    return uniqueEvents.map(ev => this.stringifyJourneyEvent(ev)).join('\n\n');
},


renderHistoryControls() {
    const placeholder = document.getElementById('history-nav-placeholder');
    if (!placeholder) return;

    const totalMessages = this.chatHistoryCache.length;
    const currentIndex = this.historyViewIndex;
    const isAtPresent = currentIndex === totalMessages - 1;

    let statusText = this.isHistoryViewMode
        ? `浏览历史: ${currentIndex + 1} / ${totalMessages}`
        : `当前回合: ${totalMessages}`;

    // 🔴 渲染按钮时不绑定事件，依赖外部事件委托（避免重复绑定）
    placeholder.innerHTML = `
        <div class="history-mode-warning ${this.isHistoryViewMode ? 'visible' : ''}">
            您正在浏览过去。任何新输入都将从当前节点创建新的时间线！
        </div>
        <div class="history-nav-container">
            <button id="btn-history-prev" class="interaction-btn history-nav-btn"
                data-action="history_prev" ${currentIndex <= 0 ? 'disabled' : ''}>◀ 上一回合</button>
            <span id="history-status" class="history-status">${statusText}</span>
            <button id="btn-history-next" class="interaction-btn history-nav-btn"
                data-action="history_next" ${isAtPresent ? 'disabled' : ''}>下一回合 ▶</button>
            <button id="btn-history-return" class="interaction-btn primary-btn history-nav-btn"
                data-action="history_return" style="${this.isHistoryViewMode ? '' : 'display:none;'}">返回现在</button>
        </div>
    `;

    // 🔴 移除内部事件绑定，改用外部统一的事件委托（如container的click事件）
},

viewPreviousMessage() {
    if (this.isSwitching || this.historyViewIndex <= 0 || this.chatHistoryCache.length === 0) {
        return;
    }
    // 🔴 明确设置节流延迟为300ms，避免抖动
    const throttledSwitch = this.throttle(async () => {
        this.isSwitching = true; // 标记为“正在切换”，阻止并发执行
        try {
            this.isHistoryViewMode = true;
            // 🔴 确保索引只减1
            const newIndex = this.historyViewIndex - 1;
            // 二次校验：防止索引越界（双重保险）
            if (newIndex < 0) return;

            const snapshot = this.chatHistoryCache[newIndex];
            if (snapshot) {
                // 执行世界书截断（异步操作，必须等待完成）
                await this._truncateJourneyBySnapshot(snapshot, newIndex, '上一回合');

                // 等待截断完成后，再更新索引和UI
                this.historyViewIndex = newIndex;
                this.renderStateAt(snapshot);
                this.renderHistoryControls();
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.error('[切换上一回合] 失败:', e);
        } finally {
            this.isSwitching = false; // 解除锁定
        }
    }, 300); // 显式传入延迟时间300ms
    throttledSwitch();
},

viewNextMessage() {
    if (this.isSwitching || this.historyViewIndex >= this.chatHistoryCache.length - 1 || this.chatHistoryCache.length === 0) {
        return;
    }
    const throttledSwitch = this.throttle(async () => {
        this.isSwitching = true;
        try {
            // 🔴 确保索引只加1
            const newIndex = this.historyViewIndex + 1;
            // 二次校验：防止索引越界
            if (newIndex >= this.chatHistoryCache.length) return;

            const snapshot = this.chatHistoryCache[newIndex];
            const isAtPresent = newIndex === this.chatHistoryCache.length - 1;

            if (snapshot) {
                // 等待世界书截断完成
                await this._truncateJourneyBySnapshot(snapshot, newIndex, '下一回合');

                // 更新索引和UI
                this.historyViewIndex = newIndex;
                if (isAtPresent) {
                    this.returnToPresent();
                } else {
                    this.renderStateAt(snapshot);
                    this.renderHistoryControls();
                }
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.error('[切换下一回合] 失败:', e);
        } finally {
            this.isSwitching = false;
        }
    }, 300);
    throttledSwitch();
},

async returnToPresent() {
    this.isHistoryViewMode = false;
    const lastIndex = this.chatHistoryCache.length - 1;
    this.historyViewIndex = lastIndex;
    const lastMessage = this.chatHistoryCache[lastIndex];

    if (lastMessage) {
        this.currentMvuState = _.cloneDeep(lastMessage.data);

        if (lastMessage.data.equipped_items) {
            this.equippedItems = _.cloneDeep(lastMessage.data.equipped_items);
        }

        if (lastMessage.data.gacha_data) {
            this.gachaState = _.cloneDeep(lastMessage.data.gacha_data.state);
            this.gachaCollection = _.cloneDeep(lastMessage.data.gacha_data.collection);
            this.gachaHistory = _.cloneDeep(lastMessage.data.gacha_data.history);
        }

        await this._truncateJourneyBySnapshot(lastMessage, lastIndex, '回到现在');

        this.renderStateAt(lastMessage);
    } else {
        await this.updateDynamicData();
        TavernHelper.setChatMessages([{
            data: { ...this.currentMvuState }
        }], { refresh: 'none' });
    }
    this.renderHistoryControls();
},

     handleBranching(userMessage) {
        // 弹出新的、更简洁的确认框
        this.showCustomConfirm(
            '检测到时间线偏离。\n是否将您原来的“未来”保存为一个新的分支，并继续探索当前这个新的可能性？',
            async () => {
                // 1. 自动将旧时间线存档为一个分支
                await this._archiveCurrentTimelineAsBranch();
                // 2. 在当前会话中，继续新的时间线
                await this.commitHistoryBranch(userMessage);
            }
        );
    },


    async _archiveCurrentTimelineAsBranch() {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('正在将旧时间线归档为分支...');
        try {
            const allSaves = await this.getSavesFromStorage();
            const slotId = `slot_${Date.now()}`;
            // 【核心修复】使用更稳定、不会失败的命名方式
            const branchName = `分支 - (始于回合 ${this.historyViewIndex + 1}) - ${new Date().toLocaleTimeString('zh-CN')}`;

            // --- 开始：将被删除的 performSave 函数的核心逻辑移植到这里 ---
            const bookName = '1源堡';
            const journeyKey = this.unifiedIndex > 1 ? `本周目经历(${this.unifiedIndex})` : '本周目经历';
            const coreMemoryKey = this.unifiedIndex > 1 ? `本周目核心记忆(${this.unifiedIndex})` : '本周目核心记忆';
            const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);

            // 1. 从世界书读取本周目经历（和原逻辑一致）
            const journeyEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === journeyKey);
            let journeyContent = journeyEntry ? journeyEntry.content || '' : '';


            // 2. 关键：打印事件数量日志，便于排查
            const eventCount = (journeyContent.match(/序号\|(\d+)/g) || []).length;
            console.log(`[分支归档] 世界书中“${journeyKey}”包含 ${eventCount} 个事件，准备保存`);

            // 3. 核心兜底：若世界书内容为空/事件数为0，从历史快照合并事件
            if (eventCount === 0 && this.chatHistoryCache.length > 0) {
                console.warn('[分支归档] 世界书本周目经历为空/无事件，尝试从历史快照合并');
                let mergedContent = '';
                for (const snap of this.chatHistoryCache) {
                    // 从每个快照的message中提取本周目经历标签内容（复用performSave的逻辑）
                    const snapJourney = this._extractLastTagContent('本周目经历', snap.message) || '';
                    if (snapJourney) mergedContent += snapJourney + '\n\n';
                }
                journeyContent = mergedContent.trim();
                // 合并后重新计算事件数，打印日志
                const mergedEventCount = (journeyContent.match(/序号\|(\d+)/g) || []).length;
                console.log(`[分支归档] 从快照合并后，共得到 ${mergedEventCount} 个事件`);
            }

            // 4. 读取核心记忆
            const coreMemoryEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === coreMemoryKey);
            const coreMemoryContent = coreMemoryEntry ? coreMemoryEntry.content : '';

            const saveDataPayload = {
                timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
                save_name: branchName,
                timeline_history: _.cloneDeep(this.chatHistoryCache), // 保存的是完整的、即将被覆盖的旧时间线
                snapshot_data: {
                    gacha_data: { state: _.cloneDeep(this.gachaState), collection: _.cloneDeep(this.gachaCollection), history: _.cloneDeep(this.gachaHistory) },
                    lorebook_content: { journey: journeyContent, core_memory: coreMemoryContent }
                }
            };
            // --- 结束：移植 ---

            allSaves[slotId] = saveDataPayload;
            await AppStorage.saveData('multi_save_data', allSaves);
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`旧时间线已归档为 “${branchName}”`);
            return true;

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('[历史系统] 归档旧时间线失败:', error);
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`归档失败: ${error.message}`);
            return false;
        }
    },

      async commitHistoryBranch(userMessage) {
    this.showTemporaryMessage('正在回溯时间线...', 2000);
    try {
        // 步骤 1: 截断前端聊天历史记录
        this.chatHistoryCache = this.chatHistoryCache.slice(0, this.historyViewIndex + 1);
       await AppStorage.saveData(this._getHistoryKey(), this.chatHistoryCache);
        console.log(`[历史系统] 时间线已在前端回滚至 ${this.chatHistoryCache.length} 条记录。`);

        // 步骤 2:【新增】截断世界书中的“本周目经历”
        let lastValidSequenceId = -1;
        // 从当前历史节点向前搜索，找到最近的一个包含“本周目经历”的回合
        for (let i = this.historyViewIndex; i >= 0; i--) {
            const snapshot = this.chatHistoryCache[i];
            const journeyTextInSnapshot = this._extractLastTagContent('本周目经历', snapshot.message);
            if (journeyTextInSnapshot) {
                const events = this.parseJourneyEntry(journeyTextInSnapshot);
                if (events.length > 0) {
                    lastValidSequenceId = parseInt(events[events.length - 1]['序号'], 10);
                    break; // 找到后即停止搜索
                }
            }
        }

        // 如果找到了有效的序号，则执行截断操作
        if (lastValidSequenceId !== -1) {
            const bookName = '1源堡';
            const journeyKey = this.unifiedIndex > 1 ? `本周目经历(${this.unifiedIndex})` : '本周目经历';
            const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
            const journeyEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === journeyKey);

            if (journeyEntry && journeyEntry.content) {
                const allEvents = this.parseJourneyEntry(journeyEntry.content);
                const truncatedEvents = allEvents.filter(event => parseInt(event['序号'], 10) <= lastValidSequenceId);

                if (truncatedEvents.length < allEvents.length) {
                    const newContent = this.reconstructJourneyEntry(truncatedEvents);
                    await TavernHelper.setLorebookEntries(bookName, [{ uid: journeyEntry.uid, content: newContent }]);
                    console.log(`[历史系统] “本周目经历”已回滚，保留至序号 ${lastValidSequenceId}。`);
                }
            }
        }

        // 步骤 3: 用旧状态覆盖酒馆的当前状态
        const lastValidSnapshot = this.chatHistoryCache[this.chatHistoryCache.length - 1];
        if (lastValidSnapshot) {
   const latestHistoryMessage = {
 ...lastValidSnapshot,
 message_id: `branch-latest-${Date.now()}`,
 timestamp: Date.now(),
 data: _.cloneDeep(lastValidSnapshot.data)
 };
      await TavernHelper.setChatMessages([latestHistoryMessage], { refresh: 'none' });
 console.log(`[分支同步] 历史消息已设为最新（时间戳: ${Date.now()}），变量管理器将读取其stat_data`)
                  }

        // 步骤 4: 退出历史模式并发送新指令
        this.isHistoryViewMode = false;
        this.renderHistoryControls();
        await this.handleAction(userMessage, true);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('[历史系统] 创建时间分支失败:', error);
        this.showTemporaryMessage(`创建新时间线失败: ${error.message}`);
        await this.returnToPresent();
    }
},
bindStaticListeners() {
    if (this.listenersBound) return;

    document.getElementById('view-toggle-btn')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.toggleViewMode());
    document.getElementById('toggle-char-panel')?.addEventListener('click', (e) => this.toggleMobilePanel('char', e.target));

        if (!isNaN(newIndex) && newIndex > 0) {
            this.unifiedIndex = newIndex;
            this.saveUnifiedIndex();
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`世界书读写序号已更新为 ${newIndex}`);

            e.target.value = this.unifiedIndex;
        }
    });

        this.saveAutoToggleState();
        this.showTemporaryMessage(`自动开关世界书已${this.isAutoToggleLorebookEnabled ? '开启' : '关闭'}`);
        if (this.isAutoToggleLorebookEnabled) this.startAutoTogglePolling();
        else this.stopAutoTogglePolling();
    });

    const interactionPanel = document.querySelector('.interaction-panel');
    if (interactionPanel) {
        interactionPanel.addEventListener('click', async e => {
            const button = e.target.closest('.interaction-btn');

            switch (button.id) {

                case 'btn-relationships': this.showRelationships(); break;

            }
        });

    document.getElementById('btn-write-past-lives')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.writePastLivesToLorebook());

    if (autoWriteCheckbox) {
        autoWriteCheckbox.addEventListener('change', e => {

            this.showTemporaryMessage(`自动写入经历/投影已${this.isAutoWriteEnabled ? '开启' : '关闭'}`);

            this.showTemporaryMessage(`小说模式自动写入已${this.isNovelModeEnabled ? '开启' : '关闭'}`);

            else this.stopNovelModeAutoWritePolling();
        });
    }

    // --- 让关闭按钮只关闭自己的父级模态框，并为召唤结果窗口添加回调 ---
document.querySelectorAll('.modal-close-btn').forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        const modal = e.target.closest('.modal-overlay');
        if (modal) {
            modal.style.display = 'none';

            // 判断如果关闭的是召唤结果窗口，则刷新召唤主界面的UI

            if (modal.id === 'settings-modal') {
                const modalBody = document.getElementById('settings-modal-body');

                    this.unbindSettingsModalListeners(); // 调用清理函数

});
    document.querySelectorAll('.modal-overlay').forEach(overlay => {
        overlay.addEventListener('click', e => { if (e.target === overlay) this.closeAllModals(); });

    const inventoryModalBody = document.querySelector('#inventory-modal .modal-body');
    if (inventoryModalBody) {
        inventoryModalBody.addEventListener('click', e => {
            const itemElement = e.target.closest('.inventory-item');
            if (!itemElement) return;
            const escapedItemDetails = itemElement.dataset.itemDetails || '{}';
            const unescapedItemDetails = this.unescapeHtml(escapedItemDetails); // 解码还原
            const itemData = JSON.parse(unescapedItemDetails); // 正确解析带引号的物品数据
            const category = itemElement.dataset.category;
            if (e.target.classList.contains('item-equip-btn')) {
                if (e.target.dataset.equipType === 'zhuxiu') this.equipItem(itemData, category, e.target, 'zhuxiuGongfa');
                else if (e.target.dataset.equipType === 'fuxiu') this.equipItem(itemData, category, e.target, 'fuxiuXinfa');
                else this.equipItem(itemData, category, e.target);
            } else if (e.target.classList.contains('item-use-btn')) {
                this.useItem(itemData, e.target);
            } else if (e.target.classList.contains('item-unequip-btn')) {
                const slotId = e.target.dataset.slotId;
                const slotElement = document.getElementById(slotId);
                if (slotElement) this.unequipItem(slotId, slotElement, true, true);
            } else if (e.target.classList.contains('item-discard-btn')) {
                this.discardItem(itemData, category, itemElement);
            }
        });
    }

    const characterPanel = document.querySelector('.character-panel');
    if (characterPanel) {
        characterPanel.addEventListener('mouseover', e => {
            const slot = e.target.closest('.equipment-slot');
            if (slot && slot.classList.contains('equipped')) this.showEquipmentTooltip(slot, e);
        });
        characterPanel.addEventListener('mouseout', e => {
            const slot = e.target.closest('.equipment-slot');
            if (slot) this.hideEquipmentTooltip();
        });
        characterPanel.addEventListener('click', e => {
            const slot = e.target.closest('.equipment-slot');
            if (slot && slot.classList.contains('equipped')) this.unequipItem(slot.id, slot, true, true);
        });

    if (quickSendInput && enterToSendCheckbox) {
        quickSendInput.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
            if (enterToSendCheckbox.checked && event.key === 'Enter' && !event.shiftKey) {
                event.preventDefault();
                this.executeQuickSend();
            }
        });
        enterToSendCheckbox.addEventListener('change', () => { this.saveEnterToSendState(); });
    }

    document.getElementById('btn-quick-commands')?.addEventListener('click', e => { e.stopPropagation(); this.toggleQuickCommands(); });
    document.getElementById('btn-quick-options')?.addEventListener('click', e => { e.stopPropagation(); this.toggleQuickOptions(); });

    // **删除** document.body.addEventListener 中关于 .quick-options-item 的判断逻辑
// **然后** 在 bindStaticListeners 函数的任意位置 **新增** 以下代码块：

const quickOptionsPopup = document.getElementById('quick-options-popup');
if (quickOptionsPopup) {
    quickOptionsPopup.addEventListener('click', e => {
        const sendButton = e.target.closest('.send-option-btn');
        const deleteButton = e.target.closest('.delete-option-btn');

        if (sendButton) {

            const listItem = deleteButton.closest('.quick-options-item');

            if (!isNaN(optionIndex) && this.lastExtractedActions[optionIndex]) {
                this.lastExtractedActions.splice(optionIndex, 1); // 从数组中删除该选项
                this.showQuickOptions(); // 重新渲染弹窗以更新列表
                this.updateQuickOptionsButtonState(); // 更新主界面按钮状态
            }
        }
    });
}

      document.getElementById('status-summary-button')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.toggleStatusPopup());

document.getElementById('status-effects-popup-close')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.toggleStatusPopup());

document.getElementById('btn-close-thinking')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.hideThinkingOverlay());

 this.listenersBound = true;

// 主入口和状态管理
showGachaSystem() {
    this.openModal('gacha-modal');

    // --- 核心修复：为所有Gacha标签页绑定点击事件 ---
    const tabs = document.querySelectorAll('#gacha-modal .gacha-tab');
    tabs.forEach(tab => {
        tab.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const tabName = tab.dataset.tab;
            this.switchGachaTab(tabName);
        });
    });
    // --- 修复结束 ---

    this.switchGachaTab('summon'); // 默认显示召唤页
},

    async loadGachaState() {
    // 新增：定义一个包含所有默认值的“模板”
    const defaultGachaState = {
        astralDust: 0,
        starglitter: 0,
        pitySSR: 0,
        pitySR: 0,
        ssrGuarantee: false,
        redeemedCodes: [], // 新增：用于存储已兑换过的一次性兑换码
        activeCompanions: [], // 新增：用于追踪在世界中的伙伴
    };

    const savedState = await AppStorage.loadData('gacha_state', defaultGachaState);
    const savedCollection = await AppStorage.loadData('gacha_collection', {});
    const savedHistory = await AppStorage.loadData('gacha_history', []);

    // 核心修复：使用Object.assign将加载的数据覆盖到默认模板上
    // 这能确保即使加载的数据缺少新属性（如starglitter），也会使用默认值
    this.gachaState = Object.assign({}, defaultGachaState, savedState);
    this.gachaCollection = savedCollection;
    this.gachaHistory = savedHistory;

    // 新增：确保旧数据也能兼容新系统
    if (!this.gachaState.redeemedCodes) {
        this.gachaState.redeemedCodes = [];
    }
    if (!this.gachaState.activeCompanions) {
        this.gachaState.activeCompanions = [];
    }

    this.loadCharacterPoolFromLorebook();
},

async saveGachaState() {
    try {
        await AppStorage.saveData('gacha_state', this.gachaState);
        await AppStorage.saveData('gacha_collection', this.gachaCollection);
        await AppStorage.saveData('gacha_history', this.gachaHistory);
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('[Gacha Error] Failed to save Gacha state:', error);
        this.showTemporaryMessage('错误：无法保存星界之门数据！');
    }
},

// 标签页切换逻辑
switchGachaTab(tabName) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.gacha-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
    document.querySelector(`.gacha-tab[data-tab='${tabName}']`)?.classList.add('active');
    document.querySelectorAll('.gacha-tab-content').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('active'));
    const activeContent = document.getElementById(`gacha-tab-${tabName}`);
    if (activeContent) {
        activeContent.classList.add('active');
        // 根据标签页渲染不同内容
        if (tabName === 'summon') this.renderSummonTab();
        if (tabName === 'decomposition') this.renderDecompositionTab();
        if (tabName === 'gallery') this.renderGalleryTab();
        if (tabName === 'shop') this.renderShopTab(); // 新增：调用兑换码界面的渲染函数
    }
},

// 召唤标签页
// 召唤标签页
renderSummonTab() {
    const container = document.getElementById('gacha-tab-summon');
    if (!container) return;

    const companions = this.gachaState.activeCompanions || [];
    let companionsHtml = '';
    if (companions.length > 0) {
        companionsHtml = companions.map(c => {
            const rarityClass = `history-result-item rarity-${c.rarity.toUpperCase()}`;
            return `<span class="${rarityClass}" style="cursor:default;">${c.name}</span>`;
        }).join('');
    } else {
        companionsHtml = '<p style="font-style:italic; margin:0;">当前没有来自星界的伙伴。</p>';
    }
    const ssrCount = companions.filter(c => c.rarity === 'SSR').length;

    // --- 核心修改：将 gacha-currency 移到 summon-container 外部，并为 summon-container 添加 flex-grow: 1 ---
    container.innerHTML = `
        <div class="gacha-currency" style="text-align: center; margin-bottom: 15px; flex-shrink: 0;">星界之尘: <strong>${this.gachaState.astralDust}</strong> | 星辉: <strong>${this.gachaState.starglitter}</strong></div>
        <div class="summon-container" style="flex-grow: 1;">
            <div class="summon-buttons">
                <button id="btn-gacha-pull-1" class="interaction-btn">召唤1次 (160尘)</button>
                <button id="btn-gacha-pull-10" class="interaction-btn primary-btn">召唤10次 (1600尘)</button>
            </div>
            <div style="color:#F5DEB3; font-size:12px; text-align:center;">
                <p>SSR保底: ${this.gachaState.pitySSR}/90 | SR保底: ${this.gachaState.pitySR}/10</p>
                <p>大保底状态: ${this.gachaState.ssrGuarantee ? '<span style="color:#ff6b6b;">开启</span>' : '关闭'}</p>
            </div>
            <button id="btn-gacha-history" class="interaction-btn btn-secondary" style="padding: 6px 12px; font-size: 12px;">召唤记录</button>
            <div class="companion-display-container" style="margin-top:20px; padding:10px; background:rgba(0,0,0,0.3); border-radius:4px; width:80%; text-align:center;">
                <p style="font-size:12px; color:F5DEB3; margin-bottom:8px;">当前伙伴 (${companions.length}/3) (SSR: ${ssrCount}/1)</p>
                <div class="history-results" style="justify-content:center;">${companionsHtml}</div>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;

    document.getElementById('btn-gacha-pull-1').addEventListener('click', () => this.handlePull(1));
    document.getElementById('btn-gacha-pull-10').addEventListener('click', () => this.handlePull(10));
    document.getElementById('btn-gacha-history').addEventListener('click', () => this.showGachaHistory());
},

// 分解标签页


// 图鉴标签页


// 抽卡核心逻辑
handlePull(count) {
    // --- 新增修复：在抽卡前检查总卡池是否为空 ---
    const totalChars = (this.gachaCharacterPool.ssr?.length || 0) + (this.gachaCharacterPool.sr?.length || 0) + (this.gachaCharacterPool.r?.length || 0);
    if (totalChars === 0) {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('错误：角色卡池为空！请检查世界书“[星界角色卡]”条目是否正确配置并已禁用。', 5000);
        return;
    }
    // --- 新增修复结束 ---

    const cost = count * 160;
    if (this.gachaState.astralDust < cost) {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('星界之尘不足！');
        return;
    }
    this.gachaState.astralDust -= cost;
    const results = [];
    let gotSR_or_above = false;
    for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
        const result = this.getGachaRoll();
        results.push(result);
        if (result.rarity === 'SR' || result.rarity === 'SSR') gotSR_or_above = true;
    }
    // 10连保底SR
    if (count === 10 && !gotSR_or_above) {
        results[Math.floor(Math.random() * 10)] = this.getRandomItemFromPool(['sr']);
    }
    this.processPullResults(results);
    this.saveGachaState();
    this.renderSummonTab(); // 刷新UI
},

getGachaRoll() {
    // 【新增】检查首抽SR保底
    if (this.gachaState.firstPullGuaranteedSR === true) {
        this.gachaState.firstPullGuaranteedSR = false; // 使用掉保底机会
        this.saveGachaState(); // 立即保存状态，防止刷新丢失
        return this.getSRItem(); // 直接返回一个SR角色
    }

    this.gachaState.pitySR++;
    this.gachaState.pitySSR++;
    // 硬保底
    if (this.gachaState.pitySSR >= 90) return this.getSSRItem();
    if (this.gachaState.pitySR >= 10) return this.getSRItem();
    // 概率抽卡
    const rand = Math.random();
    let softPityRate = 0;
    if (this.gachaState.pitySSR >= 74) {
        softPityRate = (this.gachaState.pitySSR - 73) * 0.06; // 软保底
    }
    if (rand < 0.006 + softPityRate) return this.getSSRItem();
    if (rand < 0.006 + softPityRate + 0.051) return this.getSRItem();
    return this.getRandomItemFromPool(['r']);
},

getSSRItem() {
    this.gachaState.pitySSR = 0;
    this.gachaState.pitySR = 0;
    // 此处简化处理大保底，未来可加入UP池逻辑
    this.gachaState.ssrGuarantee = false;
    return this.getRandomItemFromPool(['ssr']);
},

getSRItem() {
    this.gachaState.pitySR = 0;
    return this.getRandomItemFromPool(['sr']);
},

getRandomItemFromPool(rarities) {
    const pool = rarities.flatMap(r => this.gachaCharacterPool[r.toLowerCase()] || []);
    if (pool.length === 0) {
        // 关键修复：如果指定稀有度的卡池为空，返回一个默认的“虚空”卡片，防止程序崩溃。
        // 您可以自定义这张“保底”卡片的名称和图片。
        console.error(`[Gacha System] 警告: 尝试从空的卡池 (${rarities.join(', ')}) 中抽卡。`);
        return { id: 'fallback_card', name: '虚空的低语', series: '未知', rarity: 'R', image: '' };
    }
    return pool[Math.floor(Math.random() * pool.length)];
},

// 抽卡后处理
processPullResults(results) {
    let newCommands = '';

    // 关键修复：始终在渲染前打开模态框，防止内容渲染失败
    // 新增：第二个参数 true，保留下方的抽卡主界面不被关闭
    this.openModal('gacha-results-modal', true);

    const gridContainer = document.getElementById('gacha-results-grid');
    if (!gridContainer) {
        console.error('[Gacha Error] 召唤结果容器 gacha-results-grid 未找到！');
        this.closeAllModals();
        return;
    }
    gridContainer.innerHTML = '';

    // 新增：根据抽卡数量为容器添加不同的样式类，以触发不同布局
    if (results.length === 1) {
        gridContainer.className = 'gacha-results-grid single-pull';
    } else {
        gridContainer.className = 'gacha-results-grid';
    }

    results.forEach((res, index) => {
        const isDuplicate = !!this.gachaCollection[res.id];
        if (!isDuplicate) {
            this.gachaCollection[res.id] = { acquired: new Date().toISOString() };
            if (res.rarity === 'SSR' && res.resource) {
                this.showTemporaryMessage(`获得了特殊物品: ${res.resource.name}!`, 4000);
                const categoryMap = { '武器': '武器列表', '饰品': '饰品列表', '衣物': '衣物列表', '封印物': '封印物列表' };
                const targetCategory = categoryMap[res.resource.type] || '杂物列表';
                const resourceName = res.resource.name || '未知物品';
                const resourceJson = JSON.stringify(res.resource).replace(/'/g, "\\'");
                newCommands += `assign('${targetCategory}', '${resourceName}', '${resourceJson}'); `;
            }
        } else {
            const dustReward = res.rarity === 'SSR' ? 80 : res.rarity === 'SR' ? 20 : 5;
            const glitterReward = res.rarity === 'SSR' ? 10 : res.rarity === 'SR' ? 2 : 0;
            this.gachaState.astralDust += dustReward;
            if(glitterReward > 0) this.gachaState.starglitter += glitterReward;
            let rewardText = `${res.name} 已转化为 ${dustReward} 星界之尘`;
            if (glitterReward > 0) rewardText += ` 和 ${glitterReward} 星辉`;
            this.showTemporaryMessage(rewardText);
        }

        const card = document.createElement('div');
        // 修正：确保稀有度总是大写，以匹配CSS类名
        card.className = `gacha-results-card rarity-${res.rarity.toUpperCase()}`;
        if (res.image) {
            card.style.backgroundImage = `url('${res.image}')`;
        }

        // 新增：为新获得的角色添加 "NEW" 标签
        if (!isDuplicate) {
            const newTag = document.createElement('div');
            newTag.className = 'gacha-results-new-tag';
            newTag.textContent = 'NEW';
            card.appendChild(newTag);
        }

        const infoContainer = document.createElement('div');
        infoContainer.className = 'gacha-results-card-info';
        const nameElement = document.createElement('div');
        nameElement.className = 'item-name';
        nameElement.textContent = res.name || '未知角色';
        infoContainer.appendChild(nameElement);
        const rarityElement = document.createElement('div');
        rarityElement.className = 'item-rarity';
        rarityElement.textContent = res.rarity || 'N/A';
        infoContainer.appendChild(rarityElement);
        if (isDuplicate) {
            const duplicateTag = document.createElement('div');
            duplicateTag.className = 'gacha-results-duplicate-tag';
            duplicateTag.textContent = '重复';
            infoContainer.appendChild(duplicateTag);
        }
        card.appendChild(infoContainer);
        gridContainer.appendChild(card);
    });

    if (newCommands) {
        this._applyLocalUpdate(newCommands);
    }

    this.gachaHistory.unshift({ timestamp: new Date().toISOString(), results });
    if (this.gachaHistory.length > 200) this.gachaHistory.pop();
    this.saveGachaState();
},

// 新增：渲染兑换码界面的函数
renderShopTab() {
    const container = document.getElementById('gacha-tab-shop');
    if (!container) return;

    container.innerHTML = `
        <div class="shop-container" style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; align-items: center; justify-content: center; height: 100%; gap: 25px; padding: 20px; text-align: center;">
            <div class="section-title" style="margin-bottom: 0;">神秘赠礼</div>
            <p style="color: #a09c91; font-size: 13px; max-width: 400px;">在此输入神秘的咒文以换取星界的馈赠。某些咒文或许低语着神的名字，蕴含着无限的力量。</p>
            <div style="display: flex; gap: 10px; align-items: center;">
                <input type="text" id="redeem-code-input" placeholder="输入兑换码" class="quick-send-input" style="width: 300px; height: 40px; text-align: center; font-size: 14px;">
                <button id="btn-redeem-code" class="interaction-btn primary-btn" style="padding: 10px 20px;">兑换</button>
            </div>
            <div style="color:#a09c91; font-size:12px;">当前星界之尘: <strong>${this.gachaState.astralDust}</strong> | 当前星辉: <strong>${this.gachaState.starglitter}</strong></div>
        </div>
    `;

    document.getElementById('btn-redeem-code').addEventListener('click', () => this.handleRedeemCode());
    document.getElementById('redeem-code-input').addEventListener('keypress', (e) => {
        if (e.key === 'Enter') {
            document.getElementById('btn-redeem-code').click();
        }
    });
},

// 新增：处理兑换码的核心逻辑函数
handleRedeemCode() {
    const input = document.getElementById('redeem-code-input');
    if (!input) return;
    const code = input.value.trim();

    if (!code) {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('请输入兑换码。');
        return;
    }

    const codeDB = {
    'qiwu1314': { reward: 300, type: 'dust', repeatable: false },
    'yemuccb': { reward: 300, type: 'dust', repeatable: false },
    'mengxing666': { reward: 300, type: 'dust', repeatable: false },
    '起物大人是执掌纯爱的神': { reward: 9999, type: 'dust', repeatable: true },
    '阿蒙修复补偿': { reward: 300, type: 'dust', repeatable: false, expires: '2025-08-30' } ,
    '诡秘剧场': { reward: 1600, type: 'dust', repeatable: false },
    '人为财死': { reward: 1600, type: 'dust', repeatable: false },
    '大航海时代': { reward: 1600, type: 'dust', repeatable: false },
    '契灵庆典': { reward: 1600, type: 'dust', repeatable: false },
    '鎏金鸾尾沙龙': { reward: 1600, type: 'dust', repeatable: false },
    '宿命之环': { reward: 1600, type: 'dust', repeatable: false },
    '逐光者': { reward: 1600, type: 'dust', repeatable: false },
};

    const entry = codeDB[code];

    if (!entry) {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('无效的兑换码。');
        input.value = '';
        return;
    }

  // --- 新增：检查兑换码是否已过期 ---
if (entry.expires) {
    const today = new Date();
    today.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0); // 将今天的时间设置为当天的零点，以便精确比较
    const expiryDate = new Date(entry.expires);

    if (today >= expiryDate) {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('抱歉，该兑换码已过期。');
        input.value = '';
        return;
    }
}
// --- 检查逻辑结束 ---  // 检查是否为一次性且已兑换
    if (!entry.repeatable && this.gachaState.redeemedCodes.includes(code)) {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('您已经兑换过这个礼包了。');
        input.value = '';
        return;
    }

    // 执行兑换
    if (entry.type === 'dust') {
        this.gachaState.astralDust += entry.reward;
    }
    // 未来可以扩展其他奖励类型，如星辉
    // else if (entry.type === 'glitter') { ... }

    if (!entry.repeatable) {
        this.gachaState.redeemedCodes.push(code);
    }

    this.saveGachaState();
    this.showTemporaryMessage(`兑换成功！获得 ${entry.reward} 星界之尘！`, 3000);
    input.value = '';

    // 刷新UI以显示新的货币数量
    this.renderShopTab();
},

// 抽卡记录
showGachaHistory(page = 1) {
    this.openModal('gacha-history-modal', true);
    const listEl = document.getElementById('history-list');
    const indicatorEl = document.getElementById('history-page-indicator');
    let prevBtn = document.getElementById('history-prev-btn');
    let nextBtn = document.getElementById('history-next-btn');
    const itemsPerPage = 5;
    const totalPages = Math.ceil(this.gachaHistory.length / itemsPerPage);
    const start = (page - 1) * itemsPerPage;
    const end = start + itemsPerPage;
    const pageItems = this.gachaHistory.slice(start, end);

    let html = pageItems.length > 0 ? '' : '<p style="color:#a09c91;text-align:center;">暂无记录</p>';
    pageItems.forEach(item => {
        let resultsHtml = '';
        item.results.forEach(res => {
            resultsHtml += `<span class="history-result-item rarity-${res.rarity.toUpperCase()}">${res.name}</span>`;
        });
        html += `
            <div class="history-item">
                <div class="history-timestamp">${new Date(item.timestamp).toLocaleString()}</div>
                <div class="history-results">${resultsHtml}</div>
            </div>
        `;
    });
    listEl.innerHTML = html;
    indicatorEl.textContent = `第 ${page} / ${totalPages || 1} 页`;

    // --- 核心修复：通过克隆节点的方式，彻底清除旧的事件监听器 ---
    const newPrevBtn = prevBtn.cloneNode(true);
    prevBtn.parentNode.replaceChild(newPrevBtn, prevBtn);
    prevBtn = newPrevBtn; // 更新按钮引用

    const newNextBtn = nextBtn.cloneNode(true);
    nextBtn.parentNode.replaceChild(newNextBtn, nextBtn);
    nextBtn = newNextBtn; // 更新按钮引用

    // 在新的、干净的按钮上设置状态和事件
    prevBtn.disabled = page <= 1;
    nextBtn.disabled = page >= totalPages;

    if (!prevBtn.disabled) {
        prevBtn.onclick = () => this.showGachaHistory(page - 1);
    }
    if (!nextBtn.disabled) {
        nextBtn.onclick = () => this.showGachaHistory(page + 1);
    }
},

     /// --- 核心修改：分解系统辅助函数实装 ---
_getDecomposableItems() {
    const allItems = [];
    if (!this.currentMvuState || !this.currentMvuState.stat_data) return [];
    const stat_data = this.currentMvuState.stat_data;

    const itemCategories = ['武器列表', '衣物列表', '饰品列表', '封印物列表', '消耗品列表', '杂物列表', '其他列表', '非凡材料列表'];

    itemCategories.forEach(categoryKey => {
        const itemsObj = this.SafeGetValue(stat_data, categoryKey, {});
        Object.values(itemsObj).forEach(item => {
            if (item && typeof item === 'object' && (item.名称 || item.name)) {
                // 简单拷贝并添加来源，避免修改原始数据
                const itemCopy = { ...item };
                itemCopy.sourceCategory = categoryKey;
                allItems.push(itemCopy);
            }
        });
    });

    return allItems;
},

calculateItemValue(item) {
    const tier = this.SafeGetValue(item, ['品阶', 'tier', '序列'], '普通');
    const valueMap = {
        '序列9': 5, '普通': 5,
        '序列8': 10,
        '序列7': 20, '非凡': 20,
        '序列6': 40,
        '序列5': 80, '罕见': 80,
        '序列4': 150, '史诗': 150,
        '序列3': 300, '传说': 300,
        '序列2': 600, '神话': 600,
        '序列1': 1200, '唯一': 1200,
        '序列0': 2500
    };
    const baseValue = valueMap[tier] || 5;
    const quantity = parseInt(this.SafeGetValue(item, ['数量', 'quantity'], 1), 10);
    return baseValue * quantity;
},




// 1. 同步点数（currentMvuState ↔ theaterState，兼容现有渲染）
syncTheaterPoints() {
  // 确保 currentMvuState 和 stat_data 存在
  this.currentMvuState = this.currentMvuState || { stat_data: {} };
  this.currentMvuState.stat_data = this.currentMvuState.stat_data || {};
  // 🔴 核心：用中文键名“剧场点数”，若不存在则自动初始化（兼容旧数据）
  if (this.currentMvuState.stat_data["剧场点数"] === undefined) {
    this.currentMvuState.stat_data["剧场点数"] = 0; // 初始化
  }

  // 同步到theaterState（供渲染用，保持原有字段名兼容渲染函数）
  this.theaterState = this.theaterState || {};
  this.theaterState.theaterPoints = this.currentMvuState.stat_data["剧场点数"];
},

switchTheaterTab(tabName) {

try {

  // 1. 切换标签按钮的激活状态
  document.querySelectorAll('.theater-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
  const targetTab = document.querySelector(`.theater-tab[data-tab='${tabName}']`);
  if (targetTab) targetTab.classList.add('active'); // 容错：防止标签不存在

  // 2. 切换模态框背景图
  const modal = document.querySelector('.theater-modal-custom');
  if (modal) {
    if (tabName === 'arena') {
      //modal.style.backgroundImage = 'url(https://i.postimg.cc/2S6g9Q6J/6.png)'; // 替换为角斗场背景图URL
      modal.setAttribute('style', `background-image: url(https://i.postimg.cc/7L5j8pzG/6.png) !important; background-size: cover; background-position: center;`);
      //modalContent.style.backgroundSize = 'cover';
      //modalContent.style.backgroundPosition = 'center';
    } else {
      //modal.style.backgroundImage = 'url(https://i.postimg.cc/76BNrNdx/ju-chang2.png)'; // 剧场背景图
      modal.setAttribute('style', `background-image: url(https://i.postimg.cc/76BNrNdx/ju-chang2.png) !important; background-size: cover; background-position: center;`);
      //modalContent.style.backgroundSize = 'cover';
      //modalContent.style.backgroundPosition = 'center';
    }
  }

  // 3. 清空所有标签页的旧内容（彻底删除DOM，避免残留）
  document.querySelectorAll('.theater-tab-content').forEach(content => {
    content.innerHTML = ''; // 关键：删除内部所有元素（包括“为何走下台”容器）
    content.classList.remove('active');
    content.style.display = 'none'; // 双重保险：强制隐藏
  });

  // 4. 渲染当前标签的新内容
  const activeContent = document.getElementById(`theater-tab-${tabName}`);
  if (activeContent) {
    activeContent.classList.add('active');
    activeContent.style.display = 'flex'; // 强制显示当前内容

    // 重新渲染对应标签页的内容
    if (tabName === 'theater' && activeContent.innerHTML === '') this.renderTheaterTab();
    if (tabName === 'arena' && activeContent.innerHTML === '') this.renderArenaTab();
    if (tabName === 'points' && activeContent.innerHTML === '') this.renderPointsTab();
  } else {
    console.error(`标签页内容未找到：theater-tab-${tabName}`);
  }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('switchTheaterTab报错：', error);
    // 报错后仍尝试显示标签页，避免完全无法切换
    const activeContent = document.getElementById(`theater-tab-${tabName}`);
    if (activeContent) {
      activeContent.classList.add('active');
      activeContent.style.display = 'flex';
    }
  }
},

// 3. 渲染剧场模态框（默认显示原剧场界面）
renderTheaterModal() {
  const existingModal = document.getElementById('theater-modal');
  if (existingModal) existingModal.remove();

  this.syncTheaterPoints();

  const modal = document.createElement('div');
  modal.id = 'theater-modal';
  modal.className = 'modal-overlay';
  modal.style.cssText = 'display: flex; z-index: 1002;';

  modal.innerHTML = `
    <div class="modal-content theater-modal-custom">
      <div class="modal-header">
        <h2 class="modal-title">你无意中发现了世界的真相……</h2>
        <button class="modal-close-btn">&times;</button>
      </div>
      <!-- 标签页（默认选中“剧场”） -->
      <div class="theater-tabs">
        <div class="theater-tab active" data-tab="theater">剧场</div>
        <div class="theater-tab" data-tab="arena">角斗场</div>
        <div class="theater-tab" data-tab="points">点数详情</div>
      </div>
      <!-- 标签页内容区域 -->
      <div class="modal-body theater-body-custom">
        <div id="theater-tab-theater" class="theater-tab-content active"></div>
        <div id="theater-tab-arena" class="theater-tab-content"></div>
        <div id="theater-tab-points" class="theater-tab-content"></div>
      </div>
    </div>
  `;

  document.querySelector('.guixu-root-container').appendChild(modal);
  this.bindTheaterModalEvents(modal);
  this.switchTheaterTab('theater'); // 强制默认显示原剧场界面
},


// 新增：渲染点数详情标签页
renderPointsTab() {
  const container = document.getElementById('theater-tab-points');
  if (!container) return;

  this.syncTheaterPoints();

  container.innerHTML = `
    <div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; align-items: center; gap: 20px; padding: 20px; width: 100%;">
      <div class="theater-currency" style="text-align: center; margin-bottom: 15px; color: #f5deb3; font-size: 16px;">
        剧场点数: <strong>${this.theaterState.theaterPoints}</strong>
      </div>
    </div>
  `;
},


// 4. 渲染原剧场界面（完全保留原有布局和功能）
renderTheaterTab() {
  const container = document.getElementById('theater-tab-theater');
  if (!container) return;

  this.syncTheaterPoints();

  container.innerHTML = `
    <div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; align-items: center; gap: 8px; margin-top: auto; width: 100%;">
      <p style="color: #f5deb3; text-align: center;">为何走下台？</p>
      <div style="width: 100%; overflow-x: auto; padding: 0; margin: 0; -webkit-overflow-scrolling: touch; white-space: nowrap; box-sizing: border-box;">
        <div style="display: flex; flex-direction: row; gap: 12px;">
          <button id="btn-find-staff" class="interaction-btn primary-btn theater-btn-custom" style="flex: 0 0 auto; min-width: 110px;">寻找幕后人员 (80点)</button>
          <button id="btn-find-ticket-seller" class="interaction-btn primary-btn theater-btn-custom" style="flex: 0 0 auto; min-width: 110px;">寻找售票人员 (50点)</button>
          <button id="btn-find-event-staff" class="interaction-btn primary-btn theater-btn-custom" style="flex: 0 0 auto; min-width: 140px;">当前剧场活动详情</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  `;

  // 绑定原剧场的所有按钮事件（新增扣点逻辑）
  const findStaffBtn = container.querySelector('#btn-find-staff');
  const findTicketSellerBtn = container.querySelector('#btn-find-ticket-seller');
  const findEventStaffBtn = container.querySelector('#btn-find-event-staff');

  findStaffBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
    if (this.isBusy) {
      this.showTemporaryMessage('正在处理上一条指令，请稍候...');
      return;
    }
    if (this.theaterState.theaterPoints < 80) {
      this.showTemporaryMessage('剧场点数不足80点，无法寻找幕后人员！');
      return;
    }
    const prePoints = this.theaterState.theaterPoints;
    try {
      // 更新 currentMvuState.stat_data（会被快照保存），同步 theaterState
      this.currentMvuState.stat_data["剧场点数"] = prePoints - 80;
      this.syncTheaterPoints();

      await this.handleAction('寻找幕后工作人员', false);
      this.showTemporaryMessage('消耗80点，正在寻找幕后人员...');
      this.renderPointsTab(); // 刷新显示
    } catch (error) {
      // 失败回滚：恢复 currentMvuState 和 theaterState
      this.currentMvuState.stat_data["剧场点数"] = prePoints;
      this.theaterState.theaterPoints = prePoints;
      this.showTemporaryMessage('操作失败，点数已回滚！');
    }
  });

  findTicketSellerBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
    if (this.isBusy) {
      this.showTemporaryMessage('正在处理上一条指令，请稍候...');
      return;
    }
    if (this.theaterState.theaterPoints < 50) {
      this.showTemporaryMessage('剧场点数不足50点，无法寻找售票人员！');
      return;
    }
     const prePoints = this.theaterState.theaterPoints;
    try {
      // 🔴 同步更新 currentMvuState 和 theaterState
      this.currentMvuState.stat_data["剧场点数"] = prePoints - 50;
      this.syncTheaterPoints();

      await this.handleAction('寻找售票工作人员', false);
      this.showTemporaryMessage('消耗50点，正在寻找售票人员...');
      this.renderPointsTab(); // 刷新显示
    } catch (error) {
      this.currentMvuState.stat_data["剧场点数"] = prePoints;
      this.theaterState.theaterPoints = prePoints;
      this.showTemporaryMessage('操作失败，点数已回滚！');
    }
  });

  findEventStaffBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
    if (this.isBusy) {
      this.showTemporaryMessage('正在处理上一条指令，请稍候...');
      return;
    }
    await this.handleAction('寻找剧场活动工作人员', false);
    this.showTemporaryMessage('正在查询剧场活动详情...');
  });
},
