},

// 6. 绑定模态框基础事件（标签页切换+关闭）
bindTheaterModalEvents(modal) {
  const closeBtn = modal.querySelector('.modal-close-btn');
  const tabs = modal.querySelectorAll('.theater-tab');

  // 关闭模态框
  closeBtn.addEventListener('click', () => modal.remove());

  // 标签页切换事件
  tabs.forEach(tab => {
    tab.addEventListener('click', () => {
      const tabName = tab.dataset.tab;
      this.switchTheaterTab(tabName);
    });
  });
},













      // --- 新增：本地状态更新辅助函数 ---
async _applyLocalUpdate(commandString) {
    if (!this.currentMvuState) return;
    try {
        const newState = await this._applyUpdateFallback(`_.${commandString}`, this.currentMvuState);
        if (newState) {
            this.currentMvuState = newState;
            // 将更新后的状态静默保存回SillyTavern
            const messages = await getChatMessages('0');
            if (messages && messages.length > 0) {
                const messageZero = messages[0];
                messageZero.data = this.currentMvuState;
                await TavernHelper.setChatMessages([messageZero], { refresh: 'none' });
                console.log('[源堡-本地更新] 已成功应用本地状态变更。');
            }
        }
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('应用本地更新时出错:', e);
    }
},

   // --- 新增：从存档记录中加载Gacha数据的通用函数 ---
_loadGachaDataFromSave(saveData) {
    if (saveData && saveData.gacha_data) {
        this.gachaState = saveData.gacha_data.state;
        this.gachaCollection = saveData.gacha_data.collection;
        this.gachaHistory = saveData.gacha_data.history;
        console.log('[Gacha] 已成功从存档文件加载Gacha数据。');
    } else {
        // 如果是旧存档或新游戏，则重置为初始状态
        this.gachaState = { astralDust: 160, starglitter: 0, pitySSR: 0, pitySR: 0, ssrGuarantee: false, redeemedCodes: [], activeCompanions: [], firstPullGuaranteedSR: true };
        this.gachaCollection = {};
        this.gachaHistory = [];
        console.log('[Gacha] 未在存档中找到Gacha数据，已重置为初始状态。');
    }
    // 确保任何情况下starglitter和新字段都有默认值，防止undefined
    if (this.gachaState.starglitter === undefined) {
        this.gachaState.starglitter = 0;
    }
    if (!this.gachaState.redeemedCodes) {
        this.gachaState.redeemedCodes = [];
    }
    if (!this.gachaState.activeCompanions) {
        this.gachaState.activeCompanions = [];
    }
    // 核心修复：将从存档加载的状态，立刻保存为当前的实时状态，以便刷新后能正确保留
    this.saveGachaState();
},  // --- 新增：个性化设置所需的全套函数 ---

// 字体控制
applyFont(fontClass) {
    const body = document.body;
    // 移除所有可能的旧字体类
    body.className = body.className.replace(/font-[\w-]+/g, '').trim();
    // 添加新字体类
    if (fontClass) {
        body.classList.add(fontClass);
    }
    this.currentFontClass = fontClass;
},
async saveFont(fontClass) {
    // 只存储有效字符串，防止意外存储非字符串类型
    if (typeof fontClass === 'string' && /^[\w-]+$/.test(fontClass)) {
        await AppStorage.saveData('custom_font_class', fontClass);
    } else {
        console.warn(`拒绝存储无效字体类名: ${fontClass}`);
        // 存储默认值，避免下次加载到非法数据
        await AppStorage.saveData('custom_font_class', 'font-noto-serif-sc');
    }
},
async loadFont() {
    // 从存储加载，强制转为字符串（防止存储了非字符串类型）
    const savedFont = await AppStorage.loadData('custom_font_class', 'font-noto-serif-sc');
    const fontClass = typeof savedFont === 'string' ? savedFont : 'font-noto-serif-sc';
    this.applyFont(fontClass); // 传入确保是字符串
},

// 背景控制
applyBackground(backgroundId) {
    const root = document.querySelector('.guixu-root-container');
    if (!root) return;

    if (backgroundId === 'default' || !backgroundId) {
        // 恢复默认的随机背景逻辑
        this.applyRandomBackground();
        this.currentBackgroundId = 'default';
        return;
    }

    const bgData = this.customBackgrounds.find(bg => bg.id === backgroundId);
    if (bgData) {
        const safeUrl = encodeURI(bgData.data);
        root.style.backgroundImage = `url('${safeUrl}')`;
        this.currentBackgroundId = backgroundId;
    } else {
        console.warn(`未找到ID为 ${backgroundId} 的背景图，将应用默认背景。`);
        this.applyRandomBackground();
        this.currentBackgroundId = 'default';
    }
},

async saveBackgrounds() {
    await AppStorage.saveData('custom_backgrounds', this.customBackgrounds);
    await AppStorage.saveData('current_background_id', this.currentBackgroundId);
},

async loadBackgrounds() {
  this.customBackgrounds = await AppStorage.loadData('custom_backgrounds', []);
  const savedId = await AppStorage.loadData('current_background_id', 'default');

  // 处理“无效ID”（空字符串、undefined、长度异常等）
  const isValidId = savedId === 'default' ||
                    (savedId && this.customBackgrounds.some(bg => bg.id === savedId));
  if (!isValidId) {
    await AppStorage.saveData('current_background_id', 'default'); // 重置为default
    this.applyRandomBackground(); // 直接随机
    return;
  }

  // 无自定义背景时，强制随机（不管savedId是什么）
  if (this.customBackgrounds.length === 0 && savedId !== 'default') {
    await AppStorage.saveData('current_background_id', 'default');
    this.applyRandomBackground();
    return;
  }

  // 原有逻辑：有效ID且有自定义背景→加载对应背景
  this.applyBackground(savedId);
},

handleBgImport(event) {
    const file = event.target.files[0];
    if (!file) return;
    if (file.size > 5 * 1024 * 1024) { // 限制5MB
        this.showTemporaryMessage('图片大小不能超过 5MB。');
        return;
    }

    this.showTemporaryMessage('正在导入图片...', 2000);
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = (e) => {
        const bgId = `bg_${Date.now()}`;
        const bgName = file.name;
        const bgData = e.target.result;

        this.customBackgrounds.push({ id: bgId, name: bgName, data: bgData });
        this.applyBackground(bgId);
        this.saveBackgrounds();
        this.showSettingsModal(); // 刷新设置面板以显示新图片
        this.showTemporaryMessage(`背景 “${bgName}” 导入成功！`);
    };
    reader.onerror = () => {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('图片读取失败！');
    };
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    event.target.value = ''; // 清空input，以便可以再次选择同一个文件
},

deleteCurrentBackground() {
    if (this.currentBackgroundId === 'default') {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('不能删除默认背景。');
        return;
    }

    const bgName = this.customBackgrounds.find(bg => bg.id === this.currentBackgroundId)?.name || '当前背景';

    this.showCustomConfirm(`确定要删除背景 “${bgName}” 吗？`, () => {
        this.customBackgrounds = this.customBackgrounds.filter(bg => bg.id !== this.currentBackgroundId);
        this.applyBackground('default'); // 恢复到默认
        this.saveBackgrounds();
        this.showSettingsModal(); // 刷新设置面板
        this.showTemporaryMessage('背景已删除。');
    });
},  // --- 新增：系统设置功能所需的全套函数 ---

    // --- 核心修复：将所有设置项整合到一个完整的HTML字符串中 ---

        <div class="panel-section appearance-section" style="padding: 10px; margin: 0;">

                        <button id="btn-import-bg" class="interaction-btn" style="padding: 6px 12px; font-size: 12px; display: block; width: 100px; margin-bottom: 5px;">导入图片</button>

                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="setting-item">
                <label class="setting-label">正文字体</label>
                <div class="setting-control">
                    <select id="font-select">${fontOptionsHtml}</select>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>


        <div class="panel-section" style="padding: 10px; margin: 0;">
            <div class="section-title">布局与尺寸</div>

                <label class="setting-label" for="fullscreen-layout-toggle">全屏布局 (占满窗口)</label>
                <div class="setting-control">
                    <label class="switch"><input type="checkbox" id="fullscreen-layout-toggle" ${this.isFullScreenLayout ? 'checked' : ''}><span class="slider"></span></label>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="setting-item">
                <label class="setting-label" for="width-slider">界面宽度</label>
                <div class="setting-control">
                    <input type="range" id="width-slider" class="font-slider" min="800" max="2500" step="10" value="${currentWidth}" ${this.isFullScreenLayout ? 'disabled' : ''}>
                    <input type="number" id="width-input" class="font-size-input" min="800" max="2500" value="${currentWidth}">
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="setting-item">
                <label class="setting-label" for="height-slider">界面高度</label>
                <div class="setting-control">
                    <input type="range" id="height-slider" class="font-slider" min="600" max="1200" step="10" value="${currentHeight}" ${this.isFullScreenLayout ? 'disabled' : ''}>
                    <input type="number" id="height-input" class="font-size-input" min="600" max="1200" value="${currentHeight}">
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>


        <div class="panel-section" style="padding: 10px; margin: 0;">
            <div class="section-title">功能设置</div>
            <div class="setting-item">
                <label class="setting-label" for="font-size-slider">正文字体大小</label>
                <div class="setting-control">
                    <input type="range" id="font-size-slider" class="font-slider" min="12" max="20" step="1" value="${this.fontSize}">
                    <input type="number" id="font-size-input" class="font-size-input" min="12" max="20" value="${this.fontSize}">

            <div class="setting-item">

                         <input type="checkbox" id="danmaku-style-toggle-checkbox" ${this.isDanmakuEntriesEnabled ? 'checked' : ''}><span class="slider"></span></label>

                <label class="setting-label" for="recent-events-input">记忆中枢-近期事件数量</label>

                    <label class="switch"><input type="checkbox" id="periodic-backup-toggle" ${this.isPeriodicBackupEnabled ? 'checked' : ''}><span class="slider"></span></label>

                <label class="setting-label" for="periodic-backup-interval">备份间隔（回合数）</label>
                <div class="setting-control">

                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="setting-item">
                <label class="setting-label">当前计数</label>
                <div class="setting-control">
                    <span id="periodic-backup-count" style="color: #a09c91;">${this.turnsSinceLastBackup} / ${this.periodicBackupInterval}</span>

    this.bindSettingsModalListeners();
    this.updateBgPreview(this.currentBackgroundId); // 新增：打开面板时，立即更新一次预览图
},

// 为设置面板内的控件绑定事件
    bindSettingsModalListeners() {
    const body = document.getElementById('settings-modal-body');
    // 【核心修复】重新添加“哨兵”检查，防止重复绑定
    if (!body || body.dataset.listenersBound) return;
    body.dataset.listenersBound = 'true';

    // --- 个性化设置事件绑定 (已更新) ---
    document.getElementById('btn-import-bg')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
        const input = document.createElement('input');
        input.type = 'file';
        input.accept = 'image/*';
        input.onchange = (e) => this.handleBgImport(e);
        input.click();
    });

    document.getElementById('background-select')?.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
        const selectedId = e.target.value;
        this.applyBackground(selectedId);
        this.saveBackgrounds();
        this.updateBgPreview(selectedId); // 新增：更新预览图
        const deleteBtn = document.getElementById('btn-delete-bg');
        if (deleteBtn) {
            deleteBtn.disabled = selectedId === 'default';
        }
    });

    document.getElementById('btn-delete-bg')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.deleteCurrentBackground());

    document.getElementById('font-select')?.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
    // 过滤选项值中的空格和非法字符（下拉框选项可能意外包含空格）
        const safeValue = e.target.value.replace(/\s+/g, ''); // 移除所有空格
        if (/^[\w-]+$/.test(safeValue)) { // 验证是否为有效类名
            this.applyFont(safeValue);
            this.saveFont(safeValue); // 传入净化后的值去存储
        } else {
            console.warn(`无效的字体选项值: ${e.target.value}，已忽略`);
        }
    });

    // --- 原有事件绑定保持不变 (复制粘贴即可) ---
    const fontSlider = document.getElementById('font-size-slider');
    const fontInput = document.getElementById('font-size-input');
    const updateFontSize = (size) => {
        const newSize = Math.max(12, Math.min(20, parseInt(size, 10)));
        if (isNaN(newSize)) return;
        this.applyFontSize(newSize);
        if (fontSlider) fontSlider.value = newSize;
        if (fontInput) fontInput.value = newSize;
    };
    if (fontSlider) {
        fontSlider.addEventListener('input', (e) => updateFontSize(e.target.value));
        fontSlider.addEventListener('change', () => this.saveFontSize());
    }
    if (fontInput) {
        fontInput.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            updateFontSize(e.target.value);
            this.saveFontSize();
        });
    }

    const widthSlider = document.getElementById('width-slider');
    const widthInput = document.getElementById('width-input');
    const heightSlider = document.getElementById('height-slider');
    const heightInput = document.getElementById('height-input');
    const fullscreenLayoutToggle = document.getElementById('fullscreen-layout-toggle');

    const updateWidth = (width) => {
        const newWidth = Math.max(800, Math.min(2500, parseInt(width, 10)));
        if(isNaN(newWidth)) return;
        this.widthSetting = `${newWidth}px`;
        if (widthSlider) widthSlider.value = newWidth;
        if (widthInput) widthInput.value = newWidth;
        this.applyDimensions();
    };
    const updateHeight = (height) => {
        const newHeight = Math.max(600, Math.min(1200, parseInt(height, 10)));
        if(isNaN(newHeight)) return;
        this.heightSetting = `${newHeight}px`;
        if (heightSlider) heightSlider.value = newHeight;
        if (heightInput) heightInput.value = newHeight;
        this.applyDimensions();
    };

    if (widthSlider) {
        widthSlider.addEventListener('input', (e) => updateWidth(e.target.value));
        widthSlider.addEventListener('change', () => this.saveDimensions());
    }
    if (widthInput) {
        widthInput.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            updateWidth(e.target.value);
            this.saveDimensions();
        });
    }
    if (heightSlider) {
        heightSlider.addEventListener('input', (e) => updateHeight(e.target.value));
        heightSlider.addEventListener('change', () => this.saveDimensions());
    }
    if (heightInput) {
        heightInput.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            updateHeight(e.target.value);
            this.saveDimensions();
        });
    }
    if (fullscreenLayoutToggle) {
        fullscreenLayoutToggle.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            this.isFullScreenLayout = e.target.checked;
            this.applyDimensions();
            this.saveDimensions();
        });
    }

    const streamingCheckbox = document.getElementById('streaming-toggle-checkbox');
    const fullscreenLoadingCheckbox = document.getElementById('fullscreen-loading-toggle-checkbox');
    const fullscreenBtn = document.getElementById('btn-toggle-fullscreen');

    if (streamingCheckbox) {
        streamingCheckbox.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            this.isStreamingEnabled = e.target.checked;
            this.saveStreamingState();
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`流式传输已${this.isStreamingEnabled ? '开启' : '关闭'}`);
        });
    }
    if (fullscreenLoadingCheckbox) {
        fullscreenLoadingCheckbox.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            this.isFullScreenLoadingEnabled = e.target.checked;
            this.saveFullScreenLoadingState();
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`全屏加载动画已${this.isFullScreenLoadingEnabled ? '开启' : '关闭'}`);
        });
    }

    const floatingEditorCheckbox = document.getElementById('floating-editor-toggle-checkbox');
    if (floatingEditorCheckbox) {
        floatingEditorCheckbox.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            this.isFloatingEditorEnabled = e.target.checked;
            this.saveFloatingEditorState();
            // 控制悬浮编辑器按钮的显示/隐藏
            if (floatingEditorInstance) {
                floatingEditorInstance.setEnabled(this.isFloatingEditorEnabled);
            }
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`悬浮变量更新器已${this.isFloatingEditorEnabled ? '开启' : '关闭'}`);
        });
    }

// --- 定义目标世界书和条目，方便管理 ---
const WORLD_BOOK_NAME = '1源堡'; // 你的世界书名
const DANMAKU_CORE_ENTRIES = ['弹幕风格', '弹幕框架', '触发']; // 弹幕核心三件套
const FORMAT_ENTRY_NORMAL = '【系统】格式要求'; // 普通格式条目
const FORMAT_ENTRY_DANMAKU = '【系统】格式要求弹幕'; // 弹幕专用格式条目


// 获取 checkbox 元素
const danmakuStyleCheckbox = document.getElementById('danmaku-style-toggle-checkbox');

if (danmakuStyleCheckbox) {
    // 1. 初始化时，根据 isDanmakuEntriesEnabled 的值设置 checkbox 的初始状态
    // 注意：这里我们不再在初始化时发送指令去“双重保险”了。
    // 原因是 API 操作比 slash command 更直接，也可能更耗资源。
    // 我们相信持久化的 isDanmakuEntriesEnabled 状态是准确的。
    // 如果非要同步，可以在页面加载时执行一次关闭操作，但通常没必要。
    (async () => {
        await this.loadDanmakuState();
        danmakuStyleCheckbox.checked = this.isDanmakuEntriesEnabled;
    })();

        // 2. 在事件监听器里，根据 checkbox 的变化，调用 API 更新世界书条目
    danmakuStyleCheckbox.addEventListener('change', async (e) => {
        const isDanmakuEnabled = e.target.checked; // isEnabled 语义更明确一点，叫 isDanmakuEnabled
        this.isDanmakuEntriesEnabled = isDanmakuEnabled; // 更新并持久化状态
        await this.saveDanmakuState(); // 状态变化时保存到存储

        try {
            await updateWorldbookWith(WORLD_BOOK_NAME, (currentEntries) => {
                // updater 函数：接收当前所有条目，返回修改后的新条目数组
                return currentEntries.map(entry => {
                    // --- 核心逻辑在这里 ---

                    // 1. 判断是否为弹幕核心三件套
                    if (DANMAKU_CORE_ENTRIES.includes(entry.name)) {
                        // 是的话，其状态直接跟随开关 (isDanmakuEnabled)
                        return { ...entry, enabled: isDanmakuEnabled };
                    }

                    // 2. 判断是否为弹幕专用格式条目
                    if (entry.name === FORMAT_ENTRY_DANMAKU) {
                        // 是的话，其状态也跟随开关 (isDanmakuEnabled)
                        // 开弹幕，它就开；关弹幕，它就关。
                        return { ...entry, enabled: isDanmakuEnabled };
                    }

                    // 3. 判断是否为普通格式条目
                    if (entry.name === FORMAT_ENTRY_NORMAL) {
                        // 是的话，其状态与开关【相反】(!isDanmakuEnabled)
                        // 开弹幕，它就关；关弹幕，它就开。
                        return { ...entry, enabled: !isDanmakuEnabled };
                    }

                    // 4. 如果以上都不是，说明是无关条目，原样返回
                    return entry;
                });
            });

            // --- 操作成功后的用户反馈 ---
            const statusText = isDanmakuEnabled ? '开启' : '关闭';
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`弹幕模式已${statusText}，相关格式已自动切换。`);

        } catch (error) {
            // 异常处理部分保持不变
            console.error('更新世界书条目失败:', error);
            this.showTemporaryMessage('操作失败，请检查控制台错误信息。', 'error');

            // 操作失败，UI状态回滚
            this.isDanmakuEntriesEnabled = !isDanmakuEnabled;
            e.target.checked = !isDanmakuEnabled;
        }
    });
}



    if (fullscreenBtn) {
        fullscreenBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.toggleFullScreen());
    }
    const recentEventsInput = document.getElementById('recent-events-input');
    if (recentEventsInput) {
        recentEventsInput.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
            const count = parseInt(e.target.value, 10);
            if (!isNaN(count) && count >= 1 && count <= 20) {
                this.recentEventsCount = count;
                this.saveRecentEventsCount();
                this.showTemporaryMessage(`近期事件发送数量已设为 ${count} 条`);
            } else {
                e.target.value = this.recentEventsCount; // 如果输入无效则恢复原值
            }
        });
    }

    // --- 定期自动备份设置事件绑定 ---
    const periodicBackupToggle = document.getElementById('periodic-backup-toggle');
    const periodicBackupInterval = document.getElementById('periodic-backup-interval');

    if (periodicBackupToggle) {
        periodicBackupToggle.addEventListener('change', async (e) => {
            this.isPeriodicBackupEnabled = e.target.checked;
            await this.savePeriodicBackupSettings();
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`定期自动备份已${this.isPeriodicBackupEnabled ? '开启' : '关闭'}`);
            // 更新计数显示
            const countSpan = document.getElementById('periodic-backup-count');
            if (countSpan) {
                countSpan.textContent = `${this.turnsSinceLastBackup} / ${this.periodicBackupInterval}`;
            }
        });
    }

    if (periodicBackupInterval) {
        periodicBackupInterval.addEventListener('change', async (e) => {
            const interval = parseInt(e.target.value, 10);
            if (!isNaN(interval) && interval >= 1 && interval <= 100) {
                this.periodicBackupInterval = interval;
                await this.savePeriodicBackupSettings();
                this.showTemporaryMessage(`备份间隔已设为 ${interval} 回合`);
                // 更新计数显示
                const countSpan = document.getElementById('periodic-backup-count');
                if (countSpan) {
                    countSpan.textContent = `${this.turnsSinceLastBackup} / ${this.periodicBackupInterval}`;
                }
            } else {
                e.target.value = this.periodicBackupInterval; // 无效输入恢复原值
            }
        });
    }
},


// 应用字体大小到UI
applyFontSize(size) {
    const gameTextContainer = document.getElementById('game-text-display');
    if (gameTextContainer) {
        gameTextContainer.style.fontSize = `${size}px`;
    }
    this.fontSize = size;
},

// 保存字体大小设置
async saveFontSize() {
    await AppStorage.saveData('font_size', this.fontSize);
},

// 加载并应用字体大小设置
async loadFontSize() {
    const savedSize = await AppStorage.loadData('font_size', 14); // 默认14px
    this.applyFontSize(savedSize);
},

// --- 定期自动备份设置保存与加载 ---

// 保存定期备份设置到存储
async savePeriodicBackupSettings() {
    try {
        await AppStorage.saveData(PERIODIC_BACKUP_KEYS.ENABLED, this.isPeriodicBackupEnabled);
        await AppStorage.saveData(PERIODIC_BACKUP_KEYS.INTERVAL, this.periodicBackupInterval);
        await AppStorage.saveData(PERIODIC_BACKUP_KEYS.TURN_COUNT, this.turnsSinceLastBackup);
        console.log('[定期备份] 设置已保存');
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('[定期备份] 保存设置失败:', error);
    }
},

// 从存储加载定期备份设置
async loadPeriodicBackupSettings() {
    try {
        this.isPeriodicBackupEnabled = await AppStorage.loadData(PERIODIC_BACKUP_KEYS.ENABLED, false);
        this.periodicBackupInterval = await AppStorage.loadData(PERIODIC_BACKUP_KEYS.INTERVAL, 5);
        this.turnsSinceLastBackup = await AppStorage.loadData(PERIODIC_BACKUP_KEYS.TURN_COUNT, 0);
        console.log(`[定期备份] 设置已加载 - 启用:${this.isPeriodicBackupEnabled}, 间隔:${this.periodicBackupInterval}回合, 当前计数:${this.turnsSinceLastBackup}`);
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('[定期备份] 加载设置失败，使用默认值:', error);
        this.isPeriodicBackupEnabled = false;
        this.periodicBackupInterval = 5;
        this.turnsSinceLastBackup = 0;
    }
},

// 创建定期自动备份（使用独立存储槽位，不影响手动存档）
async createPeriodicBackup() {
    if (!this.currentMvuState) {
        console.warn('[定期备份] 游戏状态为空，跳过备份');
        return false;
    }

    try {
        // 获取当前消息内容
        let currentMessageContent = '';
        try {
            const messages = await getChatMessages('0');
            currentMessageContent = messages?.[0]?.message || '';
        } catch (e) {
            console.warn('[定期备份] 获取消息内容失败');
        }

        const cleanedMessageContent = currentMessageContent.replace(new RegExp('', 'g'), '');

        // 构建备份数据，复用现有存档数据结构
        const backupData = {
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            save_name: '已自动备份的存档',
            message_content: cleanedMessageContent,
            mvu_data: _.cloneDeep(this.currentMvuState),
            equipped_items: _.cloneDeep(this.equippedItems),
            pending_actions: _.cloneDeep(this.pendingActions) || [],
            gacha_data: {
                state: _.cloneDeep(this.gachaState),
                collection: _.cloneDeep(this.gachaCollection),
                history: _.cloneDeep(this.gachaHistory)
            },
            backup_turn: this.chatHistoryCache ? this.chatHistoryCache.length : 0
        };

        // 捕获世界书内容（本周目经历和核心记忆）
        try {
            const bookName = '1源堡';
            const index = this.unifiedIndex;
            const journeyKey = index > 1 ? `本周目经历(${index})` : '本周目经历';
            const coreMemoryKey = index > 1 ? `本周目核心记忆(${index})` : '本周目核心记忆';
            const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
            const journeyEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === journeyKey);
            const coreMemoryEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === coreMemoryKey);
            backupData.lorebook_content = {
                journey: journeyEntry ? journeyEntry.content : null,
                core_memory: coreMemoryEntry ? coreMemoryEntry.content : null
            };
        } catch (e) {
            console.error('[定期备份] 捕获世界书快照失败:', e);
            backupData.lorebook_content = { journey: null, core_memory: null };
        }

        // 写入独立存储槽位（先删后写，确保只有一份备份）
        await AppStorage.saveData(PERIODIC_BACKUP_KEYS.SLOT, backupData);

        console.log('[定期备份] 备份创建成功，回合:', backupData.backup_turn);
        return true;
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('[定期备份] 创建备份失败:', error);
        return false;
    }
},

// 检查并执行定期备份（在每回合结束时调用）
async checkAndPerformPeriodicBackup() {
    // 未启用则跳过
    if (!this.isPeriodicBackupEnabled) {
        return;
    }

    // 增加回合计数
    this.turnsSinceLastBackup++;

    // 检查是否达到备份间隔
    if (this.turnsSinceLastBackup >= this.periodicBackupInterval) {
        console.log(`[定期备份] 已达${this.periodicBackupInterval}回合，执行备份...`);

        const success = await this.createPeriodicBackup();
        if (success) {
            this.turnsSinceLastBackup = 0;
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`已自动备份（每${this.periodicBackupInterval}回合）`);
        }
    }

    // 保存当前回合计数
    await AppStorage.saveData(PERIODIC_BACKUP_KEYS.TURN_COUNT, this.turnsSinceLastBackup);
},

//加载定期备份存档
async loadPeriodicBackup() {
    try {
        const backupData = await AppStorage.loadData(PERIODIC_BACKUP_KEYS.SLOT, null);
        if (!backupData) {
            this.showTemporaryMessage('暂无自动备份可加载');
            return false;
        }

        this.showTemporaryMessage('正在恢复自动备份...');

        //计算需要回滚的步数
        const currentTurn = this.chatHistoryCache.length;
        const backupTurn = backupData.backup_turn || 0;
        const stepsToRollback = currentTurn - backupTurn;

        console.log(`[定期备份] 当前回合:${currentTurn}, 备份回合:${backupTurn}, 需回滚:${stepsToRollback}步`);

        if (stepsToRollback > 0 && stepsToRollback < currentTurn) {
            //截断历史记录到备份时的状态
            this.chatHistoryCache = this.chatHistoryCache.slice(0, backupTurn);
            await AppStorage.saveData(this._getHistoryKey(), this.chatHistoryCache);

            //回滚世界书经历
            await this._rollbackJourneyLog(stepsToRollback);
        }

        //恢复游戏状态数据
        this.currentMvuState = backupData.mvu_data;
        this.equippedItems = backupData.equipped_items || {};
        this.pendingActions = backupData.pending_actions || [];

        //恢复Gacha数据
        if (backupData.gacha_data) {
            this.gachaState = backupData.gacha_data.state;
            this.gachaCollection = backupData.gacha_data.collection;
            this.gachaHistory = backupData.gacha_data.history;
            this.saveGachaState();
        }

        //恢复世界书内容（本周目经历和核心记忆）
        if (backupData.lorebook_content) {
            try {
                const bookName = '1源堡';
                const index = this.unifiedIndex;
                const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);

                // 恢复本周目经历
                if (backupData.lorebook_content.journey) {
                    const journeyKey = index > 1 ? `本周目经历(${index})` : '本周目经历';
                    const journeyEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === journeyKey);
                    if (journeyEntry) {
                        await TavernHelper.setLorebookEntries(bookName, [{
                            uid: journeyEntry.uid,
                            content: backupData.lorebook_content.journey
                        }]);
                    }
                }

                // 恢复核心记忆
                if (backupData.lorebook_content.core_memory) {
                    const coreMemoryKey = index > 1 ? `本周目核心记忆(${index})` : '本周目核心记忆';
                    const coreMemoryEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === coreMemoryKey);
                    if (coreMemoryEntry) {
                        await TavernHelper.setLorebookEntries(bookName, [{
                            uid: coreMemoryEntry.uid,
                            content: backupData.lorebook_content.core_memory
                        }]);
                    }
                }
            } catch (e) {
                console.error('[定期备份] 恢复世界书内容失败:', e);
            }
        }

        //同步状态到酒馆消息
        const messages = await getChatMessages('0');
        if (messages && messages.length > 0) {
            const messageZero = messages[0];
            messageZero.message = backupData.message_content || '';
            messageZero.data = _.cloneDeep(this.currentMvuState);
            await TavernHelper.setChatMessages([messageZero], { refresh: 'all' });
        }

        //保存装备和待处理动作状态
        this.saveEquipmentState();
        this.savePendingActions();

        //刷新UI显示
        await this.returnToPresent();

        this.showTemporaryMessage(`已从自动备份恢复至第${backupTurn}回合`);
        console.log('[定期备份] 存档加载成功');
        return true;
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('[定期备份] 加载备份失败:', error);
        this.showTemporaryMessage('加载自动备份失败');
        return false;
    }
},

// 渲染定期备份章节（用于时光手记界面）
async renderPeriodicBackupChapter() {
    const backupData = await AppStorage.loadData(PERIODIC_BACKUP_KEYS.SLOT, null);

    if (!backupData) {
        return `
            <div class="chronicle-chapter periodic-backup-chapter" style="opacity: 0.6;">
                <div class="chapter-header">
                    <span class="chapter-icon">📦</span>
                    <span class="chapter-title">定期自动备份</span>
                </div>
                <div class="chapter-meta" style="padding: 10px; color: #a09c91; font-size: 12px;">
                    暂无自动备份
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
    }

    const timestamp = new Date(backupData.timestamp).toLocaleString('zh-CN');
    const turnInfo = backupData.backup_turn ? `第${backupData.backup_turn}回合` : '';

    return `
        <div class="chronicle-chapter periodic-backup-chapter">
            <div class="chapter-header">
                <span class="chapter-icon">📦</span>
                <span class="chapter-title">定期自动备份</span>
            </div>
            <div class="chapter-meta" style="padding: 10px;">
                <div style="color: #d2b48c; margin-bottom: 5px;">${backupData.save_name}</div>
                <div style="color: #a09c91; font-size: 11px;">${timestamp} ${turnInfo}</div>
                <button id="btn-load-periodic-backup" class="interaction-btn" style="margin-top: 10px; padding: 6px 15px; font-size: 12px;">加载此备份</button>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;
},

// 绑定定期备份加载按钮事件
bindPeriodicBackupListeners() {
    const loadBtn = document.getElementById('btn-load-periodic-backup');
    if (loadBtn) {
        loadBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
            this.showCustomConfirm(
                '确定要加载定期自动备份吗？当前未保存的进度将丢失。',
                async () => {
                    await this.loadPeriodicBackup();
                    this.closeModal('save-load-modal');
                }
            );
        });
    }
},

// 清理旧DOM的事件绑定（防止内存泄漏）
unbindSettingsModalListeners() {
    const body = document.getElementById('settings-modal-body');
    if (!body) return;

    // 1. 移除单个元素的事件（通过克隆元素实现快速解绑）
    const unbindElement = (selector) => {
        const el = body.querySelector(selector);
        if (el) {
            // 克隆元素会丢失所有事件绑定，替换原元素实现解绑
            const clone = el.cloneNode(true);
            el.parentNode.replaceChild(clone, el);
        }
    };

    // 2. 批量解绑所有设置项的元素（覆盖所有绑定过事件的控件）
    [
        '#background-select',
        '#font-select',
        '#btn-import-bg',
        '#btn-delete-bg',
        '#font-size-slider',
        '#font-size-input',
        '#width-slider',
        '#width-input',
        '#height-slider',
        '#height-input',
        '#fullscreen-layout-toggle',
        '#streaming-toggle-checkbox',
        '#fullscreen-loading-toggle-checkbox',
        '#danmaku-style-toggle-checkbox', // 弹幕风格开关
        '#floating-editor-toggle-checkbox', // 悬浮窗开关
        '#recent-events-input',
        '#btn-toggle-fullscreen',
        '#periodic-backup-toggle',    // 定期备份开关
        '#periodic-backup-interval'   // 定期备份间隔
    ].forEach(selector => unbindElement(selector));

    // 3. 重置绑定标记
    delete body.dataset.listenersBound;
},


  // --- 新增：世界书卡池加载与解析函数 (支持单条目多角色) ---
_parseLorebookCharacter(contentBlock) {
    const char = { tags: [] };
    const lines = contentBlock.split('\n');
    lines.forEach(line => {
        const parts = line.split(':');
        if (parts.length < 2) return;
        const key = parts[0].trim();
        const value = parts.slice(1).join(':').trim();
        switch (key) {
            case '名称': char.name = value; break;
            case '系列': char.series = value; break;
            case '图片': char.image = value; break;
            case '稀有度': char.rarity = value.toUpperCase(); break;
            case '初始序列': char.initialSequence = value; break; // <<< 新增此行
            case '适配序列': char.sequence = value; break;
            case '标签': char.tags = value.replace(/[\[\]]/g, '').split(',').map(t => t.trim()); break;
            case '初始资源':
                try { char.resource = JSON.parse(value); } catch(e) { console.error('解析初始资源JSON失败:', value, e); }
                break;
        }
    });
    if (char.name && char.rarity) return char;
    return null;
},

async loadCharacterPoolFromLorebook() {
    this.showTemporaryMessage('正在从世界书同步角色卡池...', 1500);
    const bookName = '1源堡'; // 已适配为您的主世界书
    const newPool = { ssr: [], sr: [], r: [] };
    try {
        const entries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
        if (!entries || entries.length === 0) {
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`警告：未找到或“${bookName}”世界书为空。`, 3000);
            return;
        }

        let count = 0;
        for (const entry of entries) {
            if (entry.comment.includes('[星界角色卡]') && entry.enabled === false) {
                // 核心修改：将整个条目内容按“名称:”分割成多个角色块
                const characterBlocks = entry.content.split(/\n*\s*名称:/).filter(block => block.trim() !== '');
                for (const block of characterBlocks) {
                    const fullBlock = '名称:' + block; // 把分割掉的“名称:”加回来
                    const char = this._parseLorebookCharacter(fullBlock);
                    if (char) {
                        char.id = `${char.series}_${char.name}`.replace(/\s/g, '_');
                        const rarityKey = char.rarity.toLowerCase();
                        if (newPool[rarityKey]) {
                            newPool[rarityKey].push(char);
                            count++;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        this.gachaCharacterPool = newPool;
        console.log(`[Gacha] 成功从世界书加载 ${count} 个角色。`);
        if (count === 0) {
            this.showTemporaryMessage('未在禁用的条目中找到任何格式正确的角色卡。', 4000);
        }
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('从世界书加载角色卡池失败:', e);
        this.showTemporaryMessage('错误：加载角色卡池失败，请检查世界书。', 3000);
    }
},

  // --- 新增：分解与图鉴功能所需的全套函数 ---

// 分解标签页的完整渲染与事件绑定
renderDecompositionTab() {
    const container = document.getElementById('gacha-tab-decomposition');
    const inventoryItems = this._getDecomposableItems();
    let inventoryHtml = inventoryItems.length > 0 ? '' : '<p style="color:#a09c91; text-align:center;">没有可分解的物品。</p>';

    const equippedItemNames = Object.values(this.equippedItems).filter(i => i).map(i => this.SafeGetValue(i, ['名称', 'name']));
    const filteredInventory = inventoryItems.filter(item => !equippedItemNames.includes(this.SafeGetValue(item, ['名称', 'name'])));

    filteredInventory.forEach(item => {
        const itemName = this.SafeGetValue(item, ['名称', 'name']);
        const itemTier = this.SafeGetValue(item, ['品阶', 'tier', '序列'], '普通');
        const itemValue = Math.floor(this.calculateItemValue(item) / (item.数量 || 1));
        inventoryHtml += `
            <div class="decom-inventory-item" data-item='${JSON.stringify(item)}'>
                <span class="decom-item-name" style="${this.getTierStyle(itemTier)}">${itemName} (x${item.数量 || 1})</span>
                <span class="decom-item-value">价值: ${itemValue} 尘/个</span>
            </div>
        `;
    });

    container.innerHTML = `
        <div class="decomposition-container">
            <div class="decom-inventory">
                <div class="section-title">选择物品进行分解</div>
                <div id="decom-inventory-list">${inventoryHtml}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="decom-altar">
                <div class="section-title">献祭槽</div>
                <div id="decom-altar-list"></div>
                <div id="decom-results">总价值: <strong>0</strong> 星界之尘</div>
                <button id="btn-decompose" class="interaction-btn" disabled>分解</button>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;

    const altarItems = new Map();
    const inventoryListEl = document.getElementById('decom-inventory-list');
    const altarListEl = document.getElementById('decom-altar-list');
    const resultsEl = document.getElementById('decom-results');
    const decomposeBtn = document.getElementById('btn-decompose');

    const renderAltar = () => {
        altarListEl.innerHTML = '';
        altarItems.forEach((item, name) => {
            const el = document.createElement('div');
            el.className = 'decom-altar-item';
            el.textContent = `${name} x${item.数量}`;
            el.dataset.itemName = name;
            altarListEl.appendChild(el);
        });
    };

    const updateTotalValue = () => {
        let totalValue = 0;
        altarItems.forEach(item => totalValue += this.calculateItemValue(item));
        resultsEl.innerHTML = `总价值: <strong>${totalValue}</strong> 星界之尘`;
        decomposeBtn.disabled = totalValue === 0;
    };

    // 核心修改1：点击物品列表时的逻辑
    inventoryListEl.addEventListener('click', e => {
        const itemEl = e.target.closest('.decom-inventory-item');
        if (!itemEl) return;

        const itemData = JSON.parse(itemEl.dataset.item);
        const itemName = this.SafeGetValue(itemData, ['名称', 'name']);
        const originalQuantity = parseInt(this.SafeGetValue(itemData, ['数量', 'quantity'], 1), 10);
        const itemInAltar = altarItems.get(itemName);
        const currentAltarQuantity = itemInAltar ? itemInAltar.数量 : 0;
        const availableQuantity = originalQuantity - currentAltarQuantity;

        if (availableQuantity <= 0) {
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`已将所有“${itemName}”放入献祭槽。`);
            return;
        }

        const handleAddition = (quantityToAdd) => {
            if (itemInAltar) {
                itemInAltar.数量 += quantityToAdd;
            } else {
                const newItem = { ...itemData, 数量: quantityToAdd };
                altarItems.set(itemName, newItem);
            }
            renderAltar();
            updateTotalValue();
        };

        if (originalQuantity > 1) {
            this.promptDecompositionQuantity(itemData, availableQuantity, handleAddition);
        } else {
            handleAddition(1);
        }
    });

    // 核心修改2：点击献祭槽物品时的逻辑
    altarListEl.addEventListener('click', e => {
        const itemEl = e.target.closest('.decom-altar-item');
        if (!itemEl) return;
        const itemName = itemEl.dataset.itemName;
        const itemInAltar = altarItems.get(itemName);
        if (itemInAltar) {
            itemInAltar.数量--;
            if (itemInAltar.数量 <= 0) {
                altarItems.delete(itemName);
            }
            renderAltar();
            updateTotalValue();
        }
    });

    decomposeBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        if (altarItems.size === 0) return;
        let totalValue = 0;
        altarItems.forEach(item => totalValue += this.calculateItemValue(item));

        this.showCustomConfirm(`确定要分解这些物品以换取 ${totalValue} 星界之尘吗？此操作不可撤销。`,
            () => this.performDecomposition(Array.from(altarItems.values()), totalValue)
        );
    });
},

// 执行分解的核心函数
async performDecomposition(itemsToDecompose, totalValue) {
    if (itemsToDecompose.length === 0) return;
    this.showTemporaryMessage('正在分解物品...');

    let removeCommands = '';
    itemsToDecompose.forEach(item => {
        const itemName = this.SafeGetValue(item, ['名称', 'name']);
        const category = item.sourceCategory;
        // 注意：这里的实现简化为直接移除整个物品堆叠，未来可优化为减少数量
        removeCommands += `_.remove('${category}.${itemName}'); `;
    });

    // 更新星界之尘数量
    this.gachaState.astralDust += totalValue;
    this.saveGachaState();

    // 通过指令系统移除物品
    try {
        await this.handleAction(`[指令] ${removeCommands}`);
        this.showTemporaryMessage(`分解成功！获得 ${totalValue} 星界之尘。`, 3000);
        // 刷新分解界面
        this.renderDecompositionTab();
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('分解物品时执行指令失败:', e);
        this.showTemporaryMessage('分解失败，请重试。');
        // 如果失败，回滚星界之尘
        this.gachaState.astralDust -= totalValue;
        this.saveGachaState();
    }
},

        // --- 新增：分解时选择数量的弹窗函数 ---
promptDecompositionQuantity(itemData, availableQuantity, callback) {
    const itemName = this.SafeGetValue(itemData, ['名称', 'name']);
    const existingModal = document.getElementById('quantity-prompt-modal');
    if(existingModal) existingModal.remove();

    const modal = document.createElement('div');
    modal.id = 'quantity-prompt-modal';
    modal.className = 'modal-overlay';
    modal.style.cssText = 'display: flex; z-index: 1002;'; // 确保在Gacha模态框之上
    modal.innerHTML = `
        <div class="modal-content" style="width: 450px; height: auto; max-height: none;">
            <div class="modal-header"><h2 class="modal-title">选择分解数量</h2></div>
            <div class="modal-body" style="padding: 20px;">
                <p style="margin-bottom: 15px; color: #d2b48c;">请选择要加入献祭槽的 <strong>${itemName}</strong> 数量：</p>
                <p style="font-size: 12px; color: #a09c91; margin-bottom: 10px;">当前可添加数量：${availableQuantity}</p>
                <div class="setting-control" style="margin-bottom: 20px;">
                    <input type="range" id="quantity-slider" class="font-slider" min="1" max="${availableQuantity}" value="1">
                    <input type="number" id="quantity-input" class="font-size-input" min="1" max="${availableQuantity}" value="1">
                </div>
                <div style="display: flex; gap: 10px; justify-content: flex-end;">
                    <button id="quantity-cancel" class="interaction-btn">取消</button>
                    <button id="quantity-add-all" class="interaction-btn btn-secondary">全部添加</button>
                    <button id="quantity-confirm" class="interaction-btn primary-btn">确认</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;
    document.querySelector('.guixu-root-container').appendChild(modal);

    const slider = modal.querySelector('#quantity-slider');
    const input = modal.querySelector('#quantity-input');
    const confirmBtn = modal.querySelector('#quantity-confirm');
    const cancelBtn = modal.querySelector('#quantity-cancel');
    const addAllBtn = modal.querySelector('#quantity-add-all');

    const syncValues = (source) => {
        const value = source.value;
        if (source === slider) input.value = value;
        if (source === input) slider.value = value;
    };
    slider.addEventListener('input', () => syncValues(slider));
    input.addEventListener('input', () => syncValues(input));

    const closeAndCallback = (value) => {
        const quantity = parseInt(value, 10);
        if (!isNaN(quantity) && quantity > 0) {
            callback(quantity);
        }
        modal.remove();
    };

    confirmBtn.addEventListener('click', () => closeAndCallback(input.value));
    addAllBtn.addEventListener('click', () => closeAndCallback(availableQuantity));
    cancelBtn.addEventListener('click', () => modal.remove());
    input.addEventListener('keypress', (e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter') confirmBtn.click(); });
    setTimeout(() => input.focus(), 100);
},       // 图鉴标签页的完整渲染与事件绑定
renderGalleryTab() {
    const container = document.getElementById('gacha-tab-gallery');
    let gridHtml = '';
    const allChars = [...this.gachaCharacterPool.ssr, ...this.gachaCharacterPool.sr, ...this.gachaCharacterPool.r];
    // 按稀有度排序
    allChars.sort((a,b) => (b.rarity === 'SSR' ? 3 : b.rarity === 'SR' ? 2 : 1) - (a.rarity === 'SSR' ? 3 : a.rarity === 'SR' ? 2 : 1));

    allChars.forEach(char => {
        const isUnlocked = this.gachaCollection[char.id];
        const cardClass = `gallery-card rarity-${char.rarity} ${isUnlocked ? 'unlocked' : 'gallery-card-locked'}`;
        const bgImageStyle = isUnlocked && char.image ? `background-image: url('${char.image}');` : '';
gridHtml += `
        <div class="${cardClass}" title="${char.name} - ${char.series}" data-char-id="${char.id}" style="${bgImageStyle}">
                ${isUnlocked ? `<div class="gallery-card-name">${char.name}</div>` : ''}
            </div>
        `;
    });
    container.innerHTML = `<div class="gallery-grid">${gridHtml}</div>`;

    // 绑定点击事件
    container.querySelector('.gallery-grid').addEventListener('click', e => {
        const card = e.target.closest('.gallery-card.unlocked');
        if (!card) return;
        const charId = card.dataset.charId;
        const charData = allChars.find(c => c.id === charId);
        if (charData) {
            this.showGachaCharacterDetails(charData);
        }
    });
},

    const footerEl = document.getElementById('gacha-details-footer');

    if (!modal || !titleEl || !bodyEl || !footerEl) {
        console.error('Gacha详情模态框的元素未找到!');
        return;

        <p><strong>适配序列:</strong> ${charData.sequence || '未知'}</p>

    if (charData.rarity === 'SSR' && charData.resource) {
        infoHtml += `
            <div class="gacha-details-resource">
                <p><strong>初始资源:</strong> ${charData.resource.name} (${charData.resource.tier}级${charData.resource.type})</p>
                <p><em>${charData.resource.description}</em></p>

        ${joinButtonHtml}

                        keys: [characterName],
                        content: `正在等待AI生成角色设定...`,

                    proceedWithGeneration();
                }
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('检查或创建世界书条目时失败:', error);
                this.showTemporaryMessage(`操作失败！ ${error.message}`, 4000);
                return;
            }
        });
    }


    this.openModal('gacha-details-modal', true);
},

   // --- 新增：背景预览辅助函数 ---
updateBgPreview(bgId) {
    const previewImg = document.getElementById('bg-preview-image');
    if (!previewImg) return;

    if (bgId === 'default' || !bgId) {
        previewImg.src = ''; // 默认背景不预览
        return;
    }
    const bgData = this.customBackgrounds.find(bg => bg.id === bgId);
    if (bgData) {
        previewImg.src = bgData.data;
    }
},
        // --- 新增：布局与尺寸控制函数 ---
applyDimensions() {
    const rootContainer = document.querySelector('.guixu-root-container');
    if (!rootContainer) return;

    if (this.isFullScreenLayout) {
        rootContainer.style.maxWidth = '100vw';
        rootContainer.style.height = '100vh';
        // 禁用滑块
        document.getElementById('width-slider')?.setAttribute('disabled', 'true');
        document.getElementById('height-slider')?.setAttribute('disabled', 'true');
    } else {
        rootContainer.style.maxWidth = this.widthSetting;
        rootContainer.style.height = this.heightSetting;
        // 启用滑块
        document.getElementById('width-slider')?.removeAttribute('disabled');
        document.getElementById('height-slider')?.removeAttribute('disabled');
    }
},

async saveDimensions() {
    await AppStorage.saveData('layout_dimensions', {
        width: this.widthSetting,
        height: this.heightSetting,
        isFullScreen: this.isFullScreenLayout
    });
},

async loadDimensions() {
    const saved = await AppStorage.loadData('layout_dimensions', {
        width: '900px',
        height: '600px',
        isFullScreen: false
    });
    this.widthSetting = saved.width;
    this.heightSetting = saved.height;
    this.isFullScreenLayout = saved.isFullScreen;
    this.applyDimensions();
},                        async showGuixuSystem() {
    this.openModal('guixu-system-modal');

            return;

                    <div class="attribute-item"><span class="attribute-name">当前周目</span><span class="attribute-value">第 ${currentLife} 次</span></div>
                    <div class="attribute-item"><span class="attribute-name">身体年龄</span><span class="attribute-value">${shengli} / ${shengliMax}</span></div>
                    <div class="attribute-item"><span class="attribute-name">灵魂年龄</span><span class="attribute-value">${xinli} / ${xinliMax}</span></div>
                    <div class="attribute-item"><span class="attribute-name">源堡空间</span><span class="attribute-value">${guixuSpace}</span></div>
                    <div class="attribute-item"><span class="attribute-name">本周目抉择</span><span class="attribute-value">${currentChoice}</span></div>
                    <div class="attribute-item" style="margin-top: 15px;"><span class="attribute-name">灵性聚合</span><span class="attribute-value">${chargeTime}%</span></div>
                    <div class="details-progress-bar">
                        <div class="details-progress-fill" style="width: ${chargeTime}%; background: linear-gradient(90deg, #483D8B, #8A2BE2, #C71585);"></div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div style="padding: 20px 10px; text-align: center; margin-top: auto;">
                 <button id="btn-trigger-guixu" class="interaction-btn btn-danger" style="width: 80%; padding: 12px; font-size: 16px;">失控重置</button>
            </div>
        `;

        document.getElementById('btn-trigger-guixu').addEventListener('click', () => {
            this.showCustomConfirm('你确定要重置时间线吗？所有未固化的记忆都将消散在历史迷雾中。', async () => {
                try {
                    const command = '{{user}}选择了重置，世界将回到最初的锚点';
                    await this.handleAction(command);
                    this.showTemporaryMessage('时间线已重置...');
                    this.closeAllModals();
                } catch (error) {
                    console.error('执行重置指令时出错:', error);
                    this.showTemporaryMessage('重置指令失败！');
                }
            });
        });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('加载源堡系统时出错:', error);
        body.innerHTML =
          '<p class="modal-placeholder" style="text-align:center; color:#a09c91; font-size:12px;">加载数据时出错。</p>';
    }
},

   showAbilities() {
      this.openModal('abilities-modal');
      const body = document.querySelector('#abilities-modal .modal-body');
      if (!body) return;

      const currentSequenceName = this.SafeGetValue(this.currentMvuState?.stat_data, '当前序列', null);
      const allAbilities = this.currentMvuState?.stat_data?.['序列能力列表'] || [];

      let addAbilityFormHtml = '';
      // 新增：如果玩家有序列（不是普通人），则显示添加表单
      if (currentSequenceName && !currentSequenceName.includes('普通人')) {
        addAbilityFormHtml = `
            <div class="panel-section" style="margin-bottom: 20px;">
                <div class="section-title">手动添加能力 (${currentSequenceName})</div>
                <div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 10px; padding: 10px;">
                    <input id="manual-ability-name" type="text" class="quick-send-input" placeholder="输入能力名称...">
                    <textarea id="manual-ability-desc" class="quick-send-input" placeholder="输入能力描述..." style="height: 60px;"></textarea>
                    <div style="display: flex; gap: 10px; align-items: center;">
                        <select id="manual-ability-type" class="quick-send-input" style="height: 32px; flex-grow: 1;">
                            <option value="非凡能力">非凡能力</option>
                            <option value="被动特性">被动特性</option>
                            <option value="仪式能力">仪式能力</option>
                                               <option value="神之权柄">神之权柄</option>
                        </select>
                        <button id="btn-manual-add-ability" class="interaction-btn primary-btn">确认添加</button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;
      }

      if (allAbilities.length === 0 && !addAbilityFormHtml) {
        body.innerHTML = '<p class=\"modal-placeholder\" style=\"text-align:center; color:#a09c91; font-size:12px;\">尚未获得任何序列能力。</p>';
        return;
      }

      const groupedAbilities = allAbilities.reduce((acc, ability) => {
        const key = ability.fromSequence || '未知来源';
        if (!acc[key]) {
          acc[key] = [];
        }
        acc[key].push(ability);
        return acc;
      }, {});

      const sortedGroups = Object.keys(groupedAbilities).sort((a, b) => {
        const matchA = a.match(/序列(\\d+)/);
        const matchB = b.match(/序列(\\d+)/);
        const rankA = matchA ? parseInt(matchA[1], 10) : 99;
        const rankB = matchB ? parseInt(matchB[1], 10) : 99;
        return rankB - rankA;
      });

      let html = addAbilityFormHtml; // 将表单放在最前面
      for (const groupName of sortedGroups) {
        const abilitiesInGroup = groupedAbilities[groupName];
   //console.log('[groupName原始值]', groupName);
 const groupRegex = new RegExp('序列(\\d+)');
    const tierMatch = groupName.match(groupRegex);
 const pureTier = tierMatch ? `序列${tierMatch[1]}` : groupName;
 //console.log('[分类标题正则匹配结果]', tierMatch);
 //console.log('[提取的pureTier]', pureTier);
 const tierStyle = this.getTierStyle(pureTier);
  //console.log('[生成的tierStyle]', tierStyle);
      html += `
          <details class=\"inventory-category\" open>
            <summary class=\"inventory-category-title\" style=\"${tierStyle}\">${groupName}</summary>
            <div class=\"inventory-item-list\">
        `;

        abilitiesInGroup.forEach(ability => {
 //console.log('[ability.fromSequence原始值]', ability.fromSequence);
 const abilityRegex = new RegExp('序列(\\d+)');
 const abilityTierMatch = ability.fromSequence.match(abilityRegex);
 const abilityPureTier = abilityTierMatch ? `序列${abilityTierMatch[1]}` : '序列9';
 //console.log('[能力项正则匹配结果]', abilityTierMatch);
 //console.log('[能力项提取的abilityPureTier]', abilityPureTier);
 const abilityNameStyle = this.getTierStyle(abilityPureTier);
  //console.log('[能力项生成的abilityNameStyle]', abilityNameStyle);
       html += `
            <div class=\"inventory-item\" style=\"align-items: flex-start;\">
              <div class=\"item-name-desc\">
                <p class=\"item-name\" style=\"${abilityNameStyle}\">${ability.name}</p>
                <p class=\"item-description\">${ability.description}</p>
              </div>
              <div class=\"item-meta\">
                 <span class=\"item-tier-display\">${ability.type}</span>
              </div>
            </div>
          `;
        });

        html += `</div></details>`;
      }
      body.innerHTML = html;

      // 新增：为新添加的按钮绑定事件
      document.getElementById('btn-manual-add-ability')?.addEventListener('click', () => this.handleManualAddAbility());
    },

          async handleManualAddAbility() {
      const nameInput = document.getElementById('manual-ability-name');
      const descInput = document.getElementById('manual-ability-desc');
      const typeSelect = document.getElementById('manual-ability-type');

      if (!nameInput || !descInput || !typeSelect) return;

      const name = nameInput.value.trim();
      const desc = descInput.value.trim();
      const type = typeSelect.value;

      if (!name) {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('能力名称不能为空。');
        return;
      }

      this.showTemporaryMessage('正在添加新能力...');

      try {
        const newState = _.cloneDeep(this.currentMvuState);
        const currentAbilities = _.get(newState, 'stat_data.序列能力列表', []);

        if (currentAbilities.some(ab => ab.name === name)) {
            this.showTemporaryMessage('已存在同名能力，无法重复添加。');
            return;
        }

        const fromSequence = this.SafeGetValue(this.currentMvuState.stat_data, '当前序列', '手动添加');

        const newAbility = {
            name: name,
            description: desc || '无详细描述。',
            type: type,
            fromSequence: fromSequence
        };

        currentAbilities.push(newAbility);
        _.set(newState, 'stat_data.序列能力列表', currentAbilities);

        // 将更新后的状态静默保存回SillyTavern
        const messages = await getChatMessages('0');
        if (messages && messages.length > 0) {
            const messageZero = messages[0];
            messageZero.data = newState;
            await TavernHelper.setChatMessages([messageZero], { refresh: 'none' });

            this.currentMvuState = newState; // 更新内部状态
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`能力 “${name}” 添加成功！`);
            this.showAbilities(); // 刷新能力列表界面
        } else {
            throw new Error('无法获取聊天记录以保存状态。');
        }

      } catch (error) {
        console.error('手动添加能力时出错:', error);
        this.showTemporaryMessage(`添加失败: ${error.message}`);
      }
    },
    /**
 * 提取并补充序列能力（纯函数，无副作用）
 * @param {Object} inputState - 传入的最新状态（变量更新后的状态）
 * @returns {Object} 修改后的状态（仅补充序列能力，不修改其他字段）
 */
async updateAcquiredAbilities(inputState) {
  // 1. 严格校验输入：必须传入最新状态，且深克隆避免引用污染
  if (!inputState?.stat_data) {
    console.warn('[源堡-能力] 中断：无有效输入状态');
    return inputState; // 无修改，返回原状态
  }
  const targetState = _.cloneDeep(inputState); // 仅操作克隆体，不碰全局状态

  // 2. 获取当前玩家序列名称（如"序列5-旅行家"）
  let currentSequenceName = this.SafeGetValue(targetState.stat_data, '当前序列', null);
  if (!currentSequenceName || currentSequenceName.includes('普通人')) {
    console.log('[源堡-能力] 普通人，无非凡能力能力');
    return targetState; // 无修改，返回原状态
  }

  try {
    // 3. 从世界书读取「神之途径」和「序列能力」数据（核心修改：新增序列能力fallback）
    const readLorebookEntry = async (comment) => {
      const bookName = '1源堡';
      try {
        const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
        const targetEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === comment);
        if (!targetEntry || !targetEntry.content.trim()) return null;
        // 清理JSON中多余逗号（兼容玩家常见语法错误）
        const cleanedContent = targetEntry.content.trim()
          .replace(/,\\s*([}])/g, '$1');
        //console.log(`[世界书] 解析${comment}，清理后内容:`, cleanedContent);
        return JSON.parse(cleanedContent); // 解析清理后的内容
      } catch (e) {
        console.error(`[世界书] 解析${comment}失败！错误:`, e.message);
        //console.error(`[世界书] ${comment}原始内容:`, targetEntry?.content || '无');
        return null;
      }
    };

    // 4. 读取序列能力数据
    // 读取神之途径（无fallback，必须从世界书获取）
    const godPathways = await readLorebookEntry('[神之途径]');
    // 读取序列能力（新增：失败则用全局sequenceAbilitiesDB替代）
    let sequenceAbilities = await readLorebookEntry('[序列能力]');

    // 序列能力读取失败时，切换到全局静态库
    if (!sequenceAbilities || typeof sequenceAbilities !== 'object') {
    console.warn('[源堡-能力] 世界书[序列能力]读取失败，启用全局sequenceAbilitiesDB替代');
    // 校验全局库是否存在且格式正确
    if (window.sequenceAbilitiesDB && typeof window.sequenceAbilitiesDB === 'object') {
       sequenceAbilities = window.sequenceAbilitiesDB; // 切换到备用库
    } else {
       console.error('世界书[序列能力]失败且全局sequenceAbilitiesDB无效');
       return;
      }
    }

    // 校验数据有效性（神之途径仍强制校验，序列能力已通过fallback确保有效）
    if (!godPathways || typeof godPathways !== 'object') throw new Error('世界书[神之途径]格式错误');

    // 5. 匹配当前序列所属途径及索引
    let targetPathway = null, currentSeqIndex = -1;
    // 序列标准化函数——去除前后空格、中间所有空格、统一横线
    const normalizeSeq = (seqStr) => {
  try {
    //console.log(`[normalizeSeq 开始] 接收序列: "${seqStr}"，类型: ${typeof seqStr}`); // 新增：确认输入类型
    if (!seqStr) {
      console.log(`[normalizeSeq] 空序列，直接返回`); // 新增
      return '';
    }
    //console.log(`[标准化前] 序列: ${seqStr}`);

    // 第一步：执行 trim()，加日志
    const trimmed = seqStr.trim();
    //console.log(`[步骤1-Trim后] 序列: "${trimmed}"`); // 新增：确认trim是否执行

    // 第二步：执行第一个replace（空格处理），加日志
    const noSpace = trimmed.replace(/\s+/g, '');
    //console.log(`[步骤2-去空格后] 序列: "${noSpace}"`); // 新增：确认replace是否执行

    // 第三步：执行第二个replace（连字符处理），加日志
    const normalized = noSpace.replace(/\\-+/g, '-');
    //console.log(`[步骤3-统一横线后] 序列: "${normalized}"`); // 新增：确认第二个replace是否执行

    //console.log(`[标准化后] 最终序列: ${normalized}`);
    return normalized;
  } catch (e) {
    // 增强错误日志：同时用log和error，确保能看到
    console.log(`[normalizeSeq 捕获错误] 序列: "${seqStr}"`);
    console.error(`[normalizeSeq 错误详情] 消息: ${e.message}，堆栈: ${e.stack}`);
    return seqStr ? seqStr.trim() : '';
  }
};
    const normalizedCurrentSeq = normalizeSeq(currentSequenceName);
    for (const [pathwayName, sequences] of Object.entries(godPathways)) {
      //console.log(`[匹配循环] 正在检查途径: "${pathwayName}"`);
 const seqIndex = sequences.findIndex(seq => normalizeSeq(seq) === normalizedCurrentSeq);
      if (seqIndex !== -1) {
        targetPathway = pathwayName;
        currentSeqIndex = seqIndex;
        break;
      }
    }
    const targetSequences = godPathways[targetPathway];
 if (!targetPathway || currentSeqIndex === -1) {
      this.showTemporaryMessage(`无法识别序列「${currentSequenceName}」，检查[神之途径]`, 10000);
      return targetState;
    } else {
       //console.log(`[能力提取] 匹配成功：途径=${targetPathway}，当前序列索引=${currentSeqIndex}，总序列数=${targetSequences.length}`);
      }
      const currentSeqMatch = currentSequenceName.match(/序列([0-9]+)/);
      const currentSeqRank = currentSeqMatch ? parseInt(currentSeqMatch[1], 10) : 9;
      //console.log(`[能力提取] 当前角色序列等级：${currentSeqRank}（数字越小，序列越高）`);
      // 6. 提取当前及所有前置序列的能力（9→当前等级，兼容备用库结构）
      const requiredAbilities = [];
      // 能力键名标准化函数——兼容空格、横线、前置0错误（修复：补充函数闭合大括号）
      const normalizeAbilityKey = (key) => {
      if (!key) return '';
      return key
        .trim()
        .replace(/\s+/g, '')
        .replace(/[_-—–]+/g, '-')
        .replace(/序列0(\\d)/g, '序列$1');
    };
    // 提前标准化所有序列能力的键（避免循环内重复处理，提升性能）
    const normalizedSequenceAbilities = {};
    Object.entries(sequenceAbilities).forEach(([key, abilities]) => {
      const normalizedKey = normalizeAbilityKey(key);
      normalizedSequenceAbilities[normalizedKey] = abilities;
    });

 const normalizedPathway = normalizeAbilityKey(targetPathway);
 //console.log(`[途径标准化] 原始途径名: "${targetPathway}" → 标准化后: "${normalizedPathway}"`);
 //console.log(`[序列能力校验] 标准化后所有键名:`, Object.keys(normalizedSequenceAbilities));
   for (let i = 0; i <= currentSeqIndex; i++) {
       const seqFullName = targetSequences[i];
 const normalizedSeq = normalizeSeq(seqFullName);
 //console.log(`[能力提取-循环${i}] 标准化后序列："${normalizedSeq}"`);
       const seqRankMatch = normalizedSeq.match(/序列([0-9]+)/);
      if (!seqRankMatch) {
 console.log(`[能力提取-循环${i}] 等级提取失败！标准化序列："${normalizedSeq}"`);
 continue;
 }

      const seqRank = seqRankMatch[1];
 const seqRankNum = parseInt(seqRank, 10);
 //console.log(`[能力键生成] 原始序列等级: ${seqRank}，当前角色等级: ${currentSeqRank}`);
 if (seqRankNum < currentSeqRank) {
 console.log(`[能力提取-循环${i}] 跳过高序列能力：序列${seqRank}（当前角色序列${currentSeqRank}）`);
 continue;
 }
     const rawAbilityKey = `${normalizedPathway}-序列${seqRank}`;
      const abilityKey = normalizeAbilityKey(rawAbilityKey); // 兼容世界书和备用库的键结构
 //console.log(`[能力提取-循环${i}] 提取到等级=${seqRank}，能力键名=${abilityKey}，是否存在=${!!normalizedSequenceAbilities[abilityKey]}`);
 //console.log(`[能力键匹配] 原始键: ${rawAbilityKey} → 标准化键: ${abilityKey}`);
 //console.log(`[能力键校验] 该键对应能力:`, normalizedSequenceAbilities[abilityKey]?.map(ab => ab.name) || '无');
       const seqAbilities = normalizedSequenceAbilities[abilityKey] || [];

      requiredAbilities.push(...seqAbilities.map(ab => ({
        ...ab,
        fromSequence: seqFullName,
        seqRank: parseInt(seqRank, 10)
      })));
    }

    // 7. 去重：保留手动添加能力，补充缺失系统能力
    let currentAbilities = this.currentMvuState.stat_data['序列能力列表'] || [];
    if (typeof currentAbilities === 'string' || !Array.isArray(currentAbilities)) currentAbilities = [];

console.log(`[能力提取] 提取到前置能力总数=${requiredAbilities.length}，当前已拥有能力数=${currentAbilities.length}`);
     const existingNames = new Set(currentAbilities.map(ab => ab.name.trim()));
    const missingAbilities = requiredAbilities.filter(ab => !existingNames.has(ab.name.trim()));
    console.log(`[能力提取] 缺失能力数=${missingAbilities.length}，缺失能力=${missingAbilities.map(ab => ab.name).join(',')}`);
 if (missingAbilities.length === 0) {
      console.log('[源堡-能力] 已拥有所有前置能力');
      return targetState;
    }

    // 8. 排序：按序列等级从低到高，仅修改克隆体的序列能力列表，不碰全局状态
    missingAbilities.sort((a, b) => b.seqRank - a.seqRank);

    targetState.stat_data['序列能力列表'] = [...currentAbilities, ...missingAbilities];

    // 9. 反馈与刷新，仅提示，不修改任何存储/缓存
    const unlockedSeqs = [...new Set(missingAbilities.map(ab => ab.fromSequence))].join('、');
    this.showTemporaryMessage(`已解锁能力：${missingAbilities.map(ab => ab.name).join('、')}（来自${unlockedSeqs}）`, 8000);
    if (document.querySelector('#abilities-modal')) this.showAbilities();

    // 10. 返回修改后的克隆体（无全局副作用）
    return targetState;

  } catch (error) {
    console.error('[源堡-能力] 更新失败：', error);
    this.showTemporaryMessage(`能力更新失败：${error.message}`, 8000);
 return targetState; // 出错时返回原状态，不覆盖新值
 }
},
       async showCharacterDetails() {
            this.openModal('character-details-modal');
            const body = document.querySelector('#character-details-modal .modal-body');
            if (!body) return;
            body.innerHTML =
              '<p class="modal-placeholder" style="text-align:center; color:#a09c91; font-size:12px;">正在调取档案...</p>';

            try {
              const messages = await getChatMessages(getCurrentMessageId());
              const stat_data = messages?.[0]?.data?.stat_data;
              if (!stat_data) {
                body.innerHTML =
                  '<p class="modal-placeholder" style="text-align:center; color:#a09c91; font-size:12px;">无法加载档案数据。</p>';
                return;
              }

              this.updateDisplayedAttributes();

              const huoli = document.getElementById('attr-huoli')?.innerText || 'N/A';
              const fali = document.getElementById('attr-fali')?.innerText || 'N/A';
              const shenhai = document.getElementById('attr-shenhai')?.innerText || 'N/A';
              const daoxin = document.getElementById('attr-daoxin')?.innerText || 'N/A';
              const kongsu = document.getElementById('attr-kongsu')?.innerText || 'N/A';
              const qiyun = document.getElementById('attr-qiyun')?.innerText || 'N/A';
              const shengli = this.SafeGetValue(stat_data, '身体年龄', 'N/A');
              const xinli = this.SafeGetValue(stat_data, '灵魂年龄', 'N/A');
              const xiuxingjindu = this.SafeGetValue(stat_data, '消化进度', '0');
              const xiuxingpingjing = this.SafeGetValue(stat_data, '失控进度', '0');

              body.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="panel-section">
                        <div class="section-title">调查员档案 <span style="font-size: 10px; color: #a09c91;">(当前/上限)</span></div>
                        <div class="attributes-list">
                            <div class="attribute-item"><span class="attribute-name">活力</span><span class="attribute-value">${huoli}</span></div>
                            <div class="attribute-item"><span class="attribute-name">灵性</span><span class="attribute-value">${fali}</span></div>
                            <div class="attribute-item"><span class="attribute-name">理智</span><span class="attribute-value">${shenhai}</span></div>
                            <div class="attribute-item"><span class="attribute-name">人性</span><span class="attribute-value">${daoxin}</span></div>
                            <div class="attribute-item"><span class="attribute-name">敏捷</span><span class="attribute-value">${kongsu}</span></div>
                            <div class="attribute-item"><span class="attribute-name">运气</span><span class="attribute-value">${qiyun}</span></div>
                            <div class="attribute-item"><span class="attribute-name">身体年龄</span><span class="attribute-value">${shengli}</span></div>
                            <div class="attribute-item"><span class="attribute-name">灵魂年龄</span><span class="attribute-value">${xinli}</span></div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="panel-section">
                        <div class="section-title">扮演法详情</div>
                        <div class="attributes-list">
                            <div class="attribute-item">
                                <span class="attribute-name">消化进度</span>
                                <span class="attribute-value">${xiuxingjindu}%</span>
                            </div>
                            <div class="details-progress-bar">
                                <div class="details-progress-fill" style="width: ${xiuxingjindu}%;"></div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="attribute-item" style="margin-top: 8px;">
                                <span class="attribute-name">失控进度</span>
                                <span class="attribute-value">${xiuxingpingjing}</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `;
            } catch (error) {
              console.error('加载档案详情时出错:', error);
              body.innerHTML =
                '<p class="modal-placeholder" style="text-align:center; color:#a09c91; font-size:12px;">加载数据时出错。</p>';
            }
          },

          openModal(modalId, keepOpen = false) {
    if (!keepOpen) {
        this.closeAllModals();
    }
    const modal = document.getElementById(modalId);
    if (modal) {
        modal.style.display = 'flex';
        if (keepOpen) {
            const highestZ = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.modal-overlay'))
                .filter(el => el.style.display === 'flex' && el.id !== modalId)
                .reduce((maxZ, el) => Math.max(maxZ, parseInt(window.getComputedStyle(el).zIndex, 10) || 1000), 1000);
            modal.style.zIndex = highestZ + 1;
        } else {
            modal.style.zIndex = '';
        }
    }
},

          closeAllModals() {
    document.querySelectorAll('.modal-overlay').forEach(modal => {
        modal.style.display = 'none';
    });
    // 关键修复：当关闭任何模态框时，都检查并清除导入状态
    if (this.importedSaveData) {
        this.importedSaveData = null;
        this.showTemporaryMessage('存档导入已取消。');
    }
},

          showCustomConfirm(message, onConfirm, onCancel = null) {
    const modal = document.getElementById('custom-confirm-modal');
    const messageEl = document.getElementById('custom-confirm-message');
    const okBtn = document.getElementById('custom-confirm-btn-ok');
    const cancelBtn = document.getElementById('custom-confirm-btn-cancel');

    if (!modal || !messageEl || !okBtn || !cancelBtn) return;

    messageEl.innerHTML = message;

    // 使用 .cloneNode(true) 来移除旧的事件监听器，防止重复触发
    const newOkBtn = okBtn.cloneNode(true);
    okBtn.parentNode.replaceChild(newOkBtn, okBtn);

    const newCancelBtn = cancelBtn.cloneNode(true);
    cancelBtn.parentNode.replaceChild(newCancelBtn, cancelBtn);

    newOkBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        this.closeAllModals();
        if (typeof onConfirm === 'function') {
            onConfirm();
        }
    });

    // 【核心修正】为“取消”按钮添加回调逻辑
    newCancelBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        this.closeAllModals();
        if (typeof onCancel === 'function') {
            onCancel(); // 执行传入的取消回调
        }
    });

    this.openModal('custom-confirm-modal');
},

          async showInventory() {
            this.openModal('inventory-modal');
            const body = document.querySelector('#inventory-modal .modal-body');
            if (!body) return;

            body.innerHTML =
              '<p class=\"modal-placeholder\" style=\"text-align:center; color:#a09c91; font-size:12px;\">正在清点物品...</p>';

            try {
              let stat_data = this.currentMvuState?.stat_data;
              if (!stat_data || Object.keys(stat_data).length === 0) {
 console.log('[物品栏] 内存数据无效，尝试从快照读取');
 const latestSnapshot = this.chatHistoryCache.at(-1);
 if (latestSnapshot?.data?.stat_data) {
 stat_data = latestSnapshot.data.stat_data;
 this.currentMvuState = latestSnapshot.data;
 } else {
               body.innerHTML =
                  '<p class=\"modal-placeholder\" style=\"text-align:center; color:#a09c91; font-size:12px;\">无法获取物品数据。</p>';
                return;
  }
            }
 body.innerHTML = this.renderInventory(stat_data || {});
            } catch (error) {
              console.error('加载物品栏时出错:', error);
              body.innerHTML = `<p class=\"modal-placeholder\" style=\"text-align:center; color:#a09c91; font-size:12px;\">加载物品栏时出错: ${error.message}</p>`;
            }
          },
          // HTML转义工具函数（处理中文/英文引号、特殊字符）
    escapeHtml(str) {
        if (!str) return '';
        // 用对象映射显式管理转义规则，避免链式replace的引号冲突
        const escapeRules = {
          '&': '&amp;',
          '"': '&quot;',
          //"'": '&apos;',
          '“': '&ldquo;',
          '”': '&rdquo;',
          '‘': '&lsquo;',
          '’': '&rsquo;'
        };
        // 正则用[]包裹，显式匹配所有需要转义的字符
        return str.replace(/[&"'“”‘’]/g, match => escapeRules[match]);
    },

    // HTML解码工具函数（还原转义后的名称）
    unescapeHtml(str) {
        if (!str) return '';
        const tempDiv = document.createElement('div');
        // 利用浏览器原生解析HTML的能力还原转义字符
        tempDiv.innerHTML = str.replace(/<script[^>]*>([\S\s]*?)<\/script>/gi, ''); // 过滤脚本（安全防护）
        return tempDiv.textContent || tempDiv.innerText;
    },

          async showRelationships() {
    this.openModal('relationships-modal');
    const body = document.querySelector('#relationships-modal .modal-body');
    if (!body) return;

    body.innerHTML = '<p class=\"modal-placeholder\">正在梳理人际关系...</p>';

    try {
        let stat_data = this.currentMvuState?.stat_data;
 if (!stat_data || Object.keys(stat_data).length === 0) {
 console.log('[人物关系列表] 内存数据无效，尝试从快照中读取');
 const latestSnapshot = this.chatHistoryCache.at(-1);
 if (latestSnapshot?.data?.stat_data) {
 stat_data = latestSnapshot.data.stat_data;
 this.currentMvuState = latestSnapshot.data;
 console.log('[人物关系列表] 从快照读取数据成功');
 } else {
 body.innerHTML = '<p class=\"modal-placeholder\">暂无人物关系快照数据。</p>';
 return;
 }
 }
                   const relationshipsObj = this.SafeGetValue(stat_data, '人物关系列表', {});

       body.innerHTML = this.renderRelationships(relationshipsObj);

        const container = document.getElementById('relationship-cards-container');
        if (container) {
            container.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                const button = e.target.closest('.rel-action-btn');
                if (button) {
                    const card = button.closest('.relationship-card');
                    const action = button.dataset.action;
                    const charName = card.dataset.charName;
                    this.handleRelationshipAction(action, charName);
                }
            });
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('加载人物关系时出错:', error);
        body.innerHTML = `<p class=\"modal-placeholder\">加载人物关系时出错: ${error.message}</p>`;
    }
},

           renderRelationships(relationshipsObj) {
    if (typeof relationshipsObj !== 'object' || relationshipsObj === null) {
        return '<p class="modal-placeholder" style="text-align:center; color:#a09c91; font-size:12px;">暂无重要人际关系。</p>';
    }

    const allGachaChars = [ ...this.gachaCharacterPool.ssr, ...this.gachaCharacterPool.sr, ...this.gachaCharacterPool.r ];

    const validRelationships = Object.entries(relationshipsObj).filter(([name, details]) => {
        return name !== '$meta' && typeof details === 'object' && details !== null;
    });

    if (validRelationships.length === 0) {
        return '<p class="modal-placeholder" style="text-align:center; color:#a09c91; font-size:12px;">暂无重要人际关系。</p>';
    }

    validRelationships.sort(([nameA, detailsA], [nameB, detailsB]) => (detailsB.isImportant ? 1 : 0) - (detailsA.isImportant ? 1 : 0));

    let html = `
 <style>
        /* 能力清单容器样式 */
        .relationship-abilities {
            margin: 10px 0;
            padding: 8px 12px;
            background-color: rgba(30, 25, 18, 0.3);
            border-radius: 4px;
        }
        /* 能力清单标题样式 */
        .relationship-abilities strong {
            color: #d9c6a8;
            font-size: 13px;
            margin-right: 6px;
        }
        /* 能力清单内容样式 */
        .abilities-list {
            color: #f0e68c;
            font-size: 12.5px;
            line-height: 1.5;
            white-space: normal;
        }
        /* 能力项前缀符号 */
        .abilities-list::before {
            content: "• ";
            opacity: 0.7;
        }
    </style>
    <div id="relationship-cards-container">
`;

    const parseTimeKeyForSort = (key) => {
      // 兼容以下所有格式：
      // - 带星期几+时段："第五纪1349年6月29日星期五 下午 14:35"
      // - 带星期几+无时段："第五纪1349年6月29日星期五 14:35"
      // - 不带星期几+时段："第五纪1349年6月29日 下午 14:35"
      // - 不带星期几+无时段："第五纪1349年6月29日 14:35"
      // - 多空格变体："第五纪 1349年 6月 29日 星期五 下午 14:35"
      const match = key.match(/第五纪\s*(\d+)年\s*(\d+)月\s*(\d+)日\s*(?:星期. )?\s*(?:凌晨|清晨|上午|中午|下午|傍晚|晚间|晚上|深夜|)\s*(\d+):(\d+)/);
      if (!match) return 0; // 格式完全错误则排最前
      const [, year, month, day, hour, minute] = match.map(Number);
      // 构造权重数值
      return year * 1000000 + month * 70000 + day * 2000 + hour * 70 + minute;
    };
     validRelationships.forEach(([name, rel]) => {
        try {
            const gachaData = allGachaChars.find(c => c.name === name);
            const imageUrl = gachaData ? gachaData.image : null;

            let portraitHtml = '';
            if (imageUrl) {
                portraitHtml = `<div class="relationship-portrait" style="background-image: url('${imageUrl}');"></div>`;
            }

            const tierOrSequence = this.SafeGetValue(rel, '当前序列', '普通人');
            const relationship = this.SafeGetValue(rel, '关系', '陌生人');
            const description = this.SafeGetValue(rel, '描述', this.SafeGetValue(rel, '性格', '背景不详'));
            const favorability = parseInt(this.SafeGetValue(rel, '好感度', 0), 10);
            const abilities = this.SafeGetValue(rel, '能力清单', '');
           let abilitiesHtml = '';
           if (abilities.trim()) {
           abilitiesHtml = `
           <div class="relationship-abilities">
           <strong>能力清单:</strong>
           <span class="abilities-list">${abilities}</span>
           </div>
           `;
           }
           const isImportant = rel.isImportant || false;

            // --- 核心修复：增强事件历史的读取逻辑，使其更健壮 ---
            let currentState = '暂无记录';
            const eventHistory = this.SafeGetValue(rel, '事件历史', null);


            if (typeof eventHistory === 'object' && eventHistory !== null && !Array.isArray(eventHistory)) {
                // 格式正确：是键值对对象
                const eventKeys = Object.keys(eventHistory).filter(key => key !== '$meta');
                if (eventKeys.length > 0) {
                    const latestKey = eventKeys.sort((a, b) => {
