                  <div class="detail-item"><strong>周目概述:</strong> ${data['本周目概述'] || data['周目概述'] || '不详'}</div>
                  <div class="detail-item"><strong>周目成就:</strong> ${data['本周目成就'] || data['周目成就'] || '无'}</div>
                  <div class="detail-item"><strong>获得物品:</strong> ${data['本周目获得物品'] || data['获得物品'] || '无'}</div>
                  <div class="detail-item"><strong>人物关系:</strong> ${data['本周目人物关系网'] || data['人物关系网'] || '无'}</div>
                  <div class="detail-item"><strong>失控原因:</strong> ${data['失控原因'] || '不详'}</div>
                  <div class="detail-item"><strong>周目总结:</strong> ${data['本周目总结'] || data['周目总结'] || '无'}</div>
                  <div class="detail-item"><strong>周目评价:</strong> ${data['本周目评价'] || data['周目评价'] || '无'}</div>
              </div>
          </div>
      </div>`;
  }
  html += '</div>';
  return html;
},

          bindJourneyListeners() {
            const timelineContainer = document.querySelector('.timeline-container');
            if (timelineContainer) {
              timelineContainer.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
                const timelineEvent = e.target.closest('.timeline-event');
                if (timelineEvent) this.handleJourneyEventClick(timelineEvent);
              });
            }
          },

          handleJourneyEventClick(eventElement) {
            const detailedInfo = eventElement.querySelector('.timeline-detailed-info');
            if (!detailedInfo) return;
            if (detailedInfo.style.display === 'block') {
                detailedInfo.style.display = 'none';
            } else {
                detailedInfo.style.display = 'block';
            }
          },

 // 【新增】写入当前线索的辅助函数
 async writeCluesToLorebook(silent = false) {

                      async writeNovelModeToLorebook(silent = false) {
 const content = this.lastExtractedNovelText;
 await this.writeToLorebook('小说模式', content, silent);
 },

          async writeToLorebook(baseEntryKey, contentToWrite, silent = false) {
    if (!contentToWrite || contentToWrite.trim() === '') {
        if (!silent) this.showTemporaryMessage('没有可写入的内容。');
        return;
    }

    const index = this.unifiedIndex;
    const finalEntryKey = index > 1 ? `${baseEntryKey}(${index})` : baseEntryKey;
    const bookName = '1源堡';
    const reformattedContent = contentToWrite.trim();

    try {
        const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
        let targetEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === finalEntryKey);

        // 如果条目不存在，则创建它
        if (!targetEntry) {
            if (!silent) this.showTemporaryMessage(`条目 \"${finalEntryKey}\" 不存在，正在创建...`);
            const baseEntryTemplate = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === baseEntryKey);
            const newEntryData = {
                comment: finalEntryKey, content: reformattedContent,
                keys: baseEntryTemplate ? [...baseEntryTemplate.keys, finalEntryKey] : [finalEntryKey],
                enabled: false, selective: baseEntryTemplate?.selective, constant: baseEntryTemplate?.constant,
                position: baseEntryTemplate?.position, case_sensitive: baseEntryTemplate?.case_sensitive,
            };
            await TavernHelper.createLorebookEntries(bookName, [newEntryData]);
            if (!silent) this.showTemporaryMessage(`已创建并写入到“${finalEntryKey}”。`);
            if (this.isAutoToggleLorebookEnabled) this.updateAutoToggledEntries();
            return;
        }

        // 如果条目已存在，执行更新或追加逻辑
        const existingContent = targetEntry.content || '';
        let finalContent = '';

        if (baseEntryKey === '本周目经历') {
            const existingEvents = this.parseJourneyEntry(existingContent);
            const newEvents = this.parseJourneyEntry(reformattedContent);
            if (newEvents.length === 0) return;
            const newEvent = newEvents[0];
            const newEventId = newEvent['序号'];
            const eventIndex = existingEvents.findIndex(event => event['序号'] === newEventId);
            if (eventIndex !== -1) {
                existingEvents[eventIndex] = newEvent;
                if (!silent) this.showTemporaryMessage(`已更新事件 #${newEventId}。`);
            } else {
                existingEvents.push(newEvent);
                if (!silent) this.showTemporaryMessage(`已追加新事件 #${newEventId}。`);
            }
            existingEvents.sort((a, b) => (parseInt(a.序号, 10) || 0) - (parseInt(b.序号, 10) || 0));
            finalContent = existingEvents.map(ev => this.stringifyJourneyEvent(ev)).join('\n\n');
        } else if (baseEntryKey === '本周目核心记忆' || baseEntryKey === '当前线索') {
            // 【新增逻辑】对于核心记忆和线索，执行覆盖式更新
            finalContent = reformattedContent;
            if (!silent) this.showTemporaryMessage(`已更新“${finalEntryKey}”。`);
        } else {
            // 【保留】对于其他条目（如历史的投影），执行追加逻辑
            if (existingContent.includes(reformattedContent)) {
              if (!silent) this.showTemporaryMessage('内容已存在，无需重复写入。');
              return;
            }
            finalContent = existingContent + (existingContent ? '\n\n' : '') + reformattedContent;
            if (!silent) this.showTemporaryMessage(`已追加内容到“${finalEntryKey}”。`);
        }

        // 将最终构建好的内容写回世界书
        await TavernHelper.setLorebookEntries(bookName, [{ uid: targetEntry.uid, content: finalContent }]);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error(`写入世界书 \"${finalEntryKey}\" 时出错:`, error);
        if (!silent) this.showTemporaryMessage(`写入失败: ${error.message}`);
    }
},

          async writeCharacterCardToLorebook() {
            const content = this.lastExtractedCharacterCard;
            if (!content) {
              this.showTemporaryMessage('没有可写入的角色内容。');
              return;
            }
            const button = document.getElementById('btn-write-character-card');
            if (button) button.textContent = '写入中...';
            try {
              const lines = content.trim().split('\n');
              const characterData = {};
              lines.forEach(line => {
                const parts = line.split('|');
                if (parts.length >= 2) {
                  const key = parts[0].trim();
                  const value = parts.slice(1).join('|').trim();
                  characterData[key] = value;
                }
              });
              const characterName = characterData['姓名'];
              if (!characterName) throw new Error('无法从提取内容中找到角色“姓名”。');
              const bookName = '1源堡';
              const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
              const existingEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === characterName);
              if (existingEntry) {
                this.showTemporaryMessage(`角色“${characterName}”已存在，请手动修改。`);
                if (button) button.textContent = '写入世界书';
                return;
              }
              await TavernHelper.createLorebookEntries(bookName, [{
                  comment: characterName, keys: [characterName],
                  content: content.trim(), enabled: true,
              }]);
              this.showTemporaryMessage(`已成功创建角色“${characterName}”。`);
              if (button) button.textContent = '写入成功';
              setTimeout(() => { if (button) button.textContent = '写入世界书'; }, 2000);
            } catch (error) {
              console.error('写入角色卡到世界书时出错:', error);
              this.showTemporaryMessage(`写入失败: ${error.message}`);
              if (button) button.textContent = '写入失败';
            }
          },

          async loadAndDisplayCurrentScene(messageOrText = null) {
    const gameTextDisplay = document.getElementById('game-text-display');
    if (!gameTextDisplay) return;
    try {
        let contentToParse = null;

        // --- 核心修复：智能判断传入的是对象还是字符串 ---
        if (typeof messageOrText === 'string') {
            contentToParse = messageOrText;
        } else if (messageOrText && typeof messageOrText === 'object') {
            contentToParse = messageOrText.message;
        } else {
            const messages = await getChatMessages(getCurrentMessageId());
            if (!messages || messages.length === 0) return;
            const lastAiMessage = [...messages].reverse().find(m => m.role === 'assistant');
            if (lastAiMessage) contentToParse = lastAiMessage.message;
        }
        // --- 修复结束 ---

        if (contentToParse) {
            this.lastExtractedThinking = this._extractLastTagContent('thinking', contentToParse);
            const displayText = this._getDisplayText(contentToParse);
            gameTextDisplay.innerHTML = this.formatMessageContent(displayText);

            const thinkingBtn = document.getElementById('btn-toggle-thinking');
            if (thinkingBtn) {
                thinkingBtn.style.display = this.lastExtractedThinking ? 'flex' : 'none';
            }
            this.hideThinkingOverlay();

            this.lastExtractedDanmaku = this._extractAllTags('dm', contentToParse);
            const dmBtn = document.getElementById('btn-toggle-dm');
            if (dmBtn) dmBtn.style.display = this.lastExtractedDanmaku.length ? 'flex' : 'none';

            this.lastExtractedNovelText = this._extractLastTagContent('gametxt', contentToParse);
            this.lastExtractedJourney = this._extractLastTagContent('本周目经历', contentToParse);
            this.lastExtractedPastLives = this._extractLastTagContent('历史的投影', contentToParse);
            this.lastExtractedVariables = this._extractLastTagContent('UpdateVariable', contentToParse, true);
            this.lastExtractedCharacterCard = this._extractLastTagContent('角色提取', contentToParse);
            this.lastExtractedCoreMemory = this._extractLastTagContent('本周目核心记忆', contentToParse);
            this.lastExtractedClues = this._extractLastTagContent('当前线索', contentToParse);

            const actionText = this._extractLastTagContent('action', contentToParse);
            this.lastExtractedActions = actionText ? this._parseActions(actionText) : [];
            this.updateQuickOptionsButtonState();
        }
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('[源堡] 加载并显示当前场景时出错:', error);
        gameTextDisplay.innerHTML = `<gametxt>加载场景时出错。</gametxt>`;
    }
},

          startAutoWritePolling() {
    this.stopAutoWritePolling();
    console.log('[源堡] 启动自动写入轮询 (setTimeout模式)...');
    const poll = async () => {
        if (!this.isAutoWriteEnabled) return;

        // 检查是否有新的“本周目经历”需要写入
        if (this.lastExtractedJourney && this.lastExtractedJourney !== this.lastWrittenJourney) {
            await this.writeJourneyToLorebook(true);
            this.lastWrittenJourney = this.lastExtractedJourney; // 写入成功后，更新“记忆”
        }

        // 检查是否有新的“历史的投影”需要写入
        if (this.lastExtractedPastLives && this.lastExtractedPastLives !== this.lastWrittenPastLives) {
            await this.writePastLivesToLorebook(true);
            this.lastWrittenPastLives = this.lastExtractedPastLives; // 写入成功后，更新“记忆”
        }

        // 【新增】检查是否有新的“本周目核心记忆”需要写入
        //if (this.lastExtractedCoreMemory && this.lastExtractedCoreMemory !== this.lastWrittenCoreMemory) {
        //    await this.writeCoreMemoryToLorebook(true);
        //    this.lastWrittenCoreMemory = this.lastExtractedCoreMemory;
        //}

    // 【新增】检查是否有新的“当前线索”需要写入
        if (this.lastExtractedClues && this.lastExtractedClues !== this.lastWrittenClues) {
            await this.writeCluesToLorebook(true);
            this.lastWrittenClues = this.lastExtractedClues;
        }

     // 计划下一次轮询
        if (this.isAutoWriteEnabled) {
            this.autoWriteIntervalId = setTimeout(poll, 5000); // 轮询间隔改为5秒
        }
    };
    this.autoWriteIntervalId = setTimeout(poll, 5000); // 立即开始第一次轮询
},

          stopAutoWritePolling() {
    if (this.autoWriteIntervalId) {
        console.log('[源堡] 停止自动写入轮询。');
        clearTimeout(this.autoWriteIntervalId); // 改为 clearTimeout
        this.autoWriteIntervalId = null;
    }
},

          startNovelModeAutoWritePolling() {
    this.stopNovelModeAutoWritePolling();
    console.log('[源堡] 启动小说模式自动写入轮询 (setTimeout模式)...');
    const poll = async () => {
        if (!this.isNovelModeEnabled) return;

        // 检查是否有新的小说内容需要写入
        if (this.lastExtractedNovelText && this.lastExtractedNovelText !== this.lastWrittenNovelText) {
            await this.writeNovelModeToLorebook(true);
            this.lastWrittenNovelText = this.lastExtractedNovelText; // 写入成功后，更新“记忆”
        }

        // 计划下一次轮询
        if (this.isNovelModeEnabled) {
            this.novelModeAutoWriteIntervalId = setTimeout(poll, 5000);
        }
    };
    this.novelModeAutoWriteIntervalId = setTimeout(poll, 5000);
},

          stopNovelModeAutoWritePolling() {
    if (this.novelModeAutoWriteIntervalId) {
        console.log('[源堡] 停止小说模式自动写入轮询。');
        clearTimeout(this.novelModeAutoWriteIntervalId); // 改为 clearTimeout
        this.novelModeAutoWriteIntervalId = null;
    }
},

          async saveEquipmentState() {
            await AppStorage.saveData('equipped_items', this.equippedItems);
          },

          // ====================================================================
    // 核心装备加载函数 (Equipment Loading Core Functions)
    // ====================================================================

    async loadEquipmentState(retryCount = 0) {
        const MAX_RETRY = 5; // 最多重试5次（共5秒）
        // 数据库就绪检查
        const dbReady = await AppStorage.ensureDbOpen();
        if (!dbReady) {
            if (retryCount >= MAX_RETRY) {
                console.error(`[loadEquipmentState] 重试${MAX_RETRY}次后数据库仍未就绪，使用内存缓存`);
                this.equippedItems = window._tempEquipCache || {}; // 最终兜底
                return;
            }
            console.warn(`[loadEquipmentState] 数据库未就绪，${retryCount+1}秒后重试`);
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
            return this.loadEquipmentState(retryCount + 1); // 递增重试次数
        }
         try {
        // 优先读取currentMvuState中的正确装备数据
        let sourceData = null;
        if (this.currentMvuState?.equipped_items && typeof this.currentMvuState.equipped_items === 'object') {
            sourceData = this.currentMvuState.equipped_items;
            console.log('[loadEquipmentState] 优先使用读档恢复的装备数据');
        } else {
            // 无内存数据时，再从IndexDB加载（兼容首次启动）
            sourceData = await AppStorage.loadData('equipped_items');
            console.log('[loadEquipmentState] 从IndexDB加载装备数据');
        }

        // 校验并同步正确数据到IndexDB
        if (sourceData && typeof sourceData === 'object' && !Array.isArray(sourceData)) {
            this.equippedItems = sourceData;
            // 将正确数据写入IndexDB，确保后续加载同步
            await AppStorage.saveData('equipped_items', this.equippedItems);
            console.log('[loadEquipmentState] 装备数据同步到IndexDB完成');
        } else {
            // 数据异常时的修复逻辑（保留）
            if (sourceData) {
                console.warn('[loadEquipmentState] 装备数据异常，尝试修复');
                this.equippedItems = this._repairEquipmentData(sourceData);
            } else {
                this.equippedItems = {};
                console.log('[loadEquipmentState] 初始化空装备数据');
            }
            // 修复后同步到IndexDB
            await AppStorage.saveData('equipped_items', this.equippedItems);
        }
                const defaultTextMap = { wuqi: '武器', fangju: '衣物', shipin: '饰品', fabao1: '封印物', zhuxiuGongfa: '主要扮演法', fuxiuXinfa: '辅助能力' };
                for (const slotKey in defaultTextMap) {
                    const slotElement = document.getElementById(`equip-${slotKey}`);
                    if (!slotElement) continue;
                    const itemData = this.equippedItems[slotKey];
                    if (itemData && typeof itemData === 'object') {
                        const tier = this.SafeGetValue(itemData, '品阶', '普通');
                        const tierStyle = this.getTierStyle(tier);
                        slotElement.textContent = this.SafeGetValue(itemData, '名称');
                        slotElement.setAttribute('style', tierStyle);
                        slotElement.classList.add('equipped');
                        slotElement.dataset.itemDetails = JSON.stringify(itemData);
                    } else {
                        slotElement.textContent = defaultTextMap[slotKey];
                        slotElement.classList.remove('equipped');
                        slotElement.removeAttribute('style');
                        delete slotElement.dataset.itemDetails;
                    }
                }
                console.log('%c[loadEquipmentState 前] currentMvuState 是否存在:', 'color: purple;', !!this.currentMvuState);
                console.log('%c[loadEquipmentState 前] currentMvuState.stat_data:', 'color: purple;', this.currentMvuState?.stat_data);
                this.updateDisplayedAttributes();

        } catch (e) {
            console.error('[loadEquipmentState] 加载异常，尝试从缓存恢复:', e);
            // 🔴 第三步：异常时不清空，尝试从内存缓存恢复（避免丢失当前数据）
            if (!this.equippedItems || typeof this.equippedItems !== 'object') {
                this.equippedItems = window._tempEquipCache || {}; // 内存临时缓存
            }
            // 仅在完全无法恢复时，才初始化空对象（极端情况）
            if (typeof this.equippedItems !== 'object') {
                this.equippedItems = {};
               console.warn('[loadEquipmentState] 极端情况：装备数据完全无法恢复，初始化空对象');
            }
        }
    },

    loadEquipmentFromMVU(data) {
        const equipmentMap = { '武器': 'wuqi', '主要扮演法': 'zhuxiuGongfa', '辅助能力': 'fuxiuXinfa', '衣物': 'fangju', '饰品': 'shipin', '封印物': 'fabao1' };
        const defaultTextMap = { wuqi: '武器', fangju: '衣物', shipin: '饰品', fabao1: '封印物', zhuxiuGongfa: '主要扮演法', fuxiuXinfa: '辅助能力' };

        for (const [mvuKey, slotKey] of Object.entries(equipmentMap)) {
            const slot = document.getElementById(`equip-${slotKey}`);
            if (!slot) continue;

            const item = this.SafeGetValue(data, mvuKey, null);
if (item && typeof item === 'object') {
    this.equippedItems[slotKey] = item; // 新增：核心修复，同步内部状态
    const tier = this.SafeGetValue(item, '品阶', '普通');
    const tierStyle = this.getTierStyle(tier);
    slot.textContent = this.SafeGetValue(item, '名称');
    slot.setAttribute('style', tierStyle);
    slot.classList.add('equipped');
    slot.dataset.itemDetails = JSON.stringify(item);
} else {
    this.equippedItems[slotKey] = null; // 新增：核心修复，同步内部状态
    slot.textContent = defaultTextMap[slotKey];
    slot.classList.remove('equipped');
    slot.removeAttribute('style');
    delete slot.dataset.itemDetails;
}
        }
    },

  refreshEquipmentSlots() {
    const defaultTextMap = { wuqi: '武器', fangju: '衣物', shipin: '饰品', fabao1: '封印物', zhuxiuGongfa: '扮演法', fuxiuXinfa: '辅助能力' };
    for (const slotKey in this.equippedItems) {
        const slotElement = document.getElementById(`equip-${slotKey}`);
        if (!slotElement) continue;
        const itemData = this.equippedItems[slotKey];
        if (itemData && typeof itemData === 'object') {
            const tier = this.SafeGetValue(itemData, ['品阶', 'tier', '序列'], '普通');
            const tierStyle = this.getTierStyle(tier);
            slotElement.textContent = this.SafeGetValue(itemData, '名称');
            slotElement.setAttribute('style', tierStyle);
            slotElement.classList.add('equipped');
            slotElement.dataset.itemDetails = JSON.stringify(itemData);
        } else {
            slotElement.textContent = defaultTextMap[slotKey];
            slotElement.classList.remove('equipped');
            slotElement.removeAttribute('style');
            delete slotElement.dataset.itemDetails;
        }
    }
},
async savePendingActions() {
    try {
        await AppStorage.saveData('pending_actions', this.pendingActions);
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('保存指令队列状态失败:', e);
    }
},

       async loadPendingActions() {
    try {
        const savedActions = await AppStorage.loadData('pending_actions');
        // 确保赋值后一定是数组（即使savedActions格式异常）
        this.pendingActions = Array.isArray(savedActions) ? savedActions : [];
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('加载指令队列状态失败，使用内存缓存:', e);
        // 失败时不删除存储（保留可能的有效数据），只确保内存中是数组
        if (!Array.isArray(this.pendingActions)) {
            this.pendingActions = []; // 仅内存兜底，不删存储
        }
    }
},

          async updateAutoToggledEntries(andDisableAll = false) {
            const bookName = '1源堡';
            const index = this.unifiedIndex;
            const journeyKey = index > 1 ? `本周目经历(${index})` : '本周目经历';
            const pastLivesKey = index > 1 ? `历史的投影(${index})` : '历史的投影';
            try {
                let allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
                const entriesToCreate = [];
                const targetJourneyEntry = allEntries.find(e => e.comment === journeyKey);
                if (!targetJourneyEntry) {
                    const baseTemplate = allEntries.find(e => e.comment === '本周目经历');
                    if (baseTemplate) {
                        const newJourneyEntry = { ...baseTemplate };
                        delete newJourneyEntry.uid;
                        newJourneyEntry.comment = journeyKey; newJourneyEntry.content = '';
                        newJourneyEntry.keys = [...(baseTemplate.keys || []), journeyKey];
                        newJourneyEntry.enabled = true; newJourneyEntry.position = 'before_character_definition';
                        newJourneyEntry.order = 20;
                        entriesToCreate.push(newJourneyEntry);
                    }
                }
                const targetPastLivesEntry = allEntries.find(e => e.comment === pastLivesKey);
                if (!targetPastLivesEntry) {
                    const baseTemplate = allEntries.find(e => e.comment === '历史的投影');
                    if (baseTemplate) {
                        const newPastLivesEntry = { ...baseTemplate };
                        delete newPastLivesEntry.uid;
                        newPastLivesEntry.comment = pastLivesKey; newPastLivesEntry.content = '';
                        newPastLivesEntry.keys = [...(baseTemplate.keys || []), pastLivesKey];
                        newPastLivesEntry.enabled = true; newPastLivesEntry.position = 'before_character_definition';
                        newPastLivesEntry.order = 19;
                        entriesToCreate.push(newPastLivesEntry);
                    }
                }
                if (entriesToCreate.length > 0) {
                    await TavernHelper.createLorebookEntries(bookName, entriesToCreate);
                    console.log(`[源堡自动开关] 已自动创建 ${entriesToCreate.length} 个新世界书条目。`);
                    allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
                }
                const entriesToUpdate = [];
                for (const entry of allEntries) {
                    const isJourneyEntry = entry.comment.startsWith('本周目经历');
                    const isPastLivesEntry = entry.comment.startsWith('历史的投影');
                    if (!isJourneyEntry && !isPastLivesEntry) continue;
                    const isTarget = entry.comment === journeyKey || entry.comment === pastLivesKey;
                    const shouldBeEnabled = isTarget && !andDisableAll;
                    if (entry.enabled !== shouldBeEnabled) {
                        entriesToUpdate.push({ uid: entry.uid, enabled: shouldBeEnabled });
                    }
                }
                if (entriesToUpdate.length > 0) {
                    await TavernHelper.setLorebookEntries(bookName, entriesToUpdate);
                    console.log(`[源堡自动开关] 更新了 ${entriesToUpdate.length} 个世界书条目状态。`);
                }
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('[源堡自动开关] 更新世界书条目状态时出错:', error);
            }
          },

          startAutoTogglePolling() {
              this.stopAutoTogglePolling(false);
              console.log('[源堡] 启动世界书自动开关轮询...');
              this.updateAutoToggledEntries();
              // 【核心修复】将轮询间隔从5秒延长到30秒，大幅降低内存压力
              this.autoToggleIntervalId = setInterval(() => this.updateAutoToggledEntries(), 30000);
          },

          stopAutoTogglePolling(disableEntries = true) {
              if (this.autoToggleIntervalId) {
                  console.log('[源堡] 停止世界书自动开关轮询。');
                  clearInterval(this.autoToggleIntervalId);
                  this.autoToggleIntervalId = null;
              }
              if (disableEntries) this.updateAutoToggledEntries(true);
          },

           applyRandomBackground() {
            const backgrounds = [
              'https://i.postimg.cc/wv6qJydc/bei-jing-tu5.png',
              'https://i.postimg.cc/sfHjQgHh/bei-jing-tu4.png',
              'https://i.postimg.cc/xjpfJ1pN/bei-jing-tu3.png',
              'https://i.postimg.cc/y6p1g8pS/bei-jing-tu2.png',
              'https://i.postimg.cc/J7YrDzYy/bei-jing-tu1.png',
              'https://i.postimg.cc/JzbrYVMN/bei-jing-tu10.png',
              'https://i.postimg.cc/43sJrLx1/bei-jing-tu14.png',
              'https://i.postimg.cc/HLdpfZk0/bei-jing-tu13.png',
              'https://i.postimg.cc/3w1K7Xkt/bei-jing-tu15.png',
              'https://i.postimg.cc/9fbWVdD1/bei-jing-tu16.png',
              'https://i.postimg.cc/mrjbRYcx/bei-jing-tu18.png',
              'https://i.postimg.cc/GpKcrFBH/bei-jing-tu20.png',
              'https://i.postimg.cc/GmkLgwdL/bei-jing-tu9.png',
              'https://i.postimg.cc/Vkt3kGnY/121599044-p0.jpg',
              'https://i.postimg.cc/vTDKF3bq/121599044-p2.jpg',


            ];
            try {
            if (backgrounds.length === 0) return;
            const bgUrl = backgrounds[Math.floor(Math.random() * backgrounds.length)];
            if (!bgUrl) return;
            const container = document.querySelector('.guixu-root-container');
            if (!container) return;
            container.style.backgroundImage = `url('${encodeURI(bgUrl)}')`;
            } catch (e) {
            // 加载失败（跨域、404等），直接跳过，只打印日志不干扰其他功能
             console.log('背景图加载失败，已跳过:', e.message);
           }
          },

          async executeQuickSend() {
            const input = document.getElementById('quick-send-input');
            if (!input) return;
            const userMessage = input.value.trim();
            await this.handleAction(userMessage);
          },

    async createPendingAutoSave() {
    if (!this.currentMvuState) {
        console.warn('[AutoSave] 状态为空，无法创建待定存档。');
        this.pendingAutoSave = null;
        return;
    }
    try {
        let currentMessageContent = '';
        try {
            const messages = await getChatMessages('0');
            currentMessageContent = messages?.[0]?.message || '';
        } catch (e) {
            console.warn('[AutoSave] 创建快照时获取消息内容失败。');
        }

        const cleanedMessageContent = currentMessageContent.replace(new RegExp('', 'g'), '');

        this.pendingAutoSave = {
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            save_name: '自动存档 - 上一回合',
            message_content: cleanedMessageContent,
            mvu_data: _.cloneDeep(this.currentMvuState), // 使用深拷贝确保数据独立
            equipped_items: _.cloneDeep(this.equippedItems),
            pending_actions: _.cloneDeep(this.pendingActions) || [],
            gacha_data: { // 确保Gacha数据也被快照
                state: _.cloneDeep(this.gachaState),
                collection: _.cloneDeep(this.gachaCollection),
                history: _.cloneDeep(this.gachaHistory)
            },

        };

        // --- 新增：捕获当前“本周目经历”的内容并存入快照 ---
        try {
            const bookName = '1源堡';
            const index = this.unifiedIndex;
            const journeyKey = index > 1 ? `本周目经历(${index})` : '本周目经历';
            const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
            const journeyEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === journeyKey);

            this.pendingAutoSave.lorebook_content = {
                journey: journeyEntry ? journeyEntry.content : null
            };
        } catch (e) {
            console.error('[AutoSave] 捕获世界书快照失败:', e);
            this.pendingAutoSave.lorebook_content = { journey: null };
        }
        // --- 新增结束 ---

        console.log('[源堡] 已成功创建“上一回合”的待定存档快照。');
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('[源堡] 创建待定存档快照时出错:', error);
        this.pendingAutoSave = null;
    }
},

    async performAutoSave() {
    if (!this.pendingAutoSave) {
        console.warn('[AutoSave] 没有待定的存档快照，跳过提交。');
        return;
    }

    try {
        const allSaves = await this.getSavesFromStorage();

        if (allSaves['auto_save_slot_1']) {
            allSaves['auto_save_slot_2'] = _.cloneDeep(allSaves['auto_save_slot_1']);
            allSaves['auto_save_slot_2'].save_name = '自动存档 - 上上回合';
        }

        allSaves['auto_save_slot_1'] = this.pendingAutoSave;

        await AppStorage.saveData('multi_save_data', allSaves);
        console.log('[源堡] 已成功提交待定存档至“上一回合”存档位。');

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('[源堡] 提交自动存档时发生错误:', error);
    } finally {
        this.pendingAutoSave = null; // 无论成功与否，都清空待定存档
    }
},

     async startStreamingMirror(targetDisplayElement) {
            console.log('[源堡-镜像] 启动镜像流程，开始轮询查找原生UI元素...');
            const selector = '.last_mes .mes_text'; // 我们要寻找的目标选择器

            // 这是一个持续尝试寻找目标元素的Promise
            return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
                const timeout = 20000; // 最长等待20秒
                const pollInterval = 100; // 每0.1秒检查一次
                let elapsedTime = 0;

                const intervalId = setInterval(() => {
                    const nativeChatOutput = document.querySelector(selector);

                    if (nativeChatOutput) {
                        // 找到了！停止轮询，启动观测器
                        clearInterval(intervalId);
                        console.log('[源堡-镜像] 成功找到原生UI元素！启动镜像。');

                        const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
                            if (this.isBusy) {
                                this.hideWaitingMessage();
                                targetDisplayElement.innerHTML = nativeChatOutput.innerHTML;
                            }
                        });

                        observer.observe(nativeChatOutput, { childList: true, subtree: true, characterData: true });
                        resolve(observer); // 将观测器实例返回给主流程
                    } else {
                        // 还没找到，继续等待
                        elapsedTime += pollInterval;
                        if (elapsedTime >= timeout) {
                            clearInterval(intervalId);
                            console.error(`[源堡-镜像] 致命错误：轮询${timeout/1000}秒后，仍未能找到原生聊天输出元素 (${selector})。`);
                            reject(new Error('Mirror target not found after timeout.'));
                        }
                    }
                }, pollInterval);
            });
          },



 _createCurrentStatusBlock () {
 if (!this.currentMvuState || !this.currentMvuState.stat_data || !this.calculatedMaxAttributes) { return ''; }
 const stat_data = this.currentMvuState.stat_data;
 let statusParts = [
    '[判定属性（使用当前值而不是上限值进行判定，并根据<动态属性检测系统>处理，特别是出现0或者负数时要最优先处理!!）]',
    '[额外：需关注当前状态和失控进度，用于判定角色状态稳定性]'
  ];
 this.attributeConfig.forEach (attr => {
 const maxVal = this.calculatedMaxAttributes [attr.key];
 const displayName = attr.key.replace('值', '');
 if (typeof maxVal !== 'number' || isNaN(maxVal)) {
 return;
 }
 if (attr.key === '运气') {
 statusParts.push (`- ${displayName}: ${maxVal}`);
 } else {
 const currentVal = Number(this.SafeGetValue(stat_data, attr.currentVar, maxVal));
 statusParts.push(`- ${displayName}: ${Math.min(currentVal, maxVal)}/${maxVal}`);
 }
 });

 return statusParts.join('\n');
},
 // --- 终极解决方案：动态关联性记忆系统 ---

// 1. “记忆组装”核心函数
async _assembleDynamicContext(userMessage) {
    let contextParts = [];
    let memoryParts = [];
    let recentEventsContent = '';
    let coreMemoryPart = '';
    const stat_data = this.currentMvuState?.stat_data;
    if (!stat_data) return '';

    // 提取区域中心坐标
    const regionWithCenter = mapSystem.DEFAULT_LOCATIONS.mainRegions.map(region => {
        const centerX = (Math.min(...region.points.outer.map(p => p.x)) + Math.max(...region.points.outer.map(p => p.x))) / 2;
        const centerY = (Math.min(...region.points.outer.map(p => p.y)) + Math.max(...region.points.outer.map(p => p.y))) / 2;
        return `${region.name}（中心坐标：(${centerX.toFixed(2)}, ${centerY.toFixed(2)})）`;
    });
    // 提取地标精确坐标
    const landmarkWithCoord = mapSystem.DEFAULT_LOCATIONS.landmarks.map(landmark => {
        const landX = parseFloat(landmark.marker.left);
        const landY = parseFloat(landmark.marker.top) * this.Y_SCALE;;
        return `${landmark.name}（坐标：(${landX.toFixed(2)}, ${landY.toFixed(2)})，属于${landmark.mainRegionName}）`;
    });

    const mapOverview = `
<地图地理总览>
- 大型区域（含中心坐标）：${regionWithCenter.join('、')}（神弃之地与西大陆为与世隔绝状态）
- 知名地标：${landmarkWithCoord.join('、')}
- 地理规则：区域间移动需符合地理逻辑（如南北大陆隔狂暴海相望，正常情况下需要坐船等交通工具），移动消耗的时间得正确更新，没有使用超凡手段下从一个城市移动到另一个城市应该经过漫长时间
</地图地理总览>`;

    const playerLocation = {
      区域: stat_data["当前区域"] || "未知",
      地标: stat_data["当前地标"] || "未知",
      坐标: stat_data["当前坐标"] || { x: 50.0, y: 50.0 }
    };

     // 计算当前区域实际面积
    let areaString = "未知";
    const playerRegion = mapSystem.DEFAULT_LOCATIONS.mainRegions.find(r =>
      r.name === playerLocation.区域 || r.name === playerLocation.地标
    );
    if (playerRegion) {
      const regionArea = MapEarthTool.calculatePolygonArea(playerRegion.points);
      areaString = `约 ${regionArea.toLocaleString()} km²`;
    }

    const spatialContextBlock = `
<当前空间情景>
【地图参考：本地图总宽度约为${MapEarthTool.EARTH_CONFIG.mapScaleKm}公里（与地球赤道周长一致）。坐标系为百分比制，(0,0)在左上角。如果有移动，请按照合理的数据继续修改，百分比小于百分之一的移动可忽略】
- **玩家的位置**:
  - 区域: ${playerLocation.区域} / ${playerLocation.地标}
  - 坐标: (${playerLocation.坐标.x.toFixed(2)}, ${playerLocation.坐标.y.toFixed(2)})
  - 区域面积: ${areaString}
</当前空间情景>`;

    const statusBlock = this._createCurrentStatusBlock();
    if (statusBlock) {
        contextParts.push(statusBlock);
        contextParts.push(spatialContextBlock);
        contextParts.push(mapOverview); // 新增：注入地理总览
    }

    // [短期记忆]：自动提取事件，放入 memoryParts
    try {
        const bookName = '1源堡';
        const index = this.unifiedIndex;
        const journeyKey = index > 1 ? `本周目经历(${index})` : '本周目经历';
        const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
        const journeyEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === journeyKey);


        if (journeyEntry && journeyEntry.content) {
            const events = this.parseJourneyEntry(journeyEntry.content);
            if (events.length > 0) {
                const recentEvents = events.slice(-this.recentEventsCount); // 只取最后5个
                recentEventsContent = this.reconstructJourneyEntry(recentEvents);
            }
        }

        const cluesEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === '当前线索');
        if (cluesEntry && cluesEntry.content) {
            recentEventsContent += `\n\n<当前待办线索>\n${cluesEntry.content}\n</当前待办线索>`;
        }

        // 用<>标签包裹近期事件（含线索）
        if (recentEventsContent) {
            recentEventsContent = `<近期发生的几件事，已按序号区分顺序>\n${recentEventsContent}\n</近期发生的几件事，已按序号区分顺序>`;
        }
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[记忆系统] 提取短期记忆时出错:', e);
    }

    // [动态人物档案]：自动筛选并生成相关人物的档案
    try {
        const relationships = this.SafeGetValue(stat_data, '人物关系列表', {});
        const allCharacters = Object.entries(relationships).filter(([name, details]) => name !== '$meta' && typeof details === 'object');

        const relevantCharacters = new Map(); // 使用Map确保角色不重复

        // 筛选标准1：被标记为“重要”的人物
        allCharacters
            .filter(([name, details]) => details.isImportant === true)
            .forEach(([name, details]) => relevantCharacters.set(name, details));

        // 筛选标准2：在最近的对话中被提及的人物
        const lastAiResponse = (await getChatMessages('0'))?.[0]?.message || '';
        const textToScan = `${userMessage} ${this._getDisplayText(lastAiResponse)}`;

        allCharacters.forEach(([name, details]) => {
            if (textToScan.includes(name)) {
                relevantCharacters.set(name, details);
            }
        });

        // (可选) 筛选标准3：在场的任务 (如果未来您的变量中增加了“当前位置”)
        // const playerLocation = this.SafeGetValue(stat_data, '当前位置', null); ...

        // 组装人物档案文本
        if (relevantCharacters.size > 0) {
            let dossierText = '[当前相关人物档案]\n';
            for (const [name, details] of relevantCharacters.entries()) {
                const relationship = this.SafeGetValue(details, '关系', '未知');
                const favorability = this.SafeGetValue(details, '好感度', '未知');
                const lastEventKey = details.事件历史 ? Object.keys(details.事件历史).sort().pop() : null;
                const lastEvent = lastEventKey ? details.事件历史[lastEventKey].substring(0, 50) + '...' : '暂无记录';
                dossierText += `- ${name}: 关系(${relationship}), 好感度(${favorability}). 最新动态: ${lastEvent}\n`;
            }
            memoryParts.push(dossierText);
        }
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[记忆系统] 生成动态人物档案时出错:', e);
    }

    // [核心剧情摘要]  (如果存在)
    try {
        const bookName = '1源堡';
        const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
        const coreMemoryEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === '本周目核心记忆');


        if (coreMemoryEntry && coreMemoryEntry.content) {
            coreMemoryPart = `<核心剧情摘要>\n${coreMemoryEntry.content}\n</核心剧情摘要>`;
        }
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[记忆系统] 提取核心记忆时出错:', e);
    }

    // 组装记忆内容（关键顺序：近期事件→人物档案→核心记忆）
    const wrappedMemory = [];
    // 先添加近期事件（含线索，带<>标签）
    if (recentEventsContent) {
        wrappedMemory.push(recentEventsContent);
    }
    // 再添加人物档案
    if (memoryParts.length > 0) {
        wrappedMemory.push(...memoryParts);
    }
    // 用"之前发生的事情"包裹近期事件和人物档案（不含核心记忆）
    if (wrappedMemory.length > 0) {
        contextParts.push('[以下是之前发生的事情总结（供参考，非本轮新发生内容）]');
        contextParts.push(...wrappedMemory);
        contextParts.push('[以上是之前发生的事情总结（短期内容已结束）]');
    }
    // 最后添加独立的核心剧情摘要（放在近期事件之后，突出重要性）
    if (coreMemoryPart) {
        contextParts.push(coreMemoryPart);
    }

    // 返回最终组合好的、高度浓缩的记忆备忘录
    return contextParts.join('\n\n');
},

  async handleAction(userMessage = '', isBranchingAction = false) {
    // --- 修改：调用新的分支选择处理器 ---
    if (this.isHistoryViewMode && !isBranchingAction) {
        if (!userMessage && this.pendingActions.length === 0) {
            this.showTemporaryMessage('请在返回现在后执行此操作。');
            return;
        }
        // 调用新的分支选择弹窗，而不是直接确认覆盖
        this.handleBranching(userMessage);
        return;
    }
    // --- 修改结束 ---

    this.lastUserMessage = userMessage;
    if (this.isBusy) {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('正在处理上一条指令，请稍候...');
        return;
    }
    this.isBusy = true;

    try {
        // 1. 自动存档快照（保持不变）
        await this.createPendingAutoSave();

        //检查并执行定期自动备份（在发送新消息前保存当前状态）
        await this.checkAndPerformPeriodicBackup();

        // 2. 检查是否有有效输入
        if (!userMessage && this.pendingActions.length === 0) {
            this.isBusy = false;
            this.showTemporaryMessage('请输入行动或在指令中心添加指令后发送。');
            return;
        }

        // 3. 启动加载动画
        this.showWaitingMessage();

        //定义currentViewSnapshot
        let currentViewSnapshot;
        if (this.isHistoryViewMode) {
            // 历史模式：从缓存中取当前查看的回合快照
            const currentViewIndex = this.historyViewIndex ?? (this.chatHistoryCache.length - 1);
            const safeIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(currentViewIndex, this.chatHistoryCache.length - 1));
            currentViewSnapshot = this.chatHistoryCache[safeIndex] || { message_id: 'unknown-history' };
        } else {
            // 活跃模式：取最新快照
            currentViewSnapshot = this.chatHistoryCache.at(-1) || { message_id: 'unknown-active' };
        }
        console.log(`[发送前准备] 当前操作的回合ID: ${currentViewSnapshot.message_id}`);
        // 4. 【核心】调用新函数，组装动态记忆
        const dynamicContext = await this._assembleDynamicContext(userMessage);
        // 基于currentViewSnapshot提取上一轮gametxt（仅活跃模式）
        let lastRoundContent = ''; // 默认空
        if (!this.isHistoryViewMode) { // 仅活跃模式需要上一轮内容
            // 从当前快照的message中提取<gametxt>内容
            if (currentViewSnapshot?.message) {
                const gametxtRegex = /<gametxt>([\s\S]*?)<\/gametxt>/i;
                const matchResult = currentViewSnapshot.message.match(gametxtRegex);
                const lastRoundGametxt = matchResult ? matchResult[1].trim() : '';
                // 有内容则包装成标签
                if (lastRoundGametxt) {
                    lastRoundContent = `<上一轮内容详情>\n${lastRoundGametxt}\n</上一轮内容详情>\n\n`;
                }
            }
        }

        // 5. 准备玩家的“本轮行动”
        let actionPrompt = '';
        if (this.pendingActions.length > 0) {
            actionPrompt += '[本轮组合指令]\n';
            this.pendingActions.forEach(cmd => {
                let actionText = '';
                switch (cmd.action) {
                    case 'equip': actionText = `装备 [${cmd.itemName}] 到 [${cmd.category}]。`; break;
                    case 'unequip': actionText = `卸下 [${cmd.itemName}] 从 [${cmd.category}]。`; break;
                    case 'use': actionText = `使用 ${cmd.quantity} 个 [${cmd.itemName}]。`; break;
                    case 'discard': actionText = `丢弃 ${cmd.quantity ? cmd.quantity + ' 个 ' : ''}[${cmd.itemName}]。`; break;
                }
                actionPrompt += `- ${actionText}\n`;
            });
        }
        if (userMessage) {
            actionPrompt += `[我的行动]${userMessage}\n`;
        }

        // 【核心新增】发送前同步内存中的当前状态到变量管理器
        const syncToTavernHelperBeforeSend = async () => {
        try {
        // 用你系统原生支持的 '0' 范围获取第0条消息
        const messages = await TavernHelper.getChatMessages('0');
        if (!messages || messages.length === 0) {
            console.error('[发送前同步] 无法获取第0条消息，同步失败');
            return;
        }
        const messageZero = messages[0];
        // 存在则更新，保留原有其他字段，覆盖核心数据（完全对齐你的 newSnapshot 结构）
        Object.assign(messageZero.data, {
            ..._.cloneDeep(this.currentMvuState),
            equipped_items: _.cloneDeep(this.equippedItems),
            gacha_data: {
                state: _.cloneDeep(this.gachaState),
                collection: _.cloneDeep(this.gachaCollection),
                history: _.cloneDeep(this.gachaHistory)
            },
        });

        // 用标准方式写回，强制刷新变量管理器
        await TavernHelper.setChatMessages([messageZero], {
            refresh: 'force'
        });

        console.log('[发送前同步成功] 仅更新 data 字段，完全保留原有对话内容');
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('[发送前同步失败]', e.message);
    }
};
      // 执行同步
        await syncToTavernHelperBeforeSend();
      // 6. 将记忆和行动组合为最终发送给AI的指令
        let finalPrompt = `[记忆备忘录]\n${dynamicContext}\n\n${lastRoundContent}\n\n${actionPrompt}\n`;
        finalPrompt += `\n\{\{setvar::我的行动::${userMessage}\}\}`;
        this.lastSentPrompt = finalPrompt; // 用于调试
        await AppStorage.saveData('last_sent_prompt', this.lastSentPrompt);

        // 7. 发送给AI
        const generateConfig = {
            injects: [{ role: 'user', content: finalPrompt, position: 'in_chat', depth: 0, should_scan: true }],
            should_stream: this.isStreamingEnabled,
        };
        await TavernHelper.generate(generateConfig);

    } catch (error) {
        console.error("[源堡] 处理动作时出错:", error);
        this.showTemporaryMessage(`操作失败: ${error.message}`);
        this.isBusy = false;
        this.hideWaitingMessage();
    }
},



          toggleQuickCommands() {
            const popup = document.getElementById('quick-command-popup');
            if (!popup) return;
            if (popup.style.display === 'block') this.hideQuickCommands();
            else this.showQuickCommands();
          },

          showQuickCommands() {
            const popup = document.getElementById('quick-command-popup');
            if (!popup) return;
            if (this.pendingActions.length === 0) {
              popup.innerHTML = '<div class="quick-command-empty">暂无待执行的指令</div>';
            } else {
              let listHtml = '<ul class="quick-command-list">';
              this.pendingActions.forEach(cmd => {
                let actionText = '';
                switch (cmd.action) {
                  case 'equip': actionText = `装备 [${cmd.itemName}] 到 [${cmd.category}] 槽位。`; break;
                  case 'unequip': actionText = `卸下 [${cmd.itemName}] 从 [${cmd.category}] 槽位。`; break;
                  case 'use': actionText = `使用 ${cmd.quantity} 个 [${cmd.itemName}]。`; break;
                  case 'discard': actionText = `丢弃 ${cmd.quantity ? cmd.quantity + ' 个 ' : ''}[${cmd.itemName}]。`; break;
                }
                listHtml += `<li class="quick-command-item">${actionText}</li>`;
              });
              listHtml += '</ul>';
              popup.innerHTML = listHtml;
            }
            popup.style.display = 'block';
          },

          hideQuickCommands() {
            const popup = document.getElementById('quick-command-popup');
            if (popup) popup.style.display = 'none';
          },

    toggleFullScreen() {
            const rootContainer = document.querySelector('.guixu-root-container');
            if (!rootContainer) return;

            if (!document.fullscreenElement) {
                if (rootContainer.requestFullscreen) {
                    rootContainer.requestFullscreen();
                } else if (rootContainer.webkitRequestFullscreen) { /* Safari */
                    rootContainer.webkitRequestFullscreen();
                } else if (rootContainer.msRequestFullscreen) { /* IE11 */
                    rootContainer.msRequestFullscreen();
                }
            } else {
                if (document.exitFullscreen) {
                    document.exitFullscreen();
                }
            }
          },

   hideQuickCommands() {
    const popup = document.getElementById('quick-command-popup');
    if (popup) popup.style.display = 'none';
},

// --- 以下是为“当前选项”功能新增的全部函数 ---
_parseActions(actionText) {
    if (!actionText) return [];
    // 根据换行符分割，并清理每个选项的序号和前后空格
    return actionText.split('\n')
        .map(line => line.trim())
        .filter(line => line)
        .map(line => line.replace(/^\d+\.\s*/, '').trim()); // 移除 "1. ", "2. " 等前缀
},

updateQuickOptionsButtonState() {
    const btn = document.getElementById('btn-quick-options');
    if (btn) {
        // 如果有可用选项，则启用按钮，否则禁用
        btn.disabled = this.lastExtractedActions.length === 0;
    }
},

toggleQuickOptions() {
    const popup = document.getElementById('quick-options-popup');
    if (!popup) return;
    if (popup.style.display === 'block') {
        this.hideQuickOptions();
    } else {
        this.showQuickOptions();
    }
},

showQuickOptions() {
    const popup = document.getElementById('quick-options-popup');
    if (!popup) return;

    if (this.lastExtractedActions.length === 0) {
        popup.innerHTML = '<div class="quick-options-empty">当前没有可用的行动选项</div>';
    } else {
        let listHtml = '<ul class="quick-options-list">';
        this.lastExtractedActions.forEach((actionText, index) => {
            // 为每个选项创建一个包含文本框和按钮的列表项
            listHtml += `
                <li class="quick-options-item editable" data-option-index="${index}">
                    <textarea class="option-textarea">${actionText}</textarea>
                    <div class="option-actions">
                        <button class="option-btn send-option-btn" title="发送此选项">✔️</button>
                        <button class="option-btn delete-option-btn" title="删除此选项">✖️</button>
                    </div>
                </li>
            `;
        });
        listHtml += '</ul>';
        popup.innerHTML = listHtml;
    }
    popup.style.display = 'block';
},

hideQuickOptions() {
    const popup = document.getElementById('quick-options-popup');
    if (popup) popup.style.display = 'none';
},


// 工具函数：处理嵌套路径的设置，支持容器下自动创建新键，非容器则返回错误
/**
 * 设置嵌套对象的属性值，返回操作结果
 * @param {Object} obj - 目标对象
 * @param {string} path - 路径（支持点分隔：如"人物关系列表.肉茧.状态"，或斜杠分隔："/人物关系列表/肉茧/状态"）
 * @param {any} value - 要设置的值
 * @returns {Object} - { success: boolean, error: string | null }
 */
setNestedValue(obj, path, value) {
  try {
    // 1. 统一路径格式：去掉开头的/，将/转为.，处理空路径
    if (!path || typeof path !== 'string') {
      return { success: false, error: '路径不能为空且必须是字符串' };
    }
    const dotPath = path.startsWith('/') ? path.slice(1).replace(/\//g, '.') : path.replace(/\//g, '.');
    const pathSegments = dotPath.split('.').filter(seg => seg.trim() !== ''); // 过滤空段（比如路径中有连续的.）
    if (pathSegments.length === 0) {
      return { success: false, error: '路径解析后为空（请检查路径格式）' };
    }

    // 2. 遍历路径段（除最后一个），处理容器和自动创建
    let current = obj;
    for (let i = 0; i < pathSegments.length - 1; i++) {
      const segment = pathSegments[i];
      const nextSegment = pathSegments[i + 1]; // 仅用于日志，可选

      // 关键：判断当前节点是否为「可扩展容器」（对象/数组，null不算）
      if (current === null || typeof current !== 'object') {
        return {
          success: false,
          error: `路径节点不是可扩展容器（无法创建子键）：${pathSegments.slice(0, i+1).join('.')}（当前节点类型：${typeof current}）`
        };
      }

      // 核心：如果容器中没有该子键，自动创建空对象（因为角色/封印物都是对象类型）
      if (!(segment in current)) {
        console.log(`[setNestedValue] 容器中未找到键${segment}，自动创建空对象（路径：${pathSegments.slice(0, i+1).join('.')}`);
        current[segment] = {}; // 自动创建空对象，用于存储后续属性
      }

      // 移动到下一个节点
      current = current[segment];
    }

    // 3. 设置最后一个段的值
    const lastSegment = pathSegments[pathSegments.length - 1];
    current[lastSegment] = value;
    return { success: true, error: null };

  } catch (e) {
    return {
      success: false,
      error: `设置值失败：${e.message}（路径：${path}）`
    };
  }
},


  // 3. 可选：全局兜底校验方法
  _validateWithZodSchema(obj) {
    try {
      const result = schema.safeParse(obj);
      if (result.success) {
        return { valid: true, error: "", validatedData: result.data };
      } else {
        const errorMessages = result.error.issues.map(issue => {
          const path = issue.path.length > 0 ? issue.path.join('.') : '根节点';
          return `【${path}】：${issue.message}`;
        }).join('\n');
        return { valid: false, error: `数据校验失败：\n${errorMessages}`, validatedData: null };
      }
    } catch (e) {
      return { valid: false, error: `校验异常：${e.message}`, validatedData: null };
    }
  },

// 新增：JSON Patch指令处理工具函数（整合解析+格式化，替代旧的_extractCommands）
// 功能1：解析输入文本为JSON Patch指令数组（供_applyUpdateFallback使用）
// 功能2：生成格式化的JSON Patch文本（供变量编辑器/悬浮窗编辑使用）
_processJsonPatchCommandsEnhanced(inputText) {
  const patchCommands = [];
  this.errorCommands = [];
  let formattedPatchText = ''; // 可编辑的格式化指令文本

  try {
    // 步骤1：提取[]包裹的JSON Patch内容（和原_parseJsonPatchCommands逻辑一致）
    const jsonMatch = inputText.match(/\[([\s\S]*)\]/);
    if (!jsonMatch) {
      this.errorCommands.push("指令格式错误：需用[]包裹的JSON Patch数组（如[{\"op\":\"replace\",\"path\":\"/活力\",\"value\":50}]）");
      return { patchCommands, formattedPatchText };
    }

    // 步骤2：清理文本（兼容中文标点、末尾多余逗号）
    let jsonStr = jsonMatch[0]
      .replace(/,\s*]/, ']')
      .replace(/，/g, ',')
      .replace(/：/g, ':');

    // 步骤3：解析为指令数组
    const commands = JSON.parse(jsonStr);
    if (Array.isArray(commands)) {
      // 过滤合法指令（和原逻辑一致）
      commands.forEach((cmd) => {
        if (
          cmd && typeof cmd === 'object' &&
          ['replace', 'add', 'remove'].includes(cmd.op) &&
          typeof cmd.path === 'string' && cmd.path.startsWith('/')
        ) {
          patchCommands.push(cmd);
        } else {
          this.errorCommands.push(`无效指令：${JSON.stringify(cmd)}（仅支持replace/add/remove，路径需以/开头）`);
        }
      });

      // 步骤4：生成**格式化的JSON Patch文本**（方便用户微调编辑）
      // JSON.stringify的第三个参数是缩进，让文本换行+缩进，易读易改
      formattedPatchText = JSON.stringify(patchCommands, null, 2);
    } else {
      this.errorCommands.push("指令不是数组格式（需用[]包裹多个指令）");
    }
  } catch (e) {
    this.errorCommands.push(`JSON解析失败：${e.message.slice(0, 50)}（请检查引号、逗号是否为英文）`);
    console.error('[解析JSON Patch指令失败]：', e);
  }

  // 返回：指令数组（供处理）+ 格式化文本（供编辑）
  return { patchCommands, formattedPatchText };
},

// 新增工具函数：将JSON Patch的斜杠路径转换为点分隔的路径
// 示例：/当前时间纪元 → 当前时间纪元；/封印物列表/XXX/描述 → 封印物列表.XXX.描述
_convertJsonPatchPathToDotPath(jsonPatchPath) {
  if (!jsonPatchPath) return '';
  return jsonPatchPath.startsWith('/')
    ? jsonPatchPath.slice(1).replace(/\//g, '.')
    : jsonPatchPath;
},

 async _applyUpdateFallback(script, currentMvuState) { // 改为async，处理路径提取
  console.log('[_applyUpdateFallback] 函数已触发！script长度:', script.length);
  if (!script || !currentMvuState) return null;

  const newState = _.cloneDeep(currentMvuState);
  let modified = false; // 只要有一条正确指令生效，就为true
  this.errorCommands = [];
  // 原有代码：提取_.xxx指令，现因使用外置脚本，进行注释
  //const commands = this._extractCommands(script);

  // 解析JSON Patch指令
  const { patchCommands, formattedPatchText } = this._processJsonPatchCommandsEnhanced(script);
  console.log('[解析结果] 合法指令数:', patchCommands.length, '指令列表:', { patchCommands, formattedPatchText });
  console.log('[_applyUpdateFallback] 解析到的指令数量:', patchCommands.length);


  // 定义数值限制规则（字段名匹配+上下限）
  const valueLimitRules = {
    好感度: { min: -200, max: 200 },    // 好感度±200
    消化进度: { min: 0, max: 100 },     // 消化进度0-100
    失控进度: { min: 0, max: 100 }      // 失控进度0-100
  };

  const locationDefaults = {
    "当前区域": "未知",
    "当前地标": "未知",
    "当前坐标": { x: 50.0, y: 50.0 }
  };
  // 晋升体系的默认值
  const promotionSystemDefault = "魔药";
  // 步骤1：初始化默认值（仅补缺失，不覆盖已有值）
  const initLocationKeys = (statData) => {
    if (statData["晋升体系"] === undefined) {
      statData["晋升体系"] = promotionSystemDefault;
      console.log(`初始化「晋升体系」，默认值：${promotionSystemDefault}`);
      modified = true;
    }

    for (const key in locationDefaults) {
      if (statData[key] === undefined) {
        statData[key] = locationDefaults[key];
        console.log(`初始化地址键「${key}」，默认值：${JSON.stringify(locationDefaults[key])}`);
        modified = true;
      }
    }
    return statData;
  };

  // 1.1 合法区域列表（从地图系统获取，确保区域有效性）
  const validRegions = mapSystem?.DEFAULT_LOCATIONS?.mainRegions?.map(r => r.name) || [
  "因蒂斯共和国",
  "鲁恩王国",
  "弗萨克帝国",
  "费内波特王国",
  "狂暴海",
  "苏尼亚海",
  "西拜朗",
  "东拜朗",
  "伦堡",
  "迷雾海",
  "极地海",
  "北海",
  "神弃之地",
  "西大陆"
];
  // 1.2 坐标范围限制
  const coordinateRule = { min: 0, max: 100 };

newState.stat_data = initLocationKeys(newState.stat_data);

// 【关键1：动态提取合法顶层路径（从newState.stat_data获取，与InitVar一致）】
// 排除元数据$meta，其余顶层键均为合法路径（如“武器”“非凡特性列表”等）
const legalTopPaths = Object.keys(newState.stat_data).filter(key => key !== '$meta');
//console.log('[合法顶层路径]', legalTopPaths);


// 辅助函数：仅做数值限制和坐标格式校验，
  const getLimitedValue = (path, value) => {
    const fieldName = path.split('.').pop();
    // 1. 数值字段限制
    const rule = valueLimitRules[fieldName];
    if (rule && typeof value === 'number' && !isNaN(value)) {
      const limitedValue = Math.max(rule.min, Math.min(rule.max, value));
      if (limitedValue !== value) {
        console.log(`[数值限制] ${fieldName}超出范围(${value})，已修正为${limitedValue}`);
      }
      return limitedValue;
    }

    // 2. 坐标仅做格式和0-100范围校验
    if (fieldName === "当前坐标" && typeof value === "object" && value.x !== undefined && value.y !== undefined) {

      const validX = Math.max(coordinateRule.min, Math.min(coordinateRule.max, value.x));
      const validY = Math.max(coordinateRule.min, Math.min(coordinateRule.max, value.y));
      const tempPoint = { x: validX, y: validY };

      return tempPoint;
    }

    // 坐标格式异常 → 用默认值
    if (fieldName === "当前坐标") {
      console.log(`[坐标容错] 格式异常，使用默认未知坐标`);
      return locationDefaults["当前坐标"];
    }

    return value;
  };

  // 联动地标：根据坐标自动匹配最近地标
  const syncLandmarkByCoord = (coord) => {
    const landmarks = mapSystem?.DEFAULT_LOCATIONS?.landmarks || [];
    if (!landmarks.length) return locationDefaults["当前地标"];
    // 计算当前坐标到每个地标的距离
    let nearestLandmark = locationDefaults["当前地标"];
    let minDistance = Infinity;
    landmarks.forEach(landmark => {
      // 解析地标百分比坐标
      const landmarkX = parseFloat(landmark.marker.left);
      const landmarkY = parseFloat(landmark.marker.top) * this.Y_SCALE;// 地标Y缩放

      // 玩家坐标Y缩放（与区域判断逻辑一致）
      const userX = coord.x;
      const userY = coord.y;

      // 计算欧氏距离
      const distance = Math.sqrt(Math.pow(userX - landmarkX, 2) + Math.pow(userY - landmarkY, 2));
      console.log(`玩家坐标: (${userX}, ${userY}), 地标${landmark.name}坐标: (${landmarkX}, ${landmarkY}), 距离: ${distance}`);
      if (distance < minDistance) {
        minDistance = distance;
        nearestLandmark = landmark.name;
      }
    });
    // 距离过远则仍为未知
    return minDistance < 5 ? nearestLandmark : locationDefaults["当前地标"];
  };

  // 辅助：获取所有合法地标名称（用于判定地标是否合法）
  const getValidLandmarkNames = () => {
    return mapSystem?.DEFAULT_LOCATIONS?.landmarks?.map(landmark => landmark.name) || [];
  };

  // 辅助：判定是否为异世界（区域不合法 + 地标不合法）
  const isAnotherWorld = (region, landmark) => {
    const validLands = getValidLandmarkNames();
    // 区域不在合法列表，且地标不在合法列表 → 异世界
    return !validRegions.includes(region) && !validLands.includes(landmark);
  };

  // 辅助：按地标名称获取其所属区域（优先用mainRegionName）
  const getRegionByLandmark = (landmarkName) => {
    if (!mapSystem) return null;
    const landmark = mapSystem?.DEFAULT_LOCATIONS?.landmarks?.find(l => l.name === landmarkName);
    if (landmark && landmark.mainRegionName) {
      // 直接返回地标关联的区域（权威数据）
      return mapSystem?.DEFAULT_LOCATIONS?.mainRegions?.find(r => r.name === landmark.mainRegionName);
    }
    return null;
  };

  // 辅助：按坐标匹配所属区域（新增，用于极端情况兜底）
  const getRegionByCoord = (coord) => {
    if (!mapSystem) return null;
    return mapSystem?.DEFAULT_LOCATIONS?.mainRegions?.find(region => {
      const polygon = region?.points?.outer?.map(p => ({ x: p.x, y: p.y }));
      return polygon.length && GeometryHelper.isPointInPolygon(coord, polygon);
    });
  };

  // 辅助：计算区域中心坐标（补充遗漏的关键函数）
  const getRegionCenter = (region) => {
    const points = region?.points?.outer || [];
    if (!points.length) return locationDefaults["当前坐标"];

    const xList = points.map(p => p.x);
    const yList = points.map(p => p.y);
    const centerX = (Math.min(...xList) + Math.max(...xList)) / 2;
    const centerY = (Math.min(...yList) + Math.max(...yList)) / 2;
    return { x: centerX, y: centerY };
  };




  console.log('[_applyUpdateFallback] 解析到的指令数量:', patchCommands.length);
  if (patchCommands.length > 0) console.log('[_applyUpdateFallback] 第一条指令:', patchCommands[0]);

  // 步骤2：执行AI指令,遍历每个JSON Patch指令，逐个处理
  for (const patch of patchCommands) {
    let skip = false;
    try {
      const { op, path: jsonPath, value } = patch;
      // 路径转换：JSON Patch的/路径 → 原代码的.路径（如/当前区域 → 当前区域，/人物关系列表.小红 → 人物关系列表.小红）
      const localPath = this._convertJsonPatchPathToDotPath(jsonPath); // 使用工具函数
      // 提取顶层路径（原代码的topPath，用于校验）
      const topPath = localPath.split('.')[0];

      switch (op) {
        //  1. replace指令：对应原set指令 + 兼容原add（数值增减）指令校验顶层路径+设置结果
        case 'replace':
          if (!localPath) {
            this.errorCommands.push(`指令 replace("${jsonPath}")：路径不能为空`);
            break;
          }

          let setVal = value;
          let isIncrement = false;
          let delta = 0;
          // 情况1：value是字符串（如"+10"、"-5"），且字段是数值类型
          if (typeof setVal === 'string' && (setVal.startsWith('+') || setVal.startsWith('-'))) {
            const fieldName = localPath.split('.').pop();
            if (valueLimitRules[fieldName]) { // 仅对有数值限制的字段生效
              delta = Number(setVal);
              if (!isNaN(delta)) {
                isIncrement = true;
                // 获取原值，计算增量后的值
                const currentVal = _.get(newState.stat_data, localPath, 0);
                setVal = currentVal + delta;
                // 数值限制
                setVal = getLimitedValue(localPath, setVal);
              }
            }
          }
          // 情况2：普通值，执行数值限制
          else {
            setVal = getLimitedValue(localPath, setVal);
          }

          // 校验1：顶层路径是否合法
          if (!legalTopPaths.includes(topPath)) {
            this.errorCommands.push(`指令 replace("${jsonPath}", "${JSON.stringify(setVal)}")：非法顶层路径「${topPath}」`);
            break;
          }

          console.log(`[replace指令] 处理后路径: ${localPath}，类型: ${typeof localPath}，目标键:`, newState.stat_data[localPath]);
          const setResult = this.setNestedValue(newState.stat_data, localPath, setVal);
          if (!setResult.success) {
            this.errorCommands.push(`指令 replace("${jsonPath}", "${JSON.stringify(setVal)}")：${setResult.error}`);
            break;
          }

          const setResultValue = _.get(newState.stat_data, localPath);

          // 实时获取当前区域、地标、坐标（用于判定世界类型）
          const currentRegion = newState.stat_data["当前区域"];
          const currentLandmark = newState.stat_data["当前地标"];
          const currentCoord = newState.stat_data["当前坐标"];
          const anotherWorld = isAnotherWorld(currentRegion, currentLandmark); // 异世界判定

          // 场景1：设置「当前区域」
          if (localPath === "当前区域") {
            if (anotherWorld) {
              // 异世界：不修正任何值，保留原始设置
              console.log(`[异世界] 区域设置为${setVal}，不处理坐标和地标`);
              modified = true;
              break;
            }

            // 正常世界：区域合法或地标合法
            const targetRegion = mapSystem?.DEFAULT_LOCATIONS?.mainRegions?.find(r => r.name === setVal);
            if (targetRegion) {
              // 坐标不在区域内 → 修正坐标到边缘（但保留地标，无论地标是否在列表中）
              if (!GeometryHelper.isPointInPolygon(currentCoord, targetRegion.points.outer.map(p => ({ x: p.x, y: p.y })))) {
                const clampedPoint = GeometryHelper.getClampedPointToPolygon(currentCoord, targetRegion.points.outer.map(p => ({ x: p.x, y: p.y })));
                newState.stat_data["当前坐标"] = clampedPoint;
                console.log(`[正常世界] 坐标出界，修正到${setVal}边缘：${JSON.stringify(clampedPoint)}`);
              }
              // 强制保留地标（不校验地标是否在列表，支持未录入的合法地标）
              console.log(`[正常世界] 区域更新为${setVal}，保留地标：${currentLandmark}`);
            }
            modified = true;
            break;
          }

          // 场景2：设置「当前坐标」
          if (localPath === "当前坐标") {
            if (anotherWorld) {
              // 异世界：不修正坐标，不联动地标
              console.log(`[异世界] 坐标设置为${JSON.stringify(setVal)}，不处理区域和地标`);
              modified = true;
              break;
            }

            // 正常世界：区域合法或地标合法
            const targetRegion = currentRegion && mapSystem?.DEFAULT_LOCATIONS?.mainRegions?.find(r => r.name === currentRegion);
            if (targetRegion) {
              // 坐标不在区域内 → 修正坐标到边缘（保留地标）
              if (!GeometryHelper.isPointInPolygon(setVal, targetRegion.points.outer.map(p => ({ x: p.x, y: p.y })))) {
                setVal = GeometryHelper.getClampedPointToPolygon(setVal, targetRegion.points.outer.map(p => ({ x: p.x, y: p.y })));
                this.setNestedValue(newState.stat_data, localPath, setVal); // 应用修正后的坐标
                console.log(`[正常世界] 坐标出界，修正到${currentRegion}边缘：${JSON.stringify(setVal)}`);
              }
              // 强制保留地标（不校验是否在列表）
              console.log(`[正常世界] 坐标更新，保留地标：${currentLandmark}`);
            } else {
              // 区域不合法但地标合法（正常世界）→ 按地标补区域
              if (currentLandmark) {
                const regionByLandmark = getRegionByLandmark(currentLandmark);
                if (regionByLandmark) {
                  newState.stat_data["当前区域"] = regionByLandmark.name;
                  console.log(`[正常世界] 地标${currentLandmark}关联区域${regionByLandmark.name}，补全区域`);
                }
              }

              // 若地标也无关联区域，才降级用坐标补（极端情况兜底）
              else {
                const regionByCoord = getRegionByCoord(setVal);
                if (regionByCoord) {
                  newState.stat_data["当前区域"] = regionByCoord.name;
                  console.log(`[正常世界] 地标无关联区域，按坐标补全区域：${regionByCoord.name}`);
                }
              }
            }
            modified = true;
            break;
          }

          // 场景3：设置「当前地标」
          if (localPath === "当前地标") {
            if (anotherWorld) {
              // 异世界：保留地标，不处理区域和坐标
              console.log(`[异世界] 地标设置为${setVal}，不处理区域和坐标`);
              modified = true;
              break;
            }

            // 正常世界：保留地标（无论是否在列表中）
            console.log(`[正常世界] 地标更新为${setVal}，保留区域：${currentRegion}`);
            modified = true;
            break;
          }

          // 其他字段处理（非区域/坐标/地标）

          if (isIncrement) {
            // 数值增减的日志（匹配原add指令的日志）
            console.log(`[replace指令后(增减)] ${localPath}=${setVal - delta} + ${delta} = ${setVal}`);
          } else {
            // 普通替换的日志（匹配原set指令的日志）
            console.log(`[replace指令后] ${localPath}=${JSON.stringify(setVal)}，实际值:`, setResult);
          }

          modified = true;
          break;

        // 2. add指令：校验顶层路径+数字合法性，JSON Patch标准语义（新增键/元素）→ 对应原代码的assign/insert指令
        case 'add':
          if (!localPath) {
            this.errorCommands.push(`指令 add("${jsonPath}")：路径不能为空`);
            break;
          }

          // 校验1：顶层路径是否合法
          if (!legalTopPaths.includes(topPath)) {
            this.errorCommands.push(`指令 add("${jsonPath}", "${JSON.stringify(value)}")：非法顶层路径「${topPath}」`);
            break;
          }

          const addValue = getLimitedValue(localPath, value);
          const addResult = this.setNestedValue(newState.stat_data, localPath, addValue);
          if (!addResult.success) {
            this.errorCommands.push(`指令 add("${jsonPath}", "${JSON.stringify(addValue)}")：${addResult.error}`);
            break;
          }

          console.log(`[add指令（新增）后] ${localPath} = ${JSON.stringify(addValue)}`);
          modified = true;
          break;

        // 3. remove指令：保留原有校验+叠加顶层路径校验，JSON Patch标准语义 → 对应原代码的remove指令
        case 'remove':
          const removePath = localPath;
          if (!jsonPath) { // jsonPath是原始的/路径，比如"/武器列表/剑"
            this.errorCommands.push(`指令 ${op}(...)：参数不足（需路径）`);
            break;
          }
          // 额外补充：校验localPath（转换后的.路径）是否非空（兜底）
          if (!removePath) {
            this.errorCommands.push(`指令 ${op}("${jsonPath}")：路径不能为空`);
            break;
          }

          // 校验路径是否含“.”（精确到条目）
          if (!removePath.includes(".")) {
            this.errorCommands.push(`指令 remove("${jsonPath}")：路径需含“列表.条目”（如“非凡特性列表.条目1”）`);
            break;
          }

          // 校验顶层路径合法性
          if (!legalTopPaths.includes(topPath)) {
            this.errorCommands.push(`指令 remove("${jsonPath}")：非法顶层路径「${topPath}」`);
            break;
          }

          // 校验路径是否存在
          if (!_.has(newState.stat_data, removePath)) {
            this.errorCommands.push(`指令 remove("${jsonPath}")：路径不存在`);
            break;
          }

          // 执行删除操作
          _.unset(newState.stat_data, removePath);
          console.log(`[remove指令后] 已删除路径: ${removePath}`);
          modified = true;
          break;


        // 未识别指令
        default:
          this.errorCommands.push(`指令 ${op}("${jsonPath}")：未识别指令（仅支持replace/add/remove）`);
          break;
      }
    } catch (e) {
      // 捕获意外异常（如路径格式错误等）
      const op = patch?.op || '未知';
      const jsonPath = patch?.path || '未知';
      this.errorCommands.push(`指令 ${op}("${jsonPath}")：执行失败（${e.message.slice(0, 30)}）`);
    }
    if (skip) continue;
  }

   // 最终兜底：区分正常世界和异世界
  const finalRegion = newState.stat_data["当前区域"];
  const finalLandmark = newState.stat_data["当前地标"];
  const finalCoord = newState.stat_data["当前坐标"];
  const finalAnotherWorld = isAnotherWorld(finalRegion, finalLandmark);

  if (!mapSystem) {
    // mapSystem为null时，仅做基础兜底，不执行联动逻辑
    console.warn('[最终兜底] mapSystem未初始化，仅保留基础数据');
    if (finalRegion === undefined) newState.stat_data["当前区域"] = "未知";
    if (finalLandmark === undefined) newState.stat_data["当前地标"] = "未知";
    if (finalCoord === undefined) newState.stat_data["当前坐标"] = locationDefaults["当前坐标"];
  } else if (finalAnotherWorld) {
    // 异世界：仅补全未设置的字段
    if (finalRegion === undefined) newState.stat_data["当前区域"] = "未知";
    if (finalLandmark === undefined) newState.stat_data["当前地标"] = "未知";
    if (finalCoord === undefined) newState.stat_data["当前坐标"] = locationDefaults["当前坐标"];
    console.log(`[异世界兜底] 保留原始数据：区域=${finalRegion || "未知"}, 地标=${finalLandmark || "未知"}`);
  } else {
    // 正常世界：确保区域/坐标合理，保留地标
    // 1. 按地标补区域（优先）
    if ((!finalRegion || !validRegions.includes(finalRegion)) && finalLandmark) {
      const regionByLandmark = getRegionByLandmark(finalLandmark);
      if (regionByLandmark) {
        newState.stat_data["当前区域"] = regionByLandmark.name;
        console.log(`[正常世界兜底] 按地标${finalLandmark}补全区域：${regionByLandmark.name}`);
      }
    }

    // 2. 坐标非法时修正到区域中心
    const targetRegion = finalRegion && mapSystem.DEFAULT_LOCATIONS.mainRegions.find(r => r.name === finalRegion);
    if (targetRegion) {
      if (finalCoord.x < coordinateRule.min || finalCoord.x > coordinateRule.max ||
          finalCoord.y < coordinateRule.min || finalCoord.y > coordinateRule.max) {
        const centerCoord = getRegionCenter(targetRegion);
        newState.stat_data["当前坐标"] = centerCoord;
        console.log(`[正常世界兜底] 坐标非法，修正到${finalRegion}中心：${JSON.stringify(centerCoord)}`);
      }
    }

    // 3. 无坐标时用区域中心
    if (!finalCoord) {
      const centerCoord = targetRegion ? getRegionCenter(targetRegion) : locationDefaults["当前坐标"];
      newState.stat_data["当前坐标"] = centerCoord;
      console.log(`[正常世界兜底] 无坐标，使用${finalRegion || "默认"}中心坐标`);
    }
  }

  if (modified) {
    const finalValidateResult = this._validateWithZodSchema(newState.stat_data);
    if (!finalValidateResult.valid) {
      // 将全局错误添加到错误列表，仅提示不回滚
      this.errorCommands.push(`全局校验提示：${finalValidateResult.error}`);
    }
    // 若需要，可使用zod修正后的全局数据（可选）
    // newState.stat_data = finalValidateResult.validatedData || newState.stat_data;
    // 强制应用Zod修正后的数据（实现转换和限制）
    if (finalValidateResult.validatedData) {
      newState.stat_data = finalValidateResult.validatedData;
    }
  }

  // 同步地图
  if (modified && mapSystem && mapSystem.updateStatData) {
    mapSystem.updateStatData(newState.stat_data);
  }



  console.log('[_applyUpdateFallback] 执行完毕：modified=', modified, '错误指令数:', this.errorCommands.length);
  // 批量弹出提示（错误数>0时）
  if (this.errorCommands.length > 0) {
    const errorText = `克莱恩提示：AI流口水了，${this.errorCommands.length}条指令失效！\n` +
      this.errorCommands.slice(0, 5).join("\n") +
      (this.errorCommands.length > 5 ? `\n...等${this.errorCommands.length - 5}条` : "") +
      "\n建议：在变量面板中修正错误后重新应用～";
    this.showTemporaryMessage(errorText, 8000);

  }

  if (modified && mapSystem && mapSystem.updateStatData) {
    mapSystem.updateStatData(newState.stat_data);
  }

  /* 新增：同步到全局消息状态（关键）
  if (modified) {
    (async () => {
      const messages = await getChatMessages('0');
      if (messages?.[0]) {
        messages[0].data = _.cloneDeep(newState);
        await TavernHelper.setChatMessages([messages[0]], { refresh: 'force' });
      }
    })();
  }*/

  return modified ? newState : null;
},


_trimQuotes(str) {
  return typeof str === "string" ? str.replace(/^['"`\s]+|['"`\s]+$/g, "") : str;
},

          // 统一格式修复函数（英文键替换+缺键互补+JSON补全）
 _fixFormat(keyOrPath, entryName, valueObj) {
  // 1. 英文键→中文键映射（覆盖所有规则字段，无遗漏）
  const enToCnMap = {
 name: "名称", type: "类型", description: "描述", sequence: "序列", rarity: "等阶",
 baseSpiritBonus: "基础灵性加成", baseSanityBonus: "基础理智加成", baseHumanityBonus: "基础人性加成",
 baseAgilityBonus: "基础敏捷加成", baseLuckBonus: "基础运气加成",
 playMethodName: "名称", playType: "类型", percentBonus: "百分比加成", allAttributes: "全部属性",
 negativeEffect: "负面效果", count: "数量", unit: "单位",
 favorability: "好感度", relationship: "关系", eventHistory: "事件历史", heldItems: "持有物品",
 addressToUser: "对玩家称呼", currentSequence: "当前序列",
 gender: "性别", divinity: "神性", promotionSystem: "晋升体系", digestionProgress: "消化进度", madnessProgress: "失控进度",
 mainPlayMethod: "主要扮演法", auxiliaryAbility: "辅助能力", weapon: "武器", clothes: "衣物",
 accessory: "饰品", sealedItem: "封印物", baseVitality: "基础活力", baseSpirit: "基础灵性",
 baseSanity: "基础理智", baseHumanity: "基础人性", baseAgility: "基础敏捷", baseLuck: "基础运气",
 spirit: "灵性", currentSpirit: "当前灵性", sanity: "理智", currentSanity: "当前理智",
 humanity: "人性", currentHumanity: "当前人性", agility: "敏捷", currentAgility: "当前敏捷",
 luck: "运气", extraordinaryTraitList: "非凡特性列表", currentStatus: "当前状态",
 playMethodList: "扮演法列表", weaponList: "武器列表", clothesList: "衣物列表",
 accessoryList: "饰品列表", sealedItemList: "封印物列表", consumableList: "消耗品列表",
 otherList: "其他列表", characterRelationshipList: "人物关系列表", faction: "阵营",
 currentCycle: "当前周目", currentTimeEra: "当前时间纪元", sourceCastleSpace: "源堡空间",
 currentCycleSourceCastleChoice: "本周目源堡选择", spiritAggregation: "灵性聚合度",
 soulAge: "灵魂年龄", soulAgeLimit: "灵魂年龄上限", bodyAge: "身体年龄", bodyAgeLimit: "身体年龄上限"
 };
  // 递归替换对象英文键
  const replaceEnKeys = (obj) => {
    if (!_.isObject(obj) || Array.isArray(obj)) return obj;
    const fixedObj = {};
    Object.entries(obj).forEach(([key, val]) => {
      const cnKey = enToCnMap[key] || key;
      fixedObj[cnKey] = _.isObject(val) ? replaceEnKeys(val) : val;
    });
    return fixedObj;
  };
  const fixedValue = replaceEnKeys(valueObj);

  // 2. 缺键互补（名称↔键值互相复用）
  if (fixedValue && !fixedValue["名称"] && entryName) {
    fixedValue["名称"] = entryName; // 缺“名称”键，用条目名称补
  }
  if (!entryName && fixedValue && fixedValue["名称"]) {
    entryName = fixedValue["名称"]; // 缺条目名称，用“名称”键补
  }

  // 3. 补全必填默认值（避免undefined，提升玩家体验）
  if (fixedValue && (keyOrPath.includes("消耗品列表") || keyOrPath.includes("其他列表"))) {
  // 仅当“数量”字段不存在时补默认值（AI可能设置为0，此时不覆盖）
  if (fixedValue["数量"] === undefined) fixedValue["数量"] = 1;
  // 仅当“单位”字段不存在时补默认值
  if (fixedValue["单位"] === undefined) fixedValue["单位"] = "个";
}
/* if (fixedValue &&
    fixedValue["类型"] === undefined &&
    !keyOrPath.includes("非凡特性列表") && // 排除天赋列表
    !keyOrPath.includes("序列能力列表")      // 可选：排除序列能力列表
) {
  fixedValue["类型"] = "未知类型"; // 仅缺失时补，且不影响天赋
}*/

  return { fixedEntryName: entryName, fixedValue };
},
 _parseCommandValue(valStr) {
  if (typeof valStr !== "string") return valStr;
  const isFromUpdateVar = valStr.startsWith('__UPDATE_VAR__');
  const trimmed = isFromUpdateVar ? valStr.replace('__UPDATE_VAR__', '').trim() : valStr.trim();
  // 快速处理基础类型
  if (trimmed === "true") return true;
  if (trimmed === "false") return false;
  if (trimmed === "null") return undefined;

  // 格式修复1：补全中文键引号（如 {名称:"金镑"} → {"名称":"金镑"}）
  let fixedVal = trimmed;
  if (isFromUpdateVar && trimmed.startsWith("{") && trimmed.endsWith("}")) {
    // 无捕获组修复（仅处理中文键，不碰正文）
    fixedVal = trimmed.replace(
      /([\u4e00-\u9fa5]+)(\s*:)/g,
      '\u0022\u00241\u0022\u00242' // 安全替换，只给中文键加引号
    );
  }

  // 尝试JSON解析（优先）
  try {
    if ((fixedVal.startsWith("{") && fixedVal.endsWith("}")) || (fixedVal.startsWith("[") && fixedVal.endsWith("]"))) {
      return JSON.parse(fixedVal);
    }
  } catch (e) {}

  // 备用：处理非标准对象字面量（无冗余日志）
  try {
    return new Function(`return ${fixedVal}`)();
  } catch (e) {}

  // 保底：纯字符串（去引号）
  return this._trimQuotes(valStr);
},


          _getDisplayText(aiResponse) {
            try {
              if (!aiResponse || typeof aiResponse !== 'string') return '';

              // 优先策略：寻找 <gametxt> 标签
              const gameText = this._extractLastTagContent('gametxt', aiResponse);
              if (gameText !== null) {
                  return gameText
                      .replace(new RegExp('<!--[\\s\\S]*?-->', 'g'), '') // 第一步：移除 注释
                      .replace(/<safe>[\s\S]*?<\/safe>/g, '')       // 第二步：移除 <safe>...</safe> 及其内容
                      .trim();
              }

              // 备用策略：如果找不到 <gametxt>，则清理所有已知标签，并保留剩余的纯文本
              let cleanedText = aiResponse;
              const tagsToRemove = ['本周目经历', '历史的投影', 'UpdateVariable', '角色提取', 'thinking', 'gametxt', 'dm']; // 也把gametxt加入清理列表，防止空标签残留

              tagsToRemove.forEach(tag => {
                  const regexWithContent = new RegExp(`<${tag}>[\s\S]*?<\/${tag}>`, 'gi');
                  cleanedText = cleanedText.replace(regexWithContent, '');
                  const regexSelfClosing = new RegExp(`<${tag}\s*\/>`, 'gi');
                  cleanedText = cleanedText.replace(regexSelfClosing, '');
              });

              // 最终清理：移除所有残余的、可能是HTML/XML的标签，例如 <p>, <div> 等
              cleanedText = cleanedText.replace(/<[^>]*>/g, '');

              // 如果清理后有实质内容，就返回它
              if (cleanedText.trim() !== '') {
                  return cleanedText.trim();
              }

              // 保底策略：如果以上方法都失败（例如，回复只包含标签而无任何其他文本），
              // 就返回空字符串，避免显示残留的标签或“摘要解析失败”。
              return '';

            } catch (e) {
              console.error("解析显示文本时出错:", e, "原始输入:", aiResponse);
              return "[摘要解析失败]";
            }
          },

            _extractLastTagContent(tagName, text, ignoreCase = false) {
              if (!text || typeof text !== 'string') return null;
              const endTag = `</${tagName}>`;
              let searchPool = text, endTagPattern = endTag;
              if (ignoreCase) { searchPool = text.toLowerCase(); endTagPattern = endTag.toLowerCase(); }
              const lastEndIndex = searchPool.lastIndexOf(endTagPattern);
              if (lastEndIndex !== -1) {
                  const startTag = `<${tagName}>`;
                  let startTagPattern = startTag;
                  if (ignoreCase) startTagPattern = startTag.toLowerCase();
                  const lastStartIndex = searchPool.lastIndexOf(startTagPattern, lastEndIndex);
                  if (lastStartIndex !== -1) {
                      return text.substring(lastStartIndex + startTag.length, lastEndIndex).trim();
                  }
              }
              return null;
            },
            _extractAllTags(tagName, text) {
              if (!text || typeof text !== 'string') return [];
              const matches = [...text.matchAll(new RegExp(`<${tagName}>\\s*([\\s\\S]*?)\\s*<\\/${tagName}>`, 'gi'))];
              return matches.map(m => (m[1] ?? '').trim()).filter(Boolean);
            },

    // --- 新增：AI回复格式验证函数 ---
    validateAiResponseFormat(responseText) {
    const errors = [];
    const criticalTags = ['gametxt', 'UpdateVariable', 'action', '本周目经历', '历史的投影']; // 定义所有需要严格闭合的标签
    const requiredTags = ['gametxt', '本周目经历']; // 必须存在的标签

    for (const tag of criticalTags) {
        const openTag = `<${tag}>`;
        const closeTag = `</${tag}>`;

        const openTagCount = (responseText.match(new RegExp(openTag, 'g')) || []).length;
        const closeTagCount = (responseText.match(new RegExp(closeTag, 'g')) || []).length;

        if (openTagCount > 0 || closeTagCount > 0) { // 只要出现了其中一个，就必须成对
            if (openTagCount !== closeTagCount) {
                errors.push(`标签 <${tag}> 未正确闭合 (开始标签: ${openTagCount}个, 结束标签: ${closeTagCount}个)。`);
            }
        }
    }

    // 检查必须存在的标签
    for (const tag of requiredTags) {
        const tagRegex = new RegExp(`<${tag}>[\\s\\S]*?</${tag}>`, 'i');
        if (!tagRegex.test(responseText)) {
            errors.push(`回复中缺少必需的 <${tag}> 标签。`);
        }
    }

    return {
        isValid: errors.length === 0,
        errorMessages: errors
    };
},

      _autoFixTags(text) {
            let fixedText = text;
            const tags = ['gametxt', 'UpdateVariable', 'action', '本周目经历', '历史的投影', 'thinking', 'CharacterCard', '本周目核心记忆', '当前线索'];

            for (const tag of tags) {
                const openTagRegex = new RegExp(`<${tag}(\s+[^>]*)?>`, 'gi');
                const closeTagRegex = new RegExp(`</${tag}>`, 'gi');

                const openMatches = [...fixedText.matchAll(openTagRegex)];
                const closeMatches = [...fixedText.matchAll(closeTagRegex)];

                if (openMatches.length > closeMatches.length) {
