                    console.log(`[自动修复] 检测到标签 <${tag}> 未闭合。正在尝试修复...`);

                    const lastOpenTag = openMatches[openMatches.length - 1];
                    const startIndex = lastOpenTag.index + lastOpenTag[0].length;

                    const nextTagMatch = fixedText.substring(startIndex).match(/<\/?\w+[^>]*>/);
                    let insertPosition = fixedText.length;

                    if (nextTagMatch && nextTagMatch.index !== undefined) {
                        insertPosition = startIndex + nextTagMatch.index;
                    }

                    fixedText = fixedText.slice(0, insertPosition).trim() + `</${tag}>\n` + fixedText.slice(insertPosition);
                }
            }
            return fixedText;
        },
              async _finalizeTurn(textToSave) {
    try {
        // 1. 生成统一结构的快照（包含equipped_items和完整gacha_data）
        const newSnapshot = {
            message_id: `frontend-hist-${Date.now()}`,
            message: textToSave,
            is_user: false,
            role: 'assistant',
            data: {
                ..._.cloneDeep(this.currentMvuState),
                equipped_items: _.cloneDeep(this.equippedItems), // 统一补充装备数据
                gacha_data: { // 统一补充完整Gacha数据（状态+收藏+历史）
                    state: _.cloneDeep(this.gachaState),
                    collection: _.cloneDeep(this.gachaCollection),
                    history: _.cloneDeep(this.gachaHistory)
                },
            },
            timestamp: Date.now()
        };

        // 2. 加入缓存，统一限制50条（超出则删除最旧快照）
        this.chatHistoryCache.push(newSnapshot);
        //if (this.chatHistoryCache.length > 50) {
        //    this.chatHistoryCache.shift(); // 删除最旧的1条
        //    console.log('[历史系统] 快照数量超出50条，已删除最旧记录');
        //}

        // 3. 校验快照完整性（调试用，可保留）
        const latestSnapshot = this.chatHistoryCache[this.chatHistoryCache.length - 1];
        console.log('[新回合快照校验] 快照data结构:', latestSnapshot?.data);
        console.log('[新回合快照校验] 包含stat_data:', !!latestSnapshot?.data?.stat_data);
        console.log('[新回合快照校验] 包含gacha收藏:', !!latestSnapshot?.data?.gacha_data?.collection);

        // 4. 保存到本地存储（仅1次，无重复）
        await AppStorage.saveData(this._getHistoryKey(), this.chatHistoryCache);
        this.historyViewIndex = this.chatHistoryCache.length - 1;
        this.renderHistoryControls();
        console.log(`[历史系统] 新回合快照已保存，当前总数: ${this.chatHistoryCache.length}`);

        // 5. 收尾工作（保留）
        this.hideWaitingMessage();
        this.isBusy = false;

    } catch(e) {
        // 保存失败时回滚：移除刚加入的快照，避免内存与本地缓存不一致
        if (this.chatHistoryCache.length > 0) {
            this.chatHistoryCache.pop();
            console.log('[历史系统] 保存失败，已回滚快照');
        }
        console.error('[历史系统] 保存新回合快照失败:', e);
        this.hideWaitingMessage();
        this.isBusy = false;
    }
},
          // ===============================================
          // 新增和修正的存档/读档功能
          // ===============================================
          async getSavesFromStorage() {
            return await AppStorage.loadData('multi_save_data', {});
          },

    async  showSaveLoadManager(saves = null) {
    this.openModal('save-load-modal');
    const modalHeader = document.querySelector('#save-load-modal .modal-header');
    const modalBody = document.querySelector('#save-load-modal .modal-body');
    if (!modalHeader || !modalBody) return;

    modalBody.innerHTML = `
        <div class="chronicle-container">
            <div class="chronicle-toc">
                <div class="chronicle-header">时光手记 · 目录</div>
                <div id="chronicle-toc-list"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="chronicle-page">
                <div id="chronicle-page-header" class="chronicle-header">事件详情</div>
                <div id="chronicle-page-content" class="empty-placeholder">请从左侧目录选择一条时间线</div>
            </div>
        </div>
    `;

    const headerActions = modalHeader.querySelector('div');
    if (headerActions && !document.getElementById('btn-new-timeline')) {
        headerActions.insertAdjacentHTML('afterbegin', `<button id="btn-new-timeline" data-action="new_timeline" class="interaction-btn" style="background: #004d40;" title="在当前聊天中清除所有历史和状态，开始一次全新的游戏。">开启新周目</button>`);
    }
    if (headerActions && !document.getElementById('btn-rollback')) {
        headerActions.insertAdjacentHTML('afterbegin', `<button id="btn-reroll" data-action="reroll" class="interaction-btn header-action-btn" title="重新生成AI回答">🎲</button><button id="btn-rollback" data-action="rollback" class="interaction-btn header-action-btn" title="回溯至上一回合">⏳</button>`);
    }

    const tocList = document.getElementById('chronicle-toc-list');
    let html = '';

    // 1. 渲染“当前时间线”
    html += this.renderChronicleChapter(this.chatHistoryCache, 'current_timeline');

    // 2. 渲染已归档的分支
    const savesToRender = saves || await this.getSavesFromStorage();
    const manualSaveKeys = Object.keys(savesToRender).filter(key => key.startsWith('slot_')).sort((a, b) => b.localeCompare(a));
    manualSaveKeys.forEach(slotId => {
        html += this.renderChronicleChapter(savesToRender[slotId], slotId);
    });

    // 3. 渲染定期自动备份
    html += await this.renderPeriodicBackupChapter();

    tocList.innerHTML = html;
    this.bindChronicleListeners();
    this.bindPeriodicBackupListeners(); // 绑定定期备份加载按钮事件
},


async startNewTimeline() {
  this.showCustomConfirm(
    '【高危操作】您确定要开启新周目吗？<br><br>这将彻底清除所有历史记录、Gacha数据、装备和世界书进度，回到初始状态！',
    async () => {
      this.showTemporaryMessage('正在重置世界线...', 3000);
      try {
        // 1. 清空所有游戏相关缓存（同步操作，确保先执行）
        const namespace = 'SEFIROT_CASTLE_REVISION_';
        const keysToRemove = [];
        for (let i = 0; i < localStorage.length; i++) {
            const key = localStorage.key(i);
            if (key.startsWith(namespace) || key === 'multi_save_data' || key === 'frontend_chat_history_fallback') {
              keysToRemove.push(key);
            }
        }
        keysToRemove.forEach(key => localStorage.removeItem(key));
        this.chatHistoryCache = [];

        // 2. 重置游戏状态（同步操作）
        this.equippedItems = { wuqi: null, fangju: null, shipin: null, fabao1: null, zhuxiuGongfa: null, fuxiuXinfa: null };
        this.gachaState = { astralDust: 160, starglitter: 0, pitySSR: 0, pitySR: 0, ssrGuarantee: false, redeemedCodes: [], activeCompanions: [], firstPullGuaranteedSR: true };
        this.gachaCollection = {};
        this.gachaHistory = [];
        this.theaterState = { theaterPoints: 0 };
        this.pendingActions = [];
        this.saveEquipmentState();
        this.saveGachaState();
        this.savePendingActions();

        // 3. 清空世界书相关条目（异步，等待完成）
        const bookName = '1源堡';
        const entriesToClear = ['本周目经历', '本周目核心记忆', '当前线索', '历史的投影'];
        const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
        const entriesToUpdate = allEntries.filter(entry => entriesToClear.includes(entry.comment)).map(entry => ({ uid: entry.uid, content: '' }));
        if (entriesToUpdate.length) {
          await TavernHelper.setLorebookEntries(bookName, entriesToUpdate);
        }

        // 4. 构造开局内容（字符串拼接绕过正文正则）
        const startTag = '<开' + '局>'; // 拆分标签，避免正文正则误触发
        const endTag = '</开' + '局>';
        const startContent = `${startTag}\n按照下面要求生成\n${endTag}`;

        // 5. 先清空聊天记录（等待完成）
        await TavernHelper.setChatMessages([], { refresh: 'none', force: true });
        console.log('[新周目] 已清空聊天记录');

        // 6. 写入开局内容到message0（关键：等待写入完成，用refresh: 'all'强制同步）
        let messageZero = {
            message_id: 'message0',
            message: '',
            is_user: false,
            role: 'assistant',
            data: {},
            timestamp: Date.now()
        };
        messageZero.message = startContent;
        await TavernHelper.setChatMessages([messageZero], {
          refresh: 'all', // 强制编辑栏同步新内容
        });
        console.log('[新周目] 已写入开局内容到message0');


        // 7. 延迟刷新（确保所有写入操作完成）
        this.showTemporaryMessage('新周目已重置，即将刷新...');
        setTimeout(() => {
          window.location.reload(true); // 强制刷新，加载新内容
        }, 1500); // 延长延迟到1.5秒，确保异步操作完成

      } catch (error) {
        console.error('开启新周目失败:', error);
        this.showTemporaryMessage(`操作失败: ${error.message}`);
      }
    }
  );
},

    bindChronicleListeners() {
    const container = document.getElementById('save-load-modal');
    if (!container) return;
    if (container.dataset.chronicleListenersBound) return;
    container.dataset.chronicleListenersBound = 'true';

    container.addEventListener('click', async (e) => {
        const target = e.target;
        const actionableElement = target.closest('[data-action]');

        if (actionableElement) {
            const action = actionableElement.dataset.action;
            // 【核心修复】使用不同的变量名，避免冲突
            const parentChapter = actionableElement.closest('.chronicle-chapter');
            const slotId = actionableElement.dataset.slotId || parentChapter?.dataset.slotId;

            switch (action) {
            // 新增：处理上一回合/下一回合/回到现在按钮
            case 'history_prev':
                this.viewPreviousMessage();
                return;
            case 'history_next':
                this.viewNextMessage();
                return;
            case 'history_return':
                this.returnToPresent();
                return;
            case 'new_timeline': await this.startNewTimeline(); return; // <<< 新增此行
            case 'reroll': await this.performReroll(); return;
            case 'rollback': await this.performAutoSaveLoad('auto_save_slot_1'); return;
            case 'create_bookmark':{
            const savedData = await this.performSave();
            if (savedData) {
                await this.showSaveLoadManager(savedData);
            }
            return;
            }
            case 'delete': if (slotId) await this.deleteSave(slotId); return;
            case 'export': if (slotId) await this.exportSave(slotId); return;
            case 'load_and_jump': {
            const historyIndex = parseInt(actionableElement.dataset.historyIndex, 10);
            if (slotId && !isNaN(historyIndex)) await this.performLoad(slotId, historyIndex);
            return;
            }
            case 'jump_view': {
                const historyIndex = parseInt(actionableElement.dataset.historyIndex, 10);
                if (!isNaN(historyIndex) && historyIndex < this.chatHistoryCache.length) {
                    this.isHistoryViewMode = true;
                    this.historyViewIndex = historyIndex;
                    const targetSnapshot = this.chatHistoryCache[this.historyViewIndex];
                    if (targetSnapshot) {
                        // 当前时间线jump_view的世界书更新逻辑（复用load_and_jump的合并思路）
                        try {
                            // 【核心修改1：合并当前时间线所有快照的完整经历（和load_and_jump一致）】
                            let mergedJourney = '';
                            for (const snap of this.chatHistoryCache) { // 遍历所有快照，不是只取目标快照
                                if (!snap || !snap.message) continue;
                                const snapJourney = this._extractLastTagContent('本周目经历', snap.message) || '';
                                if (snapJourney.trim()) mergedJourney += snapJourney + '\n\n';
                            }
                            mergedJourney = mergedJourney.trim();

                            // 合并后去重+排序（得到1→最大序号的完整事件链）
                            const allValidEvents = this.parseJourneyEntry(mergedJourney);
                            const uniqueEvents = Array.from(new Map(allValidEvents.map(ev => [ev.序号, ev])).values());
                            uniqueEvents.sort((a, b) => parseInt(a.序号, 10) - parseInt(b.序号, 10));
                            if (uniqueEvents.length === 0) {
                                console.warn(`[jump_view] 无任何有效经历，跳过更新`);
                                this.showTemporaryMessage(`无有效经历记录，跳过世界书更新`, 3000);
                                // 继续更新UI，不影响跳转查看
                                this.renderStateAt(targetSnapshot);
                                this.renderHistoryControls();
                                this.closeAllModals();
                                return;
                            }

                            // 【核心修改2：提取目标快照的最大事件序号（用于精准截断）】
                            const targetJourneyContent = this._extractLastTagContent('本周目经历', targetSnapshot.message) || '';
                            const targetEvents = this.parseJourneyEntry(targetJourneyContent);
                            const maxTargetEventId = targetEvents.length > 0
                                ? Math.max(...targetEvents.map(ev => parseInt(ev.序号, 10) || 0))
                                : 0;
                            console.log(`[jump_view] 目标快照${historyIndex}最大事件序号：${maxTargetEventId}`);
                            console.log(`[jump_view] 合并所有快照后完整事件链：1→${uniqueEvents[uniqueEvents.length-1].序号}（共${uniqueEvents.length}条）`);

                            // 防护：目标快照无有效序号，用完整事件链的最大序号（避免截断失败）
                            const finalMaxId = maxTargetEventId > 0 ? maxTargetEventId : parseInt(uniqueEvents[uniqueEvents.length-1].序号, 10);

                            // 【核心修改3：从完整事件链中筛选≤目标序号的事件（精准截断，不丢中间）】
                            const keepEvents = uniqueEvents.filter(ev => (parseInt(ev.序号, 10) || 0) <= finalMaxId);
                            if (keepEvents.length === 0) {
                                console.warn(`[jump_view] 筛选后无有效事件，跳过更新`);
                                this.showTemporaryMessage(`无有效事件可保留，跳过世界书更新`, 3000);
                                this.renderStateAt(targetSnapshot);
                                this.renderHistoryControls();
                                this.closeAllModals();
                                return;
                            }

                            // 【核心修改4：写入世界书（只要和当前不一致就更，支持补全+截断）】
                            const bookName = '1源堡';
                            const journeyKey = this.unifiedIndex > 1 ? `本周目经历(${this.unifiedIndex})` : '本周目经历';
                            const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
                            const journeyEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === journeyKey);

                            if (journeyEntry && journeyEntry.content) {
                                const currentEvents = this.parseJourneyEntry(journeyEntry.content);
                                const currentEventIds = JSON.stringify(currentEvents.map(ev => ev.序号));
                                const keepEventIds = JSON.stringify(keepEvents.map(ev => ev.序号));

                                if (currentEventIds !== keepEventIds) {
                                    const newContent = keepEvents.map(ev => this.stringifyJourneyEvent(ev)).join('\n\n');
                                    await TavernHelper.setLorebookEntries(bookName, [{ uid: journeyEntry.uid, content: newContent }]);
                                    console.log(`[jump_view] 世界书更新完成：保留1→${finalMaxId}（共${keepEvents.length}条，无中间缺失）`);
                                    this.showTemporaryMessage(`跳转成功！本周目经历更新至序号${finalMaxId}`, 3000);
                                } else {
                                    console.log(`[jump_view] 无需更新：当前经历已匹配目标回合（1→${finalMaxId}）`);
                                }
                            }
                        } catch (error) {
                            console.error('[jump_view] 更新世界书失败:', error);
                            this.showTemporaryMessage(`跳转成功，但世界书更新失败：${error.message}`, 3000);
                        }

                        // 原有逻辑：更新UI（不变）
                        this.renderStateAt(targetSnapshot);
                        this.renderHistoryControls();
                    }
                    this.closeAllModals();
                }
                return;
            }
            }
        }

        // 此处的 chapterElement 变量名不再冲突
        const chapterElement = target.closest('.chronicle-chapter:not(.empty)');
        if (chapterElement) {
            const slotId = chapterElement.dataset.slotId;
            if (slotId) {
                await this.renderChroniclePage(slotId);
            }
        }
    });
},

        async performSave(slotId = null, saveName = null) {
        if (this.chatHistoryCache.length === 0) {
            this.showTemporaryMessage('没有可保存的历史记录。');
            return false;
        }

        const isMobile = /Mobi|Android|iPhone|iPad|iPod/i.test(navigator.userAgent);
        const finalSlotId = slotId || `slot_${Date.now()}`;
        const finalSaveName = saveName || await this.promptForSaveName(`书签 - ${new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE').replace(/ /g, '_')}`);
        if (!finalSaveName) return false;

        // 🔴 核心：只等“编辑器自动初始化”，不操作也能避开冲突
          if (isMobile && this.isVariablePanelInitializing) {
            this.showTemporaryMessage('等待面板初始化完成...', 1000);
            // 循环等待，直到编辑器初始化完成（最多等1.5秒，覆盖编辑器所有延迟）
            let waitCount = 0;
            while (this.isVariablePanelInitializing && waitCount < 15) {
              await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 100));
              waitCount++;
            }
          }

        this.showTemporaryMessage('正在固化时间线...');
        try {
            const bookName = '1源堡';
            const journeyKey = this.unifiedIndex > 1 ? `本周目经历(${this.unifiedIndex})` : '本周目经历';
            const coreMemoryKey = this.unifiedIndex > 1 ? `本周目核心记忆(${this.unifiedIndex})` : '本周目核心记忆';
            const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
            //强制读取世界书中的完整内容
            const journeyEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === journeyKey);
            let journeyContent = journeyEntry ? journeyEntry.content || '' : '';
            // 打印存档时的事件数量
            const eventCount = (journeyContent.match(/序号\|(\d+)/g) || []).length;
            console.log(`[存档] 世界书中“${journeyKey}”包含 ${eventCount} 个事件，将完整保存`);
             if (eventCount === 0 && this.chatHistoryCache.length > 0) {
            console.warn('[存档] 世界书内容为空，尝试从历史快照合并事件');
            let mergedContent = '';
            for (const snap of this.chatHistoryCache) {
                const snapJourney = this._extractLastTagContent('本周目经历', snap.message) || '';
                if (snapJourney) mergedContent += snapJourney + '\n\n';
            }
            journeyContent = mergedContent.trim();
        }
            const coreMemoryEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === coreMemoryKey);

            const coreMemoryContent = coreMemoryEntry ? coreMemoryEntry.content : '';

            const saveDataPayload = {
                timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
                save_name: finalSaveName,
                timeline_history: _.cloneDeep(this.chatHistoryCache),
                snapshot_data: {
                    gacha_data: { state: _.cloneDeep(this.gachaState), collection: _.cloneDeep(this.gachaCollection), history: _.cloneDeep(this.gachaHistory) },
                    lorebook_content: { journey: journeyContent, core_memory: coreMemoryContent }
                }
            };
             // 🔴 核心：只在移动端做“只读验证+精准提示”，PC端跳过（确保PC安全）
        if (isMobile) {
            // 定义验证函数：只检查，不修改数据
            const checkSerialize = (name, data) => {
                try {
                    JSON.stringify(data, AppStorage.getCircularReplacer());
                    return { success: true };
                } catch (e) {
                    return { success: false, error: e.message };
                }
            };

            // 1. 验证整个timeline_history是否能序列化
            const timelineCheck = checkSerialize('时间线整体', saveDataPayload.timeline_history);
            if (!timelineCheck.success) {
                this.showTemporaryMessage(`❌ 时间线序列化失败：${timelineCheck.error}`, 3000);
                // 2. 进一步定位：逐个检查快照
                for (let i = 0; i < saveDataPayload.timeline_history.length; i++) {
                    const snapCheck = checkSerialize(`快照${i}`, saveDataPayload.timeline_history[i]);
                    if (!snapCheck.success) {
                        this.showTemporaryMessage(`❌ 快照${i}有问题：${snapCheck.error}`, 3000);
                        // 3. 定位快照内的$meta
                        if (saveDataPayload.timeline_history[i].data?.stat_data?.$meta) {
                            const metaCheck = checkSerialize(`快照${i}的$meta`, saveDataPayload.timeline_history[i].data.stat_data.$meta);
                            if (!metaCheck.success) {
                                this.showTemporaryMessage(`❌ 快照${i}的$meta：${metaCheck.error}`, 3000);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                // 4. 验证抽卡数据
                const gachaCheck = checkSerialize('抽卡数据', saveDataPayload.snapshot_data.gacha_data);
                if (!gachaCheck.success) {
                    this.showTemporaryMessage(`❌ 抽卡数据：${gachaCheck.error}`, 3000);
                }
            }
        }

            const allSaves = await this.getSavesFromStorage();
            allSaves[finalSlotId] = saveDataPayload;
            await AppStorage.saveData('multi_save_data', allSaves);
            // 🔴 核心：保存后立即读回验证（只在移动端做，PC端跳过）
        if (isMobile) {
            // 移动端延迟1000ms，确保数据落地
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
            // 读回刚保存的数据
            //const savedSaves = await AppStorage.loadData('multi_save_data');
            //if (savedSaves === null) {
            //    this.showTemporaryMessage('⚠️ 读取存档失败：未找到任何数据', 3000);
            //    return false; // 提前退出，避免后续报错
            //}
            //const savedPayload = savedSaves[finalSlotId];

            // 验证timeline_history是否存在且不为空
            //if (!savedPayload) {
            //    this.showTemporaryMessage('⚠️ 存档未找到', 3000);
            //} else if (!savedPayload.timeline_history || savedPayload.timeline_history.length === 0) {
            //    this.showTemporaryMessage('⚠️ 快照为空（未保存成功）', 3000);
            //} else {
            //    this.showTemporaryMessage(`✅ 快照已保存（共${savedPayload.timeline_history.length}回合）`, 3000);
            //}

            if (isMobile && this.renderSaveList) {
            const updatedSaves = await this.getSavesFromStorage();
            this.renderSaveList(updatedSaves);
            }
        }
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`书签 “${finalSaveName}” 创建成功！`);
            return allSaves;
        } catch (error) {
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`创建书签失败: ${error.message}`);
            return false;
        }
    },
    renderChronicleChapter(data, slotId) {
        if (slotId === 'current_timeline') {
            const history = data; // For current timeline, data is the history cache itself
            return `
                <div class="chronicle-chapter active" data-slot-id="current_timeline" style="border-color: #daa520;">
                    <div class="chapter-actions">
                        <button class="interaction-btn primary-btn" data-action="create_bookmark" title="将当前时间线固化为一个永久分支" style="padding: 4px 10px; font-size: 12px;">+ 创建书签</button>
                    </div>
                    <div class="chapter-name">当前时间线 (进行中)</div>
                    <div class="chapter-meta">共 ${history.length} 回合</div>
                </div>
            `;
        } else {
            const saveData = data; // For archived timelines, data is a save object
            if (saveData && saveData.timeline_history) {
                return `
                    <div class="chronicle-chapter" data-slot-id="${slotId}">
                        <div class="chapter-actions">
                            <button class="chapter-action-btn export" data-action="export" title="导出">↑</button>
                            <button class="chapter-action-btn delete" data-action="delete" title="删除">🔥</button>
                        </div>
                        <div class="chapter-name">${saveData.save_name}</div>
                        <div class="chapter-meta">${new Date(saveData.timestamp).toLocaleString('zh-CN')} - 共 ${saveData.timeline_history.length} 回合</div>
                    </div>
                `;
            }
        }
        return '';
    },

    async renderChroniclePage(slotId, showAll = false) {
        const existingShowAllBtn = document.getElementById('btn-show-all-events');
        if (existingShowAllBtn) existingShowAllBtn.remove();
        const pageHeader = document.getElementById('chronicle-page-header');
        const pageContent = document.getElementById('chronicle-page-content');
        let timelineData, timelineName, historyArray;

        document.querySelectorAll('.chronicle-chapter').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active'));
        document.querySelector(`.chronicle-chapter[data-slot-id="${slotId}"]`)?.classList.add('active');

        if (slotId === 'current_timeline') {
            timelineName = '当前时间线 (进行中)';
            historyArray = this.chatHistoryCache;
        } else {
            const saves = await this.getSavesFromStorage();
            timelineData = saves[slotId];
            if (timelineData) {
                timelineName = timelineData.save_name;
                historyArray = timelineData.timeline_history;
            }
        }

        if (historyArray) {
            pageHeader.textContent = timelineName;
            const titles = this._extractJourneyTitlesFromHistory(historyArray, showAll);
            if (titles.length > 0) {
                pageContent.className = '';
                // 【核心修复】根据是否为当前时间线，生成不同的action指令
                const action = (slotId === 'current_timeline') ? 'jump_view' : 'load_and_jump';
                pageContent.innerHTML = titles.map(t =>
                    `<div class="chronicle-event" data-action="${action}" data-slot-id="${slotId}" data-history-index="${t.historyIndex}">${t.title}</div>`
                ).join('');
                // 如果快照总数超过20，显示“显示全部”按钮
                if (historyArray.length > 20 && !showAll) {
                    pageContent.insertAdjacentHTML('afterend', `
                        <div style="text-align: center; margin-top: 10px;">
                            <button id="btn-show-all-events" class="interaction-btn"
                                data-slot-id="${slotId}">显示全部回合（共${historyArray.length}条）</button>
                        </div>
                    `);
                    // 绑定按钮点击事件（点击后重新渲染并显示全部）
                    document.getElementById('btn-show-all-events').addEventListener('click', async (e) => {
                        const currentSlotId = e.target.dataset.slotId;
                        await this.renderChroniclePage(currentSlotId, true);  // 传递showAll=true
                    });
                }
            } else {
                pageContent.className = 'empty-placeholder';
                pageContent.innerHTML = '此时间线无关键事件记录。';
            }
        } else {
            pageHeader.textContent = '事件详情';
            pageContent.className = 'empty-placeholder';
            pageContent.innerHTML = '请从左侧目录选择一条时间线';
        }
    },
    async performReroll() {
    const allSaves = await this.getSavesFromStorage();
    const lastTurnSave = allSaves['auto_save_slot_1'];
    if (!lastTurnSave || !this.lastSentPrompt) { this.showTemporaryMessage('没有可用于重新生成的状态。'); return; }
    if (this.chatHistoryCache.length < 1) { this.showTemporaryMessage('历史记录不足，无法重新生成。'); return; }

    this.showCustomConfirm('确定要重新生成上一次的回答吗？', async () => {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('正在回溯状态并重新请求...');
        this.closeAllModals();
        try {
            // 1. 回滚世界书
            await this._rollbackJourneyLog(1);

            // 2.【核心修正】回滚前端历史记录
            this.chatHistoryCache.pop(); // 移除最后一条记录
    const lastRecord = this.chatHistoryCache[this.chatHistoryCache.length - 1];
   console.log('[回滚保存校验] 剩余最后一条记录的data:', lastRecord?.data);
  console.log('[回滚保存校验] 是否包含stat_data:', !!lastRecord?.data?.stat_data);
   await AppStorage.saveData(this._getHistoryKey(), this.chatHistoryCache);

            // 3. 从自动存档恢复状态到酒馆
            const messageZero = (await getChatMessages('0'))[0];
            messageZero.message = lastTurnSave.message_content;
            messageZero.data = _.cloneDeep(lastTurnSave.mvu_data);
            await TavernHelper.setChatMessages([messageZero], { refresh: 'none' });

            // 4. 恢复脚本内部的各种状态
            this.currentMvuState = _.cloneDeep(lastTurnSave.mvu_data);
            this.equippedItems = _.cloneDeep(lastTurnSave.equipped_items);
            this.pendingActions = _.cloneDeep(lastTurnSave.pending_actions) || [];
            this.saveEquipmentState();
            this.savePendingActions();
            this._loadGachaDataFromSave(lastTurnSave); // 恢复Gacha数据

            // 5. 重新发送指令
            const generateConfig = {
                injects: [{
                    role: 'user',
                    content: this.lastSentPrompt, // 复用上次的完整内容（含记忆+行动）
                    position: 'in_chat',
                    depth: 0,
                    should_scan: true
                }],
                should_stream: this.isStreamingEnabled,
            };
            await TavernHelper.generate(generateConfig);

            // 刷新UI到回滚后的状态
            await this.returnToPresent();


        } catch (error) {
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`重新生成失败: ${error.message}`);
        }
    });
},
   async performLoad(slotId, historyIndex = -1) {
    const allSaves = await this.getSavesFromStorage();
    let saveData = allSaves[slotId];
    let historyArray = [];
    let isCurrentTimeline = false;

    // 1. 先区分“当前时间线”和“其他存档”，初始化 historyArray
    if (slotId === 'current_timeline') {
        isCurrentTimeline = true;
        historyArray = this.chatHistoryCache; // 当前时间线：用前端缓存的历史
    } else {
        // 非当前时间线：校验并初始化数据
        if (!saveData) {
            this.showTemporaryMessage('此存档位为空。');
            return;
        }
        // 存档格式转换
        const convertedSaveData = await this._migrateSaveData(saveData);
        if (convertedSaveData !== saveData) {
            this.showTemporaryMessage('旧版存档已自动升级！');
            allSaves[slotId] = convertedSaveData;
            await AppStorage.saveData('multi_save_data', allSaves);
            saveData = convertedSaveData;
        }
        // 校验时间线历史
        if (!saveData.timeline_history || saveData.timeline_history.length === 0) {
            this.showTemporaryMessage('此时间线为空或已损坏。');
            return;
        }
        // 给非当前时间线的 historyArray 赋值（之前遗漏！）
        historyArray = saveData.timeline_history;
    }

    // 2. 定义 confirmAction（移到分支外，确保所有场景都能访问）
    const confirmAction = async () => {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('正在加载时间线并恢复世界状态...');
        try {
            let targetJourneyContent = '';
            // 计算目标快照索引（仅声明一次，无重复）
            const targetIndex = (historyIndex !== -1 && historyIndex < historyArray.length)
                ? historyIndex
                : historyArray.length - 1;
            // 获取目标快照（historyArray 已在前面初始化，无空值）
            const targetSnapshot = historyArray[targetIndex];

            // 3. 提取目标快照的“本周目经历”
             // 核心修改：导入存档时，遍历timeline_history合并所有快照的经历
            if (!isCurrentTimeline) {
                // 优先读取snapshot_data的完整经历
                targetJourneyContent = saveData.snapshot_data?.lorebook_content?.journey || '';
                // 若经历不足（或为空），遍历timeline_history合并所有快照的经历
                if (!targetJourneyContent) {
                    console.log('[读档] 从存档快照合并完整经历');
                    let mergedJourney = '';
                    for (const snap of saveData.timeline_history) {
                        const snapJourney = this._extractLastTagContent('本周目经历', snap.message) || '';
                        if (snapJourney) mergedJourney += snapJourney + '\n\n';
                    }
                    targetJourneyContent = mergedJourney.trim();
                }
                console.log(`[读档-导入存档] 合并后共 ${(targetJourneyContent.match(/序号: \d+/g) || []).length} 个事件`);
            } else {
                targetJourneyContent = this._extractLastTagContent('本周目经历', targetSnapshot.message) || '';
                console.log(`[读档-当前时间线] 从快照 ${targetIndex} 提取的经历：${targetJourneyContent}`);
            }

            // 4. 解析最大事件序号，截断世界书
            const targetEvents = this.parseJourneyEntry(targetJourneyContent);
            const maxTargetEventId = targetEvents.length > 0
                ? Math.max(...targetEvents.map(ev => parseInt(ev.序号, 10) || 0))
                : 0;
            console.log(`[读档] 目标快照的最大事件序号：${maxTargetEventId}`);

            const bookName = '1源堡';
            const journeyKey = this.unifiedIndex > 1 ? `本周目经历(${this.unifiedIndex})` : '本周目经历';
            const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
            const journeyEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === journeyKey);

            if (journeyEntry && journeyEntry.content) {
                const currentEvents = this.parseJourneyEntry(journeyEntry.content);
                // 只保留序号 ≤ 最大事件序号的内容
                const keepEvents = currentEvents.filter(ev => (parseInt(ev.序号, 10) || 0) <= maxTargetEventId);
                if (keepEvents.length < currentEvents.length) {
                    const newContent = keepEvents.map(ev => this.stringifyJourneyEvent(ev)).join('\n\n');
                    await TavernHelper.setLorebookEntries(bookName, [{ uid: journeyEntry.uid, content: newContent }]);
                    console.log(`[读档] 截断后保留 ${keepEvents.length} 条事件`);
                }
            }

            // 5. 恢复世界书（仅非当前时间线需要）
            if (!isCurrentTimeline && saveData?.snapshot_data?.lorebook_content) {
                const coreMemoryKey = this.unifiedIndex > 1 ? `本周目核心记忆(${this.unifiedIndex})` : '本周目核心记忆';
                const coreMemoryEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === coreMemoryKey);

                if (journeyEntry) {
                    await TavernHelper.setLorebookEntries(bookName, [{
                        uid: journeyEntry.uid,
                        content: saveData.snapshot_data.lorebook_content.journey || ''
                    }]);
                }
                if (coreMemoryEntry && saveData.snapshot_data.lorebook_content.core_memory) {
                    await TavernHelper.setLorebookEntries(bookName, [{
                        uid: coreMemoryEntry.uid,
                        content: saveData.snapshot_data.lorebook_content.core_memory
                    }]);
                }
            }

            // 6. 恢复抽卡数据
            if (!isCurrentTimeline && saveData?.snapshot_data) {
                 // 恢复星界数据
                 if (saveData.snapshot_data.gacha_data) {
                   this.gachaState = _.cloneDeep(saveData.snapshot_data.gacha_data.state);
                   this.gachaCollection = _.cloneDeep(saveData.snapshot_data.gacha_data.collection);
                   this.gachaHistory = _.cloneDeep(saveData.snapshot_data.gacha_data.history);
                   this.saveGachaState();
                 }
            } else {
                this._loadGachaDataFromSave(null);
            }

            // 7. 恢复前端聊天历史
            this.chatHistoryCache = _.cloneDeep(historyArray);
            const firstRecord = this.chatHistoryCache[0];
            console.log('[加载存档保存校验] 存档中第一条记录的data:', firstRecord?.data);
            console.log('[加载存档保存校验] 是否包含stat_data:', !!firstRecord?.data?.stat_data);
            await AppStorage.saveData(this._getHistoryKey(), this.chatHistoryCache);

            // 8. 同步到酒馆聊天记录
            const messages = await getChatMessages('0');
            if (!messages || messages.length === 0) throw new Error('无法获取聊天记录，无法完成加载。');
            const messageZero = messages[0];
            messageZero.message = targetSnapshot.message;
            messageZero.data = targetSnapshot.data;
            await TavernHelper.setChatMessages([messageZero], { refresh: 'none' });

            // 9. 更新UI状态
            this.isHistoryViewMode = (historyIndex !== -1 && historyIndex < this.chatHistoryCache.length - 1);
            this.historyViewIndex = targetIndex;
            this.renderStateAt(targetSnapshot);
            this.renderHistoryControls();
            await this.loadEquipmentState();

            this.closeAllModals();
            // 适配不同场景的成功消息
            const timelineName = isCurrentTimeline ? '当前时间线' : saveData.save_name;
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`时间线 “${timelineName}” 加载成功！`);

            // 10. 清除暂存内容
            this.lastExtractedJourney = null;
            this.lastExtractedPastLives = null;
            this.lastExtractedNovelText = null;
            this.lastExtractedCharacterCard = null;
            this.lastExtractedCoreMemory = null;
            this.lastExtractedClues = null;
            this.lastWrittenJourney = null;
            this.lastWrittenPastLives = null;
            this.lastWrittenNovelText = null;
            this.lastWrittenCoreMemory = null;
            this.lastWrittenClues = null;
            console.log('[读档] 已清除所有暂存的提取内容，防止错误的自动覆盖。');

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('加载时间线时出错:', error);
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`加载失败: ${error.message}`);
        }
    };

    // 11. 统一调用 confirmAction（移到分支外，所有场景通用）
    if (historyIndex !== -1) {
        confirmAction();
    } else {
        // 非当前时间线显示存档名，当前时间线显示固定文案
        const confirmText = isCurrentTimeline
            ? '确定要加载当前时间线的此快照吗？当前进度将被覆盖。'
            : `确定要加载时间线 “${saveData.save_name}” 吗？当前的游戏进度将被覆盖。`;
        this.showCustomConfirm(confirmText, confirmAction);
    }
},

    async performAutoSaveLoad(slotId) {
    const allSaves = await this.getSavesFromStorage();
    const saveData = allSaves[slotId];
    if (!saveData) {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('此自动存档为空。');
        return;
    }

    this.showCustomConfirm(`确定要读取 "${saveData.save_name}" 吗？当前进度将丢失。`, async () => {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('正在回溯至自动存档点...');
        try {
            const stepsToRollback = (slotId === 'auto_save_slot_1') ? 1 : (slotId === 'auto_save_slot_2') ? 2 : 0;
            if (stepsToRollback === 0 || this.chatHistoryCache.length < stepsToRollback) {
                this.showTemporaryMessage('无法回滚，历史记录不足。');
                this.closeAllModals();
                return;
            }

            this.chatHistoryCache = this.chatHistoryCache.slice(0, this.chatHistoryCache.length - stepsToRollback);
            await AppStorage.saveData(this._getHistoryKey(), this.chatHistoryCache);

            await this._rollbackJourneyLog(stepsToRollback);

            const lastSnapshot = this.chatHistoryCache.length > 0 ? this.chatHistoryCache[this.chatHistoryCache.length - 1] : null;

            if (lastSnapshot) {
                const messages = await getChatMessages('0'); // 变量名改为messages（数组）
                if (!messages || messages.length === 0) {
                    throw new Error('未找到聊天消息，无法同步存档状态');
                }
                const messageZero = messages[0];
                messageZero.message = lastSnapshot.message;
                messageZero.data = lastSnapshot.data;
                await TavernHelper.setChatMessages([messageZero], { refresh: 'all' });

                await this.returnToPresent();
                this.showTemporaryMessage(`已成功回滚至 "${saveData.save_name}"`);
            } else {
                this.isBusy = false;
                if (this.isTrueNewGame && this.currentMvuState) {
                    console.log('[自动读档] 新游戏无快照，生成初始快照');
                    const initSnapshot = {
                        message_id: `frontend-hist-init-${Date.now()}`,
                        message: '新周目初始快照（读档生成）',
                        is_user: false,
                        role: 'assistant',
                        data: _.cloneDeep(this.currentMvuState),
                        timestamp: Date.now()
                    };
                    this.chatHistoryCache.push(initSnapshot);
                    await AppStorage.saveData(this._getHistoryKey(), this.chatHistoryCache);
                    await this.renderUI(this.currentMvuState.stat_data);
                    this.showTemporaryMessage('新周目初始数据已加载，无需刷新');
                } else {
                    console.log('[自动读档] 已有游戏快照丢失，刷新兜底');
                    this.closeAllModals();
                    window.location.reload();
                    return;
                }
            }

            this.closeAllModals();

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('执行自动读档时出错:', error);
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`读档失败: ${error.message}`);
            this.closeAllModals();
        }
    });
},

       // --- 新增：状态回退函数 ---
          async performRollback() {
    this.showTemporaryMessage('正在回退状态...');
    let rollbackData = null;

    if (this.pendingAutoSave) {
        rollbackData = this.pendingAutoSave;
        console.log('[源堡-回滚] 使用内存中的“待定存档”进行回退。');
    } else {
        const allSaves = await this.getSavesFromStorage();
        rollbackData = allSaves['auto_save_slot_1'];
        console.log('[源堡-回滚] 未找到待定存档，使用磁盘上的“上一回合”存档进行回退。');
    }

    if (!rollbackData) {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('回退失败：未找到可用的回退点。');
        this.isBusy = false;
        this.hideWaitingMessage(true);
        return;
    }

    try {
        this.currentMvuState = _.cloneDeep(rollbackData.mvu_data);
        this.equippedItems = _.cloneDeep(rollbackData.equipped_items);
        this.pendingActions = _.cloneDeep(rollbackData.pending_actions) || [];

        const messages = await getChatMessages('0');
        if (!messages || messages.length === 0) {
            throw new Error('无法获取聊天记录，无法完成回退。');
        }
        const messageZero = messages[0];
        messageZero.message = rollbackData.message_content;
        messageZero.data = this.currentMvuState;
        await TavernHelper.setChatMessages([messageZero], { refresh: 'none' });

        this.saveEquipmentState();
        this.savePendingActions();
        this.renderUI(this.currentMvuState.stat_data);
        await this.loadAndDisplayCurrentScene(rollbackData.message_content);

        this.showTemporaryMessage('状态已成功回退。');
        this.closeAllModals();

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('执行状态回退时出错:', error);
        this.showTemporaryMessage(`回退失败: ${error.message}`);
    } finally {
        this.isBusy = false;
        this.hideWaitingMessage(true);

        if (rollbackData.gacha_data) {
            this.gachaState = _.cloneDeep(rollbackData.gacha_data.state);
            this.gachaCollection = _.cloneDeep(rollbackData.gacha_data.collection);
            this.gachaHistory = _.cloneDeep(rollbackData.gacha_data.history);
        } else {
            this.gachaState = { astralDust: 160, starglitter: 0, pitySSR: 0, pitySR: 0, ssrGuarantee: false, firstPullGuaranteedSR: true };
            this.gachaCollection = {};
            this.gachaHistory = [];
        }
        // --- 核心修改：清除暂存的伙伴信息 ---
        this.pendingCompanionJoin = null;
        // --- 修改结束 ---



        this.pendingAutoSave = null;
    }
},

          async deleteSave(slotId) {
            const allSaves = await this.getSavesFromStorage();
            const saveData = allSaves[slotId];
            if (!saveData) { this.showTemporaryMessage('此存档位已空。'); return; }

            this.showCustomConfirm(`确定要永久删除存档 “${saveData.save_name}” 吗？`, async () => {
                try {
                    await this.deleteLorebookBackup(saveData);
                    delete allSaves[slotId];
                    await AppStorage.saveData('multi_save_data', allSaves);
                    this.showTemporaryMessage('存档已删除。');
                    await this.showSaveLoadManager();
                } catch (error) {
                    console.error('删除存档时出错:', error);
                    this.showTemporaryMessage(`删除失败: ${error.message}`);
                }
            });
          },

          async deleteLorebookBackup(saveData) {
            if (!saveData || !saveData.lorebook_entries) return;
            const bookName = '1源堡';
            try {
                const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
                const uidsToDelete = [];
                const journeyEntry = allEntries.find(e => e.comment === saveData.lorebook_entries.journey_entry_name);
                const pastLivesEntry = allEntries.find(e => e.comment === saveData.lorebook_entries.past_lives_entry_name);
                if (journeyEntry) uidsToDelete.push(journeyEntry.uid);
                if (pastLivesEntry) uidsToDelete.push(pastLivesEntry.uid);
                if (uidsToDelete.length > 0) {
                    await TavernHelper.deleteLorebookEntries(bookName, uidsToDelete);
                }
            } catch (error) {
                 console.error('删除世界书备份时出错:', error);
            }
          },

async exportSave(slotId) {
    this.showTemporaryMessage('正在准备导出数据...', 2000);
    try {
        const allSaves = await this.getSavesFromStorage();
        const saveData = allSaves[slotId];

        if (!saveData) {
            this.showTemporaryMessage('错误：找不到要导出的存档数据。');
            return;
        }

        const exportData = {
            exportVersion: '1.0',
            exportedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
            saveData: saveData,
            lorebookData: []
        };

        if (saveData.lorebook_entries && typeof saveData.lorebook_entries === 'object') {
            const bookName = '1源堡';
            const entryNamesToExport = Object.values(saveData.lorebook_entries);
            if (entryNamesToExport.length > 0) {
                const allLorebookEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
                exportData.lorebookData = allLorebookEntries.filter(entry =>
                    entryNamesToExport.includes(entry.comment)
                );
            }
        }

        // 保留缩进：保证JSON可读性
        const jsonString = JSON.stringify(exportData, null, 2);
        const blob = new Blob([jsonString], { type: 'application/json' });
        const fileSizeMB = blob.size / (1024 * 1024); // 计算文件体积（MB）
        const safeSaveName = (saveData.save_name || slotId).replace(/[\/:*?"<>|]/g, '_');
        const fileName = `SefirotSave_${safeSaveName}.json`;

        // --- 核心：调整方案逻辑（修复错误+优化用户体验） ---
        // 标记createObjectURL是否成功（移到try外，避免作用域问题）
        let isCreateObjectURLSuccess = false;
        try {
            // 大文件阈值管控：保留缩进后文件体积略增，>100MB提醒用户
            if (fileSizeMB > 100) {
                if (!confirm(`当前存档体积约${fileSizeMB.toFixed(1)}MB（含缩进），超大文件可能导致导出缓慢或失败，是否继续？`)) {
                    this.showTemporaryMessage('已取消导出');
                    return;
                }
            }

            // 方案1（第一优先级）：现代浏览器首选 - createObjectURL（大文件友好）
            const blobUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
            const a = document.createElement('a');
            a.href = blobUrl;
            a.download = fileName;
            a.style.display = 'none';
            document.body.appendChild(a);

            // 优化：监听a标签的点击事件完成，再标记成功（尽量贴近实际下载触发）
            a.addEventListener('click', () => {
                isCreateObjectURLSuccess = true;
                // 延迟释放内存：适度增加到2秒（给大文件下载留足时间，不要太长）
                setTimeout(() => {
                    URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl);
                    document.body.removeChild(a);
                }, 2000); // 2秒足够浏览器触发下载，过长会占用内存
            }, { once: true });

            // 稳定触发点击事件
            a.dispatchEvent(new MouseEvent('click', { bubbles: true, cancelable: true }));

        } catch (downloadError) {
            console.error('createObjectURL方案失败，切换为msSaveBlob:', downloadError);
            isCreateObjectURLSuccess = false;

            // 方案2（备选）：Via/Android WebView - msSaveBlob
            if (window.navigator && typeof window.navigator.msSaveBlob === 'function') {
                window.navigator.msSaveBlob(blob, fileName);
                this.showTemporaryMessage('存档已成功导出（兼容模式）！');
                return;
            }

            // 方案3（兜底）：极旧浏览器 - FileReader（优化逻辑：不直接禁止，提示风险）
            // 调整阈值为80MB（适度提高，同时提示风险）
            const downgradeThresholdMB = 80;
            if (fileSizeMB > downgradeThresholdMB) {
                // 不直接禁止，而是给出建议
                this.showTemporaryMessage(`当前存档${fileSizeMB.toFixed(1)}MB，超出降级方案处理上限！建议：1.使用Chrome/Edge浏览器导出 2.拆分存档后再导出`);
                return;
            }

            // 提示用户：降级方案可能失败，让用户有心理准备
            if (!confirm(`当前存档${fileSizeMB.toFixed(1)}MB，使用降级方案可能导致浏览器卡顿或失败，是否尝试？`)) {
                this.showTemporaryMessage('已取消导出');
                return;
            }

            const reader = new FileReader();
            reader.onload = (e) => {
                const a = document.createElement('a');
                a.href = e.target.result;
                a.download = fileName;
                document.body.appendChild(a);
                a.click();
                document.body.removeChild(a);
                this.showTemporaryMessage('存档已成功导出（降级模式）！');
            };
            reader.onerror = (e) => {
                console.error('DataURL转换失败:', e);
                this.showTemporaryMessage('降级导出失败！建议使用Chrome/Edge浏览器导出，或拆分存档后重试。');
            };
            // 开始转换（大文件可能卡顿，提前提示）
            this.showTemporaryMessage('正在转换数据（大文件请稍候）...');
            reader.readAsDataURL(blob);
            return; // 触发降级方案后直接返回
        }

        // 优化：只有当createObjectURL成功时，才提示导出成功（避免假成功）
        if (isCreateObjectURLSuccess) {
            this.showTemporaryMessage('存档导出指令已触发，请注意浏览器下载提示！');
        } else {
            // 兜底：如果标记为失败，补充提示
            this.showTemporaryMessage('导出指令已发送，若未收到下载，请尝试兼容模式！');
        }

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('导出存档时出错:', error);
        this.showTemporaryMessage(`导出失败: ${error.message}`);
    }
},

async performImportOverwrite(slotId) {
 if (!this.importedSaveData) {
 this.showTemporaryMessage('没有暂存的导入数据。');
 return;
 }

 const allSaves = await this.getSavesFromStorage();
 const existingSave = allSaves[slotId];

 const confirmMessage = existingSave
 ? `确定要用导入的存档 “${this.importedSaveData.save_name}” 覆盖现有存档 “${existingSave.save_name}” 吗？`
 : `确定要将存档 “${this.importedSaveData.save_name}” 导入到这个空槽位吗？`;

 this.showCustomConfirm(confirmMessage, async () => {
 this.showTemporaryMessage('正在导入存档...');
 try {
 // 如果覆盖的是一个已有存档，先删除它关联的旧世界书备份
 if (existingSave) {
 await this.deleteLorebookBackup(existingSave);
 }

 const importedData = _.cloneDeep(this.importedSaveData);

 // 关键：将导入的存档数据写入选定的槽位
 allSaves[slotId] = importedData;
 await AppStorage.saveData('multi_save_data', allSaves);

 this.showTemporaryMessage('存档导入成功！');
 this.importedSaveData = null; // 清除临时数据
 this.showSaveLoadManager(); // 刷新存档管理器界面
 } catch (error) {
 console.error('执行导入覆盖时出错:', error);
 this.showTemporaryMessage(`导入失败: ${error.message}`);
 }
 });
 },
   async clearAllSaves() {
        this.showCustomConfirm('【高危操作】确定要删除所有手动存档吗？此操作无法恢复。', async () => {
            this.showTemporaryMessage('正在清除所有存档...');
            try {
                // 【核心修复】不再删除整个存档对象，而是将其重置为空对象{}
                await AppStorage.saveData('multi_save_data', {});

                this.showTemporaryMessage('所有手动存档已成功清除。');
                this.showSaveLoadManager(); // 重新渲染存档界面
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('清除所有存档时出错:', error);
                this.showTemporaryMessage(`清除失败: ${error.message}`);
            }
        });
    },
       async _migrateSaveData(saveData) {
    // 检查是否为需要迁移的旧版存档 (有 message_content 但没有 timeline_history)
    if (saveData && saveData.message_content && !saveData.timeline_history) {
        console.log(`[存档迁移] 检测到旧版存档 “${saveData.save_name}”，正在进行转换...`);

        const newTimelineSave = {
            timestamp: saveData.timestamp,
            save_name: `${saveData.save_name} (旧版转换)`,
            timeline_history: [{
                message_id: `migrated-hist-${Date.now()}`,
                message: saveData.message_content,
                is_user: false,
                role: 'assistant',
                data: {
                    ..._.cloneDeep(saveData.mvu_data),
                    equipped_items: _.cloneDeep(saveData.equipped_items),
                    gacha_data: _.cloneDeep(saveData.gacha_data)
                },
                timestamp: new Date(saveData.timestamp).getTime()
            }],
            snapshot_data: {
                gacha_data: _.cloneDeep(saveData.gacha_data),
                lorebook_content: {}
            }
        };

        // 尝试从旧存档信息中恢复世界书内容
        if (saveData.lorebook_entries && saveData.lorebook_entries.journey_entry_name) {
            try {
                const bookName = '1源堡';
                const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
                const backupEntry = allEntries.find(e => e.comment === saveData.lorebook_entries.journey_entry_name);
                if (backupEntry) {
                    newTimelineSave.snapshot_data.lorebook_content.journey = backupEntry.content;
                    console.log('[存档迁移] 已成功从世界书备份中恢复“本周目经历”。');
                }
            } catch(e) {
                console.error('[存档迁移] 尝试恢复世界书时出错:', e);
            }
        }

        return newTimelineSave; // 返回转换后的新格式存档
    }

    return saveData; // 如果不是旧版，直接返回原存档
},
               async handleFileImport(event) {
    const file = event.target.files[0];
    if (!file) return;

    this.showTemporaryMessage('正在导入存档...', 3000);
    const reader = new FileReader();

    reader.onload = async (e) => {
        try {
            const importData = JSON.parse(e.target.result);

            if (importData.exportVersion !== '1.0' || !importData.saveData) {
                throw new Error('存档文件格式无效或已损坏。');
            }

            // 【核心修改】在处理导入数据前，先通过迁移函数进行转换
            const migratedSaveData = await this._migrateSaveData(importData.saveData);

            const allSaves = await this.getSavesFromStorage();
            const newSlotId = `slot_${Date.now()}`; // 使用动态ID，不再受5个槽位限制

            const bookName = '1源堡';
            const currentEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
            const currentEntryNames = new Set(currentEntries.map(entry => entry.comment));

            const newSaveData = _.cloneDeep(migratedSaveData);
            const entriesToCreate = [];

            if (Array.isArray(importData.lorebookData)) {
                for (const entryToImport of importData.lorebookData) {
                    let newEntryName = entryToImport.comment;
                    let originalEntryName = entryToImport.comment;

                    if (currentEntryNames.has(newEntryName)) {
                        newEntryName = `${newEntryName}_imported_${Date.now()}`;
                        this.showTemporaryMessage(`世界书条目“${originalEntryName}”已存在，重命名为“${newEntryName}”`, 4000);
                    }

                    const newEntry = { ...entryToImport };
                    delete newEntry.uid;
                    newEntry.comment = newEntryName;
                    newEntry.keys = [newEntryName];
                    newEntry.enabled = false;
                    entriesToCreate.push(newEntry);

                    if (newSaveData.lorebook_entries) {
                        for (const key in newSaveData.lorebook_entries) {
                            if (newSaveData.lorebook_entries[key] === originalEntryName) {
                                newSaveData.lorebook_entries[key] = newEntryName;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            if (entriesToCreate.length > 0) {
                await TavernHelper.createLorebookEntries(bookName, entriesToCreate);
            }

            newSaveData.save_name = `${newSaveData.save_name} (导入)`;
            allSaves[newSlotId] = newSaveData;
            await AppStorage.saveData('multi_save_data', allSaves);

            this.showTemporaryMessage(`存档已成功导入！`);
            this.showSaveLoadManager();

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('导入存档时出错:', error);
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`导入失败: ${error.message}`);
        } finally {
            event.target.value = '';
        }
    };

    reader.readAsText(file);
},

     async performImportOverwrite(slotId) {
    if (!this.importedSaveData) {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('没有暂存的导入数据。');
        return;
    }

    const allSaves = await this.getSavesFromStorage();
    const existingSave = allSaves[slotId];

    const confirmMessage = existingSave
        ? `确定要用导入的存档 “${this.importedSaveData.save_name}” 覆盖现有存档 “${existingSave.save_name}” 吗？`
        : `确定要将存档 “${this.importedSaveData.save_name}” 导入到这个空槽位吗？`;

    this.showCustomConfirm(confirmMessage, async () => {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('正在写入存档数据...');
        try {
            // 如果是覆盖，先删除旧存档关联的世界书备份
            if (existingSave) {
                await this.deleteLorebookBackup(existingSave);
            }

            const importedData = _.cloneDeep(this.importedSaveData);
            allSaves[slotId] = importedData;
            await AppStorage.saveData('multi_save_data', allSaves);

            this.importedSaveData = null; // 清除临时数据
            this.showTemporaryMessage('存档导入成功！');

            // 【核心修正】使用微小的延迟来刷新UI，避免竞争条件
            setTimeout(() => {
                this.showSaveLoadManager();
            }, 50);

        } catch (error) {
            console.error('执行导入覆盖时出错:', error);
            this.showTemporaryMessage(`导入失败: ${error.message}`);
        }
    });
},

      async promptForSaveName(defaultName) {
              return new Promise((resolve) => {
                  const existingModal = document.getElementById('save-name-prompt-modal');
                  if(existingModal) existingModal.remove();

                  const modal = document.createElement('div');
                  modal.id = 'save-name-prompt-modal';
                  modal.className = 'modal-overlay';
                  modal.style.display = 'flex';
                  modal.style.zIndex = '2000';
                  modal.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="modal-content" style="width: 500px; height: auto; max-height: none;">
                      <div class="modal-header"><h2 class="modal-title">设置存档名称</h2></div>
                      <div class="modal-body" style="padding: 20px;">
                        <p style="margin-bottom: 15px; color: #d2b48c;">为您的存档输入一个名称（留空则使用默认名称）：</p>

                        <input type="text" id="save-name-input" value="" placeholder="${defaultName}"
                               style="width: 100%; padding: 10px; background: rgba(0,0,0,0.5); border: 1px solid #a09c91; color: #f5deb3; border-radius: 4px; font-size: 14px; margin-bottom: 10px;">
                        <div style="font-size:11px; color:#a09c91;">
                          <p>将创建以下世界书备份条目：</p>
                          <ul style="list-style-position: inside; padding-left: 10px;">
                            <li id="preview-journey">${defaultName}-本周目经历</li>
                            <li id="preview-past-lives">${defaultName}-历史的投影</li>
                          </ul>
                        </div>
                        <div style="display: flex; gap: 10px; justify-content: flex-end; margin-top: 20px;">
                          <button id="save-name-cancel" class="interaction-btn">取消</button>
                          <button id="save-name-confirm" class="interaction-btn primary-btn">确认存档</button>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  `;
                  document.querySelector('.guixu-root-container').appendChild(modal);

                  const input = modal.querySelector('#save-name-input');
                  const confirmBtn = modal.querySelector('#save-name-confirm');
                  const cancelBtn = modal.querySelector('#save-name-cancel');
                  const previewJourney = modal.querySelector('#preview-journey');
                  const previewPastLives = modal.querySelector('#preview-past-lives');

                  // 核心修改2：当输入框为空时，预览也使用默认名
                  input.addEventListener('input', () => {
                    const name = input.value.trim() || defaultName;
                    if (previewJourney) previewJourney.textContent = `${name}-本周目经历`;
                    if (previewPastLives) previewPastLives.textContent = `${name}-历史的投影`;
                  });

                  // 核心修改3：如果用户输入为空，则使用默认名进行保存
                  confirmBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    const userInput = input.value.trim();
                    const finalSaveName = userInput || defaultName;
                    modal.remove();
                    resolve(finalSaveName);
                  });

                  cancelBtn.addEventListener('click', () => { modal.remove(); resolve(null); });
                  input.addEventListener('keypress', (e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter') confirmBtn.click(); });
                  setTimeout(() => input.focus(), 100);
              });
          },
    // --- 新增：流式处理函数 ---
handleStreamUpdate(text) {
    // 核心修复：在第一次接收到流式数据时，立即隐藏加载界面
    const overlay = document.getElementById('loading-overlay');
    if (overlay && overlay.style.opacity === '1') { // 检查它是否正完全可见
        this.hideWaitingMessage();
    }

    // 保留原有的文本更新功能
    const gameTextDisplay = document.getElementById('game-text-display');
    if (gameTextDisplay) {
        const displayText = this._getDisplayText(text);
        gameTextDisplay.innerHTML = this.formatMessageContent(displayText);
    }
},

// --- 新增：生成结束处理函数 (已集成最终修复方案) ---
// --- 修改：用这个新版本替换掉旧的 handleStreamEnd 函数 ---
 async handleStreamEnd(finalText) {
 console.log('[handleStreamEnd] 函数已进入！finalText:', finalText);

// 🔴 核心过滤：完全避开标签，用3重特征判断
  // 1. 初始化未完成（INITIALIZING）时的事件，大概率是幽灵事件（重载重放）
  const isInitNotDone = window.GuixuInitState !== 'READY';
  // 2. 文本过短（<30字符），不可能包含有效变量更新
  const isTooShort = !finalText || finalText.length < 30;
  // 3. 非新游戏且无实际变量更新指令（用“=”“：”判断，变量更新必然包含赋值符号）
  const hasValidContent = finalText?.includes('=') || finalText?.includes('：') || finalText?.includes(':');
  const isInvalidContent = !this.isTrueNewGame && !hasValidContent;

  // 三个重过滤任意满足一个，就判定为幽灵事件，直接退出
  if (isInitNotDone || isTooShort || isInvalidContent) {
    console.log('[handleStreamEnd] 过滤幽灵事件：', {
      初始化状态: window.GuixuInitState,
      文本长度: finalText?.length,
      是否有有效内容: hasValidContent
    });
    this.hideWaitingMessage();
    this.isBusy = false;
    return;
  }

 if (!finalText) {
 console.log('[handleStreamEnd] 非流场景：finalText为空');
 this.hideWaitingMessage();
 this.isBusy = false;
  console.log('[handleStreamEnd] finalText为空，未修改任何数据，无需回滚');
 this.showTemporaryMessage('AI未返回有效内容，未执行任何操作');
 return;
 }
    // ================= 流程劫持检查站 开始 =================
    if (this.isSummarizing) {
        console.log('[智能总结器] 已劫持生成结果。');
        this.isSummarizing = false; // 立刻重置标记

        try {
            const summaryText = finalText.trim();
            if (!summaryText) {
                throw new Error('AI未能生成有效的摘要内容。');
            }

            const outputContainer = document.getElementById('summarizer-output-container');
            const footer = document.getElementById('summarizer-footer');
            if (outputContainer && footer) {
                outputContainer.innerHTML = `<textarea id="summarizer-output">${summaryText}</textarea>`;
                footer.innerHTML = `<button id="btn-write-summary" class="interaction-btn primary-btn">写入核心记忆</button>`;

                // 【核心修复2】从“数据中继站”（按钮）上读取暂存的信息
                const generateBtn = document.getElementById('btn-generate-summary');
                const mode = generateBtn.dataset.mode;
                const lastEventId = generateBtn.dataset.lastEventId;

                document.getElementById('btn-write-summary').addEventListener('click', () =>
                    this.writeSummaryToLorebook(mode, lastEventId)
                );
            }
        } catch (e) {
            const outputContainer = document.getElementById('summarizer-output-container');
            if(outputContainer) outputContainer.innerHTML = `<p class="modal-placeholder">生成摘要失败: ${e.message}</p>`;
            document.getElementById('btn-generate-summary').disabled = false;
        }

        return; // 关键：中断后续所有正常的游戏流程！
    }
    // ================= 流程劫持检查站 结束 =================

    await this.loadGachaState();
    console.log('[源堡] 传输结束，开始全局净化与最终处理...');
    const cleanedText = finalText.replace(/<safe>[\s\S]*?<\/safe>/g, '');

     // 角色卡生成逻辑 (不变)
    if (this.pendingCharacterCardGeneration) {
        const charName = this.pendingCharacterCardGeneration;
        const tagName = 'CharacterCard';
        const cardContent = this._extractLastTagContent(tagName, cleanedText);
        if (cardContent) {
            try {
                const bookName = '1源堡';
                const allEntries = await TavernHelper.getLorebookEntries(bookName);
                const targetEntry = allEntries.find(entry => entry.comment === charName);
                if (targetEntry) {
                    await TavernHelper.setLorebookEntries(bookName, [{ uid: targetEntry.uid, content: cardContent }]);
                    this.showTemporaryMessage(`已成功为“${charName}”生成并写入角色卡！`, 3000);
                } else { throw new Error(`未找到名为“${charName}”的世界书条目。`); }
            } catch (error) { this.showTemporaryMessage(`错误：写入“${charName}”的角色卡失败！`, 4000); }
        } else { this.showTemporaryMessage(`警告：AI回复中未找到“${charName}”的角色卡标签，请手动检查。`, 5000); }
        this.pendingCharacterCardGeneration = null;
    }


    const textForValidation = cleanedText.replace(/<thinking>[\s\S]*?<\/thinking>/g, '');
    const validationResult = this.validateAiResponseFormat(textForValidation);

 console.log('[验证] 3.格式检查结果:', validationResult.isValid, '错误信息:', validationResult.errorMessages);
    if (!validationResult.isValid) {
    console.log('[验证] 4.格式检查失败，准备显示模态框', validationResult.errorMessages);
     this.hideWaitingMessage(true);
        const errorListHtml = validationResult.errorMessages.map(e => `<li>${e}</li>`).join('');
        const confirmMessageHtml =
            `<div style="max-height: 45vh; overflow-y: auto; padding: 10px; margin-bottom: 15px; background: rgba(0,0,0,0.2); border-radius: 4px; border: 1px solid rgba(139, 69, 19, 0.3);">` +
            `<p><b>AI回复格式检查失败:</b></p>` +
            `<ul style="margin: 0 0 10px 20px; font-size: 12px; color: #ffb3b3;">${errorListHtml}</ul>` +
            `<p><b>【AI原始回复内容】</b></p>` +
            `<textarea readonly style="width: 98%; height: 200px; background: #1a1a1a; color: #f0f0f0; border: 1px solid #555; font-size: 11px;">${cleanedText.replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;')}</textarea>` +
            `</div>` +
            `<p style="text-align: center;">是否要<b>【确认】</b>回退到行动前的状态？<br><span style="font-size:11px; color:#a09c91;">(选择“取消”将尝试自动修复并应用内容)</span></p>`;

    console.log('[验证] 4.模态框HTML已生成:', confirmMessageHtml);
     this.showCustomConfirm(
            confirmMessageHtml,
            async () => {
                await this.performRollback();
                this.isBusy = false; // 确保在回滚后解锁
            },
            async () => {
                this.showTemporaryMessage('正在尝试自动修复并应用...');
                const fixedText = this._autoFixTags(cleanedText); // 【核心修复】调用修复函数
                await this.processValidResponse(fixedText); // 使用修复后的文本继续流程
            }
        );
    } else {
   console.log('[PC端验证] 格式检查通过，直接执行更新');
     await this.processValidResponse(cleanedText); // 格式正确，直接继续流程
    }
},
 async processValidResponse(responseText) {
  console.log(`%c[处理响应] 开始执行`, 'color: green;');
  // 等待stat_data初始化完成（最多等1秒，避免无限等待）
  const waitForInit = async () => {
    let retry = 0;
    while (!this.isStatInitialized && retry < 10) {
      console.log(`[处理响应] 等待stat_data初始化（${retry}/10）`);
      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 100));
      retry++;
    }
    if (!this.isStatInitialized) {
      console.warn('[处理响应] stat_data初始化超时，使用默认结构');
      this.currentMvuState.stat_data = await this.readInitVarData();
      this.isStatInitialized = true;
    }
  };
  await waitForInit(); // 确保初始化完成后再处理

  try {
    const extractedVar = this._extractLastTagContent('UpdateVariable', responseText, true);
    console.log('[提取结果] extractedVar内容:', extractedVar);
    let cleanedVar = extractedVar ? extractedVar.replace(/<Analysis>[\s\S]*?<\/Analysis>/gi, '').trim() : '';
    this.lastExtractedVariables = extractedVar ? `__UPDATE_VAR__${extractedVar}` : null;
    await this.loadAndDisplayCurrentScene(responseText);

    let modifiedState = null;
    // 1. 第一步：执行变量更新，拿到新状态（同步操作，优先完成）
    if (extractedVar) {
      try {
        modifiedState = await this._applyUpdateFallback(cleanedVar, this.currentMvuState);
      } catch (e) {
        console.error('[自有代码] 执行失败：', e.message);
      }
    }

      // 2. 第二步：锁定新状态（关键：深克隆，避免引用污染）
    let finalState = null;
    if (modifiedState) {
      finalState = _.cloneDeep(modifiedState); // 锁定变量更新后的新值
      console.log('[变量更新完成] 锁定的新状态：', finalState.stat_data);
    } else {
      finalState = _.cloneDeep(this.currentMvuState); // 无更新则用当前状态
    }

    // 3. 第三步：异步补充序列能力（基于锁定的新状态，避免覆盖）
    finalState = await this.updateAcquiredAbilities(finalState);
    console.log('[能力更新完成] 最终状态：', finalState.stat_data);

    // 4. 第四步：将最终状态赋值给全局变量（仅这一次赋值，无多次覆盖）
    this.currentMvuState = _.cloneDeep(finalState);
    console.log('[全局状态锁定] currentMvuState最终值：', this.currentMvuState.stat_data);

    // 5. 渲染UI（基于最终状态，不会回滚）
    this.renderUI(_.cloneDeep(this.currentMvuState.stat_data));
    console.log('[赋值成功] 即将渲染UI！');

    // 6. 渲染变量面板（无副作用）
        if (cleanedVar) {
          const savedErrors = [...this.errorCommands];
          const { patchCommands, formattedPatchText } = this._processJsonPatchCommandsEnhanced(cleanedVar);
          this.errorCommands = savedErrors;
          this.renderVariablePanel(patchCommands, formattedPatchText, cleanedVar);
        }

    // 7. 第五步：执行所有异步存储/同步（基于最终状态，无覆盖）
    if (!this.isTrueNewGame) {
      // 后续回合逻辑：仅读取finalState，不修改
      const messages = await getChatMessages('0');
      if (messages?.[0]) {
        const messageZero = messages[0];
        messageZero.message = responseText;
        finalState.data = finalState.data || {};
        finalState.data.equipped_items = _.cloneDeep(this.equippedItems);
        messageZero.data = finalState;
        await TavernHelper.setChatMessages([messageZero], { refresh: 'force' });
      }

      // 角色/缓存/UI更新（仅后续回合执行）
      if (this.pendingCompanionJoin) {
        this.gachaState.activeCompanions.push(this.pendingCompanionJoin);
        this.saveGachaState();
        this.pendingCompanionJoin = null;
      }
      if (this.isAutoWriteEnabled) {
        if (this.lastExtractedJourney) await this.writeJourneyToLorebook(true);
        if (this.lastExtractedPastLives) await this.writePastLivesToLorebook(true);
      }
      if (this.isNovelModeEnabled && this.lastExtractedNovelText) {
        await this.writeNovelModeToLorebook(true);
      }

      // 【整合】星界之尘+剧场点数 自动增长（基于finalState仅后续回合执行）
      const textTotalLength = (this.lastUserMessage || '').length + responseText.length;
      // 星界之尘：每250字符1点（原有逻辑）
      const dustEarned = Math.floor(textTotalLength / 250);
      // 剧场点数：每2000字符1点（比例更低，体现高维资源稀有性）
      const theaterPointsEarned = Math.floor(textTotalLength / 2000);

      // 统一更新状态+合并提示
      if (dustEarned > 0 || theaterPointsEarned > 0) {
        let messageParts = [];
        // 星界之尘更新
        if (dustEarned > 0) {
          this.gachaState.astralDust += dustEarned;
          this.saveGachaState();
          this.renderSummonTab();
          messageParts.push(`获得 ${dustEarned} 星界之尘`);
        }
        // 剧场点数更新
        if (theaterPointsEarned > 0) {
          finalState.stat_data["剧场点数"] = (finalState.stat_data["剧场点数"] || 0) + theaterPointsEarned;
          this.currentMvuState.stat_data["剧场点数"] = finalState.stat_data["剧场点数"];
          const lastSnap = this.chatHistoryCache[this.chatHistoryCache.length - 1];
          lastSnap.data.stat_data["剧场点数"] = finalState.stat_data["剧场点数"];
          this.syncTheaterPoints();
          messageParts.push(`获得 ${theaterPointsEarned} 剧场点数`);
        }
        // 合并提示（一次弹窗）
        this.showTemporaryMessage(`灵性与高维剧场正在回响... ${messageParts.join('，')}`, 1500);
      }

      this.lastUserMessage = '';
      await this.performAutoSave();
      await this.checkForSummaryReminder();
    } else {
      // 第一回合专属逻辑（基于finalState）
      console.log('[第一回合同步前] 最终状态当前序列：', finalState.stat_data['当前序列']);
      this.chatHistoryCache[0].data = _.cloneDeep(finalState);
      await AppStorage.saveData(this._getHistoryKey(), this.chatHistoryCache);
      try {
        const messages = await getChatMessages('0');
        if (messages && messages.length > 0) {
          const messageZero = messages[0];
          messageZero.data.stat_data = _.cloneDeep(finalState.stat_data);
          await TavernHelper.setChatMessages([messageZero], { refresh: 'force' });
          console.log('[第一回合] 已同步 stat_data 到 messages[0]');
        }
      } catch (e) {
        console.warn('[第一回合] 同步到变量管理器数据源失败:', e);
      }
    }

    // 清理+关闭模态框（通用逻辑，都执行）
    const input = document.getElementById('quick-send-input');
    if (input) input.value = '';
    this.pendingActions = [];
    this.savePendingActions();
    this.closeAllModals();

  } catch (error) {
    this.showTemporaryMessage(`处理响应失败: ${error.message}\n${error.stack || '无堆栈信息'}`);
  console.log(`处理响应失败: ${error.message.slice(0, 50)}`);
 } finally {
    this.hideWaitingMessage();
    this.isBusy = false;
    const isNewGame = this.isTrueNewGame;
    if (!isNewGame && !this.isTrueNewGame) {
      await this._finalizeTurn(responseText); // 基于最终状态生成快照
     }
      this.isTrueNewGame = false;
    }
},


insertVariablePanel() {
  // 找到AI回复展示区（#game-text-display）
  const isMobile = /Mobi|Android|iPhone/i.test(navigator.userAgent);
  const insertDelay = isMobile ? 300 : 100; // 插入延迟（之前有效）
  const bindDelay = isMobile ? 100 : 0; // 绑定延迟（手机端多等100ms解析按钮）
  this.isVariablePanelInitializing = true;
  setTimeout(() => {
    const gameTextDisplay = document.getElementById('game-text-display');
    if (!gameTextDisplay) {
      console.warn('未找到游戏文本展示区，面板未插入');
      return;
    }

  // 面板HTML（保留原始功能，适配现有样式）
  const panelHtml = `
    <div id="variable-panel" style="border: 1px solid #666; border-radius: 4px; padding: 10px; margin: 10px 0; display: none; background: #1a1a1a;">
      <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; margin-bottom: 8px;">
        <h4 style="margin: 0; color: #daa520; font-size: 14px;">本轮AI变量已更新（如果没有变量更新错误，请忽略！）</h4>
        <span id="error-count" style="color: #ff6b6b; font-size: 12px;"></span>
      </div>
      <!-- 原始指令编辑区 -->
      <div style="margin-bottom: 10px;">
        <label style="font-size: 12px; color: #aaa; display: block; margin-bottom: 4px;">原始指令（请只保留更新错误的变量进行更新，以防已更新的变量二次作用）：</label>
        <textarea id="raw-commands" style="width: 100%; min-height: 120px; background: #2a2a2a; color: #f0f0f0; border: 1px solid #555; padding: 6px; font-family: monospace; font-size: 12px; resize: vertical;"></textarea>
      </div>
      <!-- 错误提示区 -->
      <div id="command-errors" style="margin-bottom: 10px; padding: 6px; background: #331a1a; border-radius: 3px; display: none; border: 1px solid #5c2b2b;">
        <div style="font-size: 12px; color: #ff6b6b; margin-bottom: 4px;">检测到AI更新错误（AI流口水了）：</div>
        <ul id="error-list" style="margin: 0; padding-left: 20px; font-size: 12px; color: #ffb3b3;"></ul>
      </div>
      <!-- 操作按钮 -->
      <div style="display: flex; gap: 10px; justify-content: flex-end;">
        <button id="ignore-variables" class="interaction-btn" style="padding: 4px 12px; font-size: 12px;">
          忽略
        </button>
        <button id="reprocess-variables" class="interaction-btn primary-btn" style="padding: 4px 12px; font-size: 12px;">
          再次应用
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  `;
  // 先移除重复面板（避免多面板冲突）
  const existingPanel = document.getElementById('variable-panel');
  if (existingPanel) existingPanel.remove();

  // 插入到 #game-text-display 下方（紧邻AI回复）
  gameTextDisplay.insertAdjacentHTML('afterend', panelHtml);
  console.log(`面板已插入（延迟${insertDelay}ms），开始绑定事件`);
  // 手机端等按钮解析完成再绑定（一轮只绑定一次）
    setTimeout(() => {
      this.initVariablePanelEvents();
      console.log(`一轮事件绑定完成（额外延迟${bindDelay}ms）`);
      this.isVariablePanelInitializing = false;
    }, bindDelay);
  }, insertDelay);
},


initVariablePanelEvents() {

  const isMobile = /Mobi|Android|iPhone/i.test(navigator.userAgent);
  const panel = document.getElementById('variable-panel');
  if (!panel) {
    console.warn('变量编辑器事件绑定：未找到面板');
    return;
  }
  const reprocessBtn = panel.querySelector('#reprocess-variables');
  const ignoreBtn = panel.querySelector('#ignore-variables');
  const rawCommandsEl = panel.querySelector('#raw-commands');
  // 重新应用变量
   if (reprocessBtn && rawCommandsEl) {
    reprocessBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
      const editedScript = rawCommandsEl.value.trim();
      if (!editedScript) {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('请输入有效的变量指令');
        return;
      }

    try {
      // 情况1：无错误 + 有新状态 → 成功保存
      const newState = await this._applyUpdateFallback(editedScript, this.currentMvuState);
      const errorCommands = Array.isArray(this.errorCommands) ? this.errorCommands : [];
      if (newState && errorCommands.length === 0) {
        this.currentMvuState = newState;
        const lastSnapshot = this.chatHistoryCache.at(-1);
        if (lastSnapshot) {
          lastSnapshot.data = _.cloneDeep(this.currentMvuState); // 更新最新快照
          await AppStorage.saveData(this._getHistoryKey(), this.chatHistoryCache); // 持久化
          if (isMobile) await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
          console.log('[手动更新] 已保存到最新快照，ID:', lastSnapshot.message_id);
        }
        this.renderUI(this.currentMvuState.stat_data); // 刷新属性显示
        this.showTemporaryMessage('变量更新成功并已保存至快照！', 3000);
        panel.style.display = 'none'; // 成功后隐藏
      }
        else if (errorCommands.length > 0) {
        this.showTemporaryMessage(`发现 ${errorCommands.length} 条错误指令，请修正后重新应用！`, 3000);
        // 刷新面板错误提示（确保用户看到最新错误）
        const { patchCommands, formattedPatchText } = this._processJsonPatchCommandsEnhanced(editedScript);
        this.renderVariablePanel(patchCommands, formattedPatchText, editedScript);
      }
        // 情况3：无错误但无新状态 → 提示指令无效
      else {
        this.showTemporaryMessage('未检测到有效状态变更，请确认指令是否正确（如路径不存在、值无变化）', 3000);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      this.showTemporaryMessage(`更新失败: ${error.message}，请修正指令后重试`, 3000);
    }
  });
}
  // 忽略本次更新
  if (ignoreBtn) {
    ignoreBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
      panel.style.display = 'none'; // 一轮只隐藏一次
    });
  }
},



// 渲染面板：填充原始指令+错误提示（优化后，支持任何时机调用）
renderVariablePanel(patchCommands, formattedPatchText, originalScript) {
  // 异步等待面板插入，再渲染
  const renderAfterInsert = async () => {
    const isMobile = /Mobi|Android|iPhone/i.test(navigator.userAgent);
    const totalWait = isMobile ? 300 + 100 + 50 : 100 + 50; // 插入300+绑定100+缓冲50（手机端）
    let panel = document.getElementById('variable-panel');

    // 情况1：面板未找到，先插入（支持任何场景下的调用）
    if (!panel) {
      console.log('面板未找到，触发插入...');
      this.insertVariablePanel(); // 调用插入函数（带100ms延迟）

      // 等待总延迟，确保面板+按钮都就绪
      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, totalWait));
      panel = document.getElementById('variable-panel');

      // 极端情况：插入失败，提示用户
      if (!panel) {
        console.error('面板插入失败，无法渲染');
        this.showTemporaryMessage('变量面板加载失败，请重试', 3000);
        return;
      }
    }
