    // 情况2：面板已存在，直接获取子元素
    const rawCommandsEl = document.getElementById('raw-commands');
    const errorCountEl = document.getElementById('error-count');
    const errorContainerEl = document.getElementById('command-errors');
    const errorListEl = document.getElementById('error-list');

    // 容错：子元素缺失时提示
    if (!rawCommandsEl || !errorCountEl || !errorContainerEl || !errorListEl) {
      console.error('面板子元素缺失');
      return;
    }

    // 填充指令和错误提示
    rawCommandsEl.value = originalScript || '';
    const errorCommands = Array.isArray(this.errorCommands) ? this.errorCommands : [];


    if (errorCommands.length > 0) {
      errorCountEl.textContent = `发现 ${errorCommands.length} 处错误`;
      errorListEl.innerHTML = errorCommands.map(err => `<li>${err}</li>`).join('');
      errorContainerEl.style.display = 'block';
    } else {
      errorCountEl.textContent = '';
      errorContainerEl.style.display = 'none';
    }

    // 强制显示面板
    panel.style.display = 'block';

    // 同步到悬浮编辑器（如果存在且用户未编辑）
    if (floatingEditorInstance && originalScript) {
      const floatingTextarea = document.getElementById('floating-editor-textarea');
      // 仅当悬浮编辑器为空或无未保存更改时自动同步
      if (floatingTextarea && (!floatingTextarea.value.trim() || !floatingEditorInstance.hasUnsavedChanges)) {
        floatingEditorInstance.setCommands(originalScript);
        floatingEditorInstance.hasUnsavedChanges = false; // 自动同步不算未保存更改
        console.log('[变量面板] 已同步指令到悬浮编辑器');
      }
    }
  };

  // 执行渲染逻辑
  renderAfterInsert();
}





 };


// ==================== 悬浮变量编辑器 ====================
// 提供随时可访问的变量编辑功能，不受AI回合限制
class FloatingVariableEditor {
  constructor(gameInstance) {
    this.game = gameInstance;
    this.isVisible = false;
    this.isMinimized = false;
    this.position = { x: 20, y: 100 };
    this.isDragging = false;
    this.dragOffset = { x: 0, y: 0 };
    this.panel = null;
    this.toggleBtn = null;
    this.hasUnsavedChanges = false;

    // 状态模型
    this.EditorStateModel = {
      STORAGE_KEY: 'floating-editor-state',
      defaultState: {
        isVisible: false,
        isMinimized: false,
        position: { x: 20, y: 100 }
      },
      serialize: (state) => JSON.stringify(state),
      deserialize: (json) => {
        try {
          return JSON.parse(json);
        } catch {
          return this.EditorStateModel.defaultState;
        }
      }
    };

    // 位置约束
    this.PositionConstraints = {
      MIN_MARGIN: 10,
      constrain: (position, panelSize, viewportSize) => {
        return {
          x: Math.max(this.PositionConstraints.MIN_MARGIN,
             Math.min(position.x, viewportSize.width - panelSize.width - this.PositionConstraints.MIN_MARGIN)),
          y: Math.max(this.PositionConstraints.MIN_MARGIN,
             Math.min(position.y, viewportSize.height - panelSize.height - this.PositionConstraints.MIN_MARGIN))
        };
      }
    };
  }

  // 生成切换按钮HTML
  generateToggleButtonHtml() {
    return `
      <button id="floating-editor-toggle" style="
        position: fixed;
        right: 20px;
        bottom: 80px;
        width: 48px;
        height: 48px;
        border-radius: 50%;
        background: linear-gradient(135deg, #daa520, #b8860b);
        border: 2px solid #ffd700;
        color: #1a1a1a;
        font-size: 20px;
        cursor: pointer;
        z-index: 9998;
        box-shadow: 0 4px 12px rgba(218, 165, 32, 0.4);
        transition: all 0.3s ease;
        display: flex;
        align-items: center;
        justify-content: center;
      " title="悬浮变量编辑器">
        ⚙
      </button>
    `;
  }

  // 生成面板HTML
  generatePanelHtml() {
    return `
      <div id="floating-editor-panel" style="
        position: fixed;
        left: ${this.position.x}px;
        top: ${this.position.y}px;
        width: 360px;
        background: #1a1a1a;
        border: 1px solid #daa520;
        border-radius: 8px;
        box-shadow: 0 8px 32px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.6);
        z-index: 9999;
        display: none;
        font-family: inherit;
      ">
        <!-- 标题栏 -->
        <div id="floating-editor-header" style="
          display: flex;
          justify-content: space-between;
          align-items: center;
          padding: 10px 12px;
          background: linear-gradient(135deg, #2a2a2a, #1a1a1a);
          border-bottom: 1px solid #444;
          border-radius: 8px 8px 0 0;
          cursor: move;
          user-select: none;
        ">
          <span style="color: #daa520; font-weight: bold; font-size: 14px;">⚙ 悬浮变量编辑器</span>
          <div style="display: flex; gap: 8px;">
            <button id="floating-editor-minimize" style="
              background: none;
              border: none;
              color: #aaa;
              font-size: 16px;
              cursor: pointer;
              padding: 2px 6px;
              border-radius: 3px;
              transition: all 0.2s;
            " title="最小化">─</button>
            <button id="floating-editor-close" style="
              background: none;
              border: none;
              color: #aaa;
              font-size: 16px;
              cursor: pointer;
              padding: 2px 6px;
              border-radius: 3px;
              transition: all 0.2s;
            " title="关闭">✕</button>
          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- 内容区 -->
        <div id="floating-editor-content" style="padding: 12px;">
          <label style="font-size: 12px; color: #aaa; display: block; margin-bottom: 6px;">
            变量指令：
          </label>
          <textarea id="floating-editor-textarea" style="
            width: 100%;
            min-height: 150px;
            background: #2a2a2a;
            color: #f0f0f0;
            border: 1px solid #555;
            border-radius: 4px;
            padding: 8px;
            font-family: 'Consolas', 'Monaco', monospace;
            font-size: 12px;
            resize: vertical;
            box-sizing: border-box;
          " placeholder="输入JSON Patch指令，例如：&#10;[{&quot;op&quot;:&quot;replace&quot;,&quot;path&quot;:&quot;/当前活力&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:100}]&#10;[{&quot;op&quot;:&quot;replace&quot;,&quot;path&quot;:&quot;/人物关系列表/小红/好感度&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:50}]"></textarea>

          <!-- 错误显示区 -->
          <div id="floating-editor-errors" style="
            display: none;
            margin-top: 8px;
            padding: 8px;
            background: #331a1a;
            border: 1px solid #5c2b2b;
            border-radius: 4px;
          ">
            <div style="font-size: 12px; color: #ff6b6b; margin-bottom: 4px;">检测到错误：</div>
            <ul id="floating-editor-error-list" style="
              margin: 0;
              padding-left: 20px;
              font-size: 12px;
              color: #ffb3b3;
            "></ul>
          </div>

          <!-- 操作按钮 -->
          <div style="display: flex; gap: 10px; justify-content: flex-end; margin-top: 12px;">
            <button id="floating-editor-sync" class="interaction-btn" style="
              padding: 6px 12px;
              font-size: 12px;
              background: #333;
              border: 1px solid #555;
              color: #aaa;
            " title="从原面板同步指令">同步</button>
            <button id="floating-editor-clear" class="interaction-btn" style="
              padding: 6px 12px;
              font-size: 12px;
              background: #333;
              border: 1px solid #555;
              color: #aaa;
            ">清空</button>
            <button id="floating-editor-apply" class="interaction-btn primary-btn" style="
              padding: 6px 12px;
              font-size: 12px;
            ">应用变量</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  // 初始化
  init() {
    // 加载保存的状态
    this.loadState();

    // 插入HTML到游戏根容器内（确保全屏模式下可见）
    const rootContainer = document.querySelector('.guixu-root-container') || document.body;
    rootContainer.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', this.generateToggleButtonHtml());
    rootContainer.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', this.generatePanelHtml());

    // 获取DOM引用
    this.toggleBtn = document.getElementById('floating-editor-toggle');
    this.panel = document.getElementById('floating-editor-panel');

    // 应用保存的位置
    if (this.panel) {
      this.panel.style.left = `${this.position.x}px`;
      this.panel.style.top = `${this.position.y}px`;
    }

    // 绑定事件
    this.bindEvents();

    // 恢复可见状态
    if (this.isVisible) {
      this.show();
      if (this.isMinimized) {
        this.minimize();
      }
    }

    console.log('[FloatingEditor] 悬浮变量编辑器初始化完成');
  }

  // 切换显示/隐藏
  toggle() {
    this.isVisible = !this.isVisible;
    if (this.isVisible) {
      this.show();
    } else {
      this.hide();
    }
    this.saveState();
  }

  // 显示面板
  show() {
    if (this.panel) {
      this.panel.style.display = 'block';
      this.isVisible = true;
      this.constrainToViewport();
    }
  }

  // 隐藏面板
  hide() {
    if (this.panel) {
      this.panel.style.display = 'none';
      this.isVisible = false;
    }
  }

  // 最小化
  minimize() {
    const content = this.panel?.querySelector('#floating-editor-content');
    const minBtn = this.panel?.querySelector('#floating-editor-minimize');
    if (content && minBtn) {
      content.style.display = 'none';
      minBtn.textContent = '□';
      minBtn.title = '展开';
      this.isMinimized = true;
      this.saveState();
    }
  }

  // 展开
  expand() {
    const content = this.panel?.querySelector('#floating-editor-content');
    const minBtn = this.panel?.querySelector('#floating-editor-minimize');
    if (content && minBtn) {
      content.style.display = 'block';
      minBtn.textContent = '─';
      minBtn.title = '最小化';
      this.isMinimized = false;
      this.saveState();
    }
  }

  // 开始拖拽
  startDrag(e) {
    if (e.target.closest('button') || e.target.closest('textarea')) return;

    this.isDragging = true;
    const rect = this.panel.getBoundingClientRect();
    const clientX = e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
    const clientY = e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientY : e.clientY;

    this.dragOffset = {
      x: clientX - rect.left,
      y: clientY - rect.top
    };

    e.preventDefault();
  }

  // 拖拽中
  onDrag(e) {
    if (!this.isDragging) return;

    const clientX = e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
    const clientY = e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientY : e.clientY;

    this.position = {
      x: clientX - this.dragOffset.x,
      y: clientY - this.dragOffset.y
    };

    this.constrainToViewport();

    this.panel.style.left = `${this.position.x}px`;
    this.panel.style.top = `${this.position.y}px`;
  }

  // 结束拖拽
  endDrag() {
    if (this.isDragging) {
      this.isDragging = false;
      this.saveState();
    }
  }

  // 约束到视口内
  constrainToViewport() {
    if (!this.panel) return;

    const rect = this.panel.getBoundingClientRect();
    const viewport = {
      width: window.innerWidth,
      height: window.innerHeight
    };
    const panelSize = {
      width: rect.width,
      height: rect.height
    };

    this.position = this.PositionConstraints.constrain(this.position, panelSize, viewport);
    this.panel.style.left = `${this.position.x}px`;
    this.panel.style.top = `${this.position.y}px`;
  }

  // 获取指令
  getCommands() {
    const textarea = this.panel?.querySelector('#floating-editor-textarea');
    return textarea?.value || '';
  }

  // 设置指令
  setCommands(commands) {
    const textarea = this.panel?.querySelector('#floating-editor-textarea');
    if (textarea) {
      textarea.value = commands;
      this.hasUnsavedChanges = true;
    }
  }

  // 清空指令
  clearCommands(skipConfirm = false) {
    const textarea = this.panel?.querySelector('#floating-editor-textarea');
    if (!textarea) return;

    if (!skipConfirm && textarea.value.trim() && this.hasUnsavedChanges) {
      if (!confirm('确定要清空编辑器内容吗？未应用的更改将丢失。')) {
        return;
      }
    }

    textarea.value = '';
    this.hasUnsavedChanges = false;
    this.hideErrors();
  }

  // 从原面板同步
  syncFromPanel() {
    const originalTextarea = document.querySelector('#raw-commands');
    if (originalTextarea && originalTextarea.value.trim()) {
      this.setCommands(originalTextarea.value);
      this.game.showTemporaryMessage('已从原面板同步指令', 2000);
    } else {
      this.game.showTemporaryMessage('原面板无可同步的指令', 2000);
    }
  }

  // 应用指令（支持历史回合编辑）
  async applyCommands() {
    const commands = this.getCommands().trim();
    if (!commands) {
      this.game.showTemporaryMessage('请输入有效的变量指令', 2000);
      return;
    }

    const isMobile = /Mobi|Android|iPhone/i.test(navigator.userAgent);

    // 判断是否在历史浏览模式，确定目标快照索引
    const isHistoryMode = this.game.isHistoryViewMode;
    const targetIndex = isHistoryMode
        ? this.game.historyViewIndex
        : this.game.chatHistoryCache.length - 1;

    // 获取目标快照
    const targetSnapshot = this.game.chatHistoryCache[targetIndex];
    if (!targetSnapshot) {
      this.game.showTemporaryMessage('未找到目标快照', 2000);
      return;
    }

    // 使用目标快照的数据作为基础状态
    const baseState = targetSnapshot.data
        ? _.cloneDeep(targetSnapshot.data)
        : _.cloneDeep(this.game.currentMvuState);

    try {
      const newState = await this.game._applyUpdateFallback(commands, baseState);
      const errorCommands = Array.isArray(this.game.errorCommands) ? this.game.errorCommands : [];

      if (newState && errorCommands.length === 0) {
        // 保存到目标快照
        targetSnapshot.data = _.cloneDeep(newState);
        await AppStorage.saveData(this.game._getHistoryKey(), this.game.chatHistoryCache);
        if (isMobile) await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));

        // 如果是当前回合（非历史模式），同步更新currentMvuState
        if (!isHistoryMode) {
          this.game.currentMvuState = newState;
        }

        // 刷新UI（使用新状态）
        this.game.renderUI(newState.stat_data);

        // 提示信息区分历史/当前
        const msg = isHistoryMode
            ? `历史回合 ${targetIndex + 1} 的变量已更新！`
            : '变量更新成功并已保存！';
        this.showSuccess(msg);
        console.log(`[FloatingEditor] 已保存到快照 [${targetIndex + 1}/${this.game.chatHistoryCache.length}]${isHistoryMode ? ' (历史模式)' : ''}`);

        this.hasUnsavedChanges = false;
        this.hideErrors();

      } else if (errorCommands.length > 0) {
        this.showErrors(errorCommands);
        this.game.showTemporaryMessage(`发现 ${errorCommands.length} 条错误指令，请修正`, 3000);

      } else {
        this.game.showTemporaryMessage('未检测到有效状态变更，请确认指令是否正确', 3000);
      }

    } catch (error) {
      this.showErrors([error.message]);
      this.game.showTemporaryMessage(`更新失败: ${error.message}`, 3000);
    }
  }

  // 显示错误
  showErrors(errors) {
    const container = this.panel?.querySelector('#floating-editor-errors');
    const list = this.panel?.querySelector('#floating-editor-error-list');

    if (!container || !list) return;

    if (errors.length === 0) {
      container.style.display = 'none';
      return;
    }

    list.innerHTML = errors.map(err => `<li>${err}</li>`).join('');
    container.style.display = 'block';
  }

  // 隐藏错误
  hideErrors() {
    const container = this.panel?.querySelector('#floating-editor-errors');
    if (container) {
      container.style.display = 'none';
    }
  }

  // 显示成功
  showSuccess(message) {
    this.game.showTemporaryMessage(message, 3000);
  }

  // 保存状态
  saveState() {
    try {
      const state = {
        isVisible: this.isVisible,
        isMinimized: this.isMinimized,
        position: this.position
      };
      localStorage.setItem(this.EditorStateModel.STORAGE_KEY, this.EditorStateModel.serialize(state));
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn('[FloatingEditor] 保存状态失败:', e);
    }
  }

  // 加载状态
  loadState() {
    try {
      const saved = localStorage.getItem(this.EditorStateModel.STORAGE_KEY);
      if (saved) {
        const state = this.EditorStateModel.deserialize(saved);
        this.isVisible = state.isVisible ?? false;
        this.isMinimized = state.isMinimized ?? false;
        this.position = state.position ?? { x: 20, y: 100 };
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.warn('[FloatingEditor] 加载状态失败:', e);
    }
  }

  // 绑定事件
  bindEvents() {
    // 切换按钮
    this.toggleBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => this.toggle());

    // 关闭按钮
    this.panel?.querySelector('#floating-editor-close')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
      this.hide();
      this.saveState();
    });

    // 最小化按钮
    this.panel?.querySelector('#floating-editor-minimize')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
      if (this.isMinimized) {
        this.expand();
      } else {
        this.minimize();
      }
    });

    // 清空按钮
    this.panel?.querySelector('#floating-editor-clear')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
      this.clearCommands();
    });

    // 同步按钮
    this.panel?.querySelector('#floating-editor-sync')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
      this.syncFromPanel();
    });

    // 应用按钮
    this.panel?.querySelector('#floating-editor-apply')?.addEventListener('click', () => {
      this.applyCommands();
    });

    // 拖拽事件 - 鼠标
    const header = this.panel?.querySelector('#floating-editor-header');
    if (header) {
      header.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
        // 排除按钮点击
        if (e.target.closest('button')) return;
        this.startDrag(e);
      });
    }
    document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
      if (this.isDragging) this.onDrag(e);
    });
    document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => {
      if (this.isDragging) this.endDrag();
    });

    // 拖拽事件 - 触摸
    if (header) {
      header.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => {
        if (e.target.closest('button')) return;
        this.startDrag(e);
      }, { passive: false });
    }
    document.addEventListener('touchmove', (e) => {
      if (this.isDragging) this.onDrag(e);
    }, { passive: false });
    document.addEventListener('touchend', () => {
      if (this.isDragging) this.endDrag();
    });

    // 窗口调整
    window.addEventListener('resize', () => this.handleResize());

    // 文本变化追踪
    this.panel?.querySelector('#floating-editor-textarea')?.addEventListener('input', () => {
      this.hasUnsavedChanges = true;
    });

    // 按钮悬停效果
    this.toggleBtn?.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
      this.toggleBtn.style.transform = 'scale(1.1)';
    });
    this.toggleBtn?.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
      this.toggleBtn.style.transform = 'scale(1)';
    });
  }

  // 处理窗口调整
  handleResize() {
    if (this.isVisible) {
      this.constrainToViewport();
    }
  }

  // 设置启用/禁用状态
  setEnabled(enabled) {
    if (enabled) {
      // 显示切换按钮
      if (this.toggleBtn) {
        this.toggleBtn.style.display = 'flex';
      }
    } else {
      // 隐藏切换按钮和面板
      if (this.toggleBtn) {
        this.toggleBtn.style.display = 'none';
      }
      this.hide();
    }
  }
}

// 全局悬浮编辑器实例
let floatingEditorInstance = null;

      "当前区域": "未知",
      "当前地标": "未知",
      "当前坐标": { x: 50.0, y: 50.0 } // 默认地图中心

  }

  // 初始化DOM绑定和事件（点击地图按钮后执行）
  initDomAndEvents() {
    if (this.isInitialized) return;
    this.isInitialized = true;

    // 绑定DOM元素
    this.mapModal = document.getElementById("map-modal");
    this.closeMap = document.getElementById("close-map");
    this.zoomIn = document.getElementById("zoom-in");
    this.zoomOut = document.getElementById("zoom-out");
    this.resetMap = document.getElementById("reset-map");
    this.mapViewport = document.getElementById("map-viewport");
    this.mapPannable = document.getElementById("map-pannable");
    this.mapLocations = document.getElementById("map-locations");

    // 绑定事件
    this.closeMap.addEventListener("click", () => this.hideMap());
    this.zoomIn.addEventListener("click", () => this.zoom(0.2));
    this.zoomOut.addEventListener("click", () => this.zoom(-0.2));
    this.resetMap.addEventListener("click", () => this.resetView());
    this.bindDragEvents();
    this.bindWheelZoom();
    this.bindPinchZoom();
  }

  // 显示地图时接收玩家状态数据
  showMap() { // 移除 statData 参数，无需外部传入
  this.initDomAndEvents();
  if (this.mapModal) {
    this.mapModal.style.display = 'flex';

    //console.log('[地图调试] 直接读 GuixuManager 内部数据:', GuixuManager.currentMvuState);
    // 主动获取主内存中的最新状态数据
    const latestStatData = GuixuManager.currentMvuState?.stat_data || {};
    // 强制更新当前状态（覆盖缓存，确保是最新值）
    this.currentStatData = {
      ...this.currentStatData,
      ...latestStatData
    };
    //console.log(`[地图主动拉取] 显示地图时获取最新坐标:`, latestStatData["当前坐标"]);
    this.renderMap();
    this.renderPlayerMarker(); // 此时渲染用的是最新数据
  }
}


  // 隐藏地图
  hideMap() {
  if (this.mapModal) {
    // 与其他弹窗保持一致：用display: none隐藏
    this.mapModal.style.display = 'none';
  }
}


  // 渲染地图区域和地标
  renderMap() {
  this.mapLocations.innerHTML = "";

  // 设置与地图宽高比一致的viewBox
  const MAP_WIDTH = 7400;  // 替换为你地图的实际宽度
  const MAP_HEIGHT = 3800; // 替换为你地图的实际高度
  const aspectRatio = MAP_WIDTH / MAP_HEIGHT;
  const viewBoxWidth = 100;
  const viewBoxHeight = viewBoxWidth / aspectRatio;

  // 正确创建SVG容器（需传入元素名称"svg"）
  const svg = document.createElementNS("http://www.w3.org/2000/svg", "svg");
  svg.setAttribute("width", "100%");
  svg.setAttribute("height", "100%");
  svg.setAttribute("viewBox", "0 0 100 51.35");

  this.DEFAULT_LOCATIONS.mainRegions.forEach(region => {
    const polygon = document.createElementNS("http://www.w3.org/2000/svg", "polygon");
    polygon.setAttribute("class", "main-region-poly");
    polygon.setAttribute("points", region.points.outer.map(p => `${p.x} ${p.y}`).join(' '));
    polygon.setAttribute("style", `--region-fill: ${region.style.fill}; --region-stroke: ${region.style.stroke}`);
    polygon.setAttribute("data-id", region.id);
    polygon.setAttribute("data-name", region.name);

    const label = document.createElementNS("http://www.w3.org/2000/svg", "text");
    label.setAttribute("class", "region-label");
    label.setAttribute("x", this.getCenterX(region.points.outer));
    label.setAttribute("y", this.getCenterY(region.points.outer));
    label.setAttribute("text-anchor", "middle");
    label.textContent = region.name;

    svg.appendChild(polygon);
    svg.appendChild(label);
  });

  this.mapLocations.appendChild(svg);

  this.DEFAULT_LOCATIONS.landmarks.forEach(landmark => {
    const dot = document.createElement("div");
    dot.className = "landmark-dot";
    dot.style.top = landmark.marker.top;
    dot.style.left = landmark.marker.left;
    dot.setAttribute("data-name", landmark.name);
    dot.setAttribute("data-description", landmark.description);
    this.mapLocations.appendChild(dot);

    const label = document.createElement("div");
    label.className = "landmark-label";
    label.style.top = landmark.marker.top;
    label.style.left = landmark.marker.left;
    label.textContent = landmark.name;
    this.mapLocations.appendChild(label);
  });

  this.updateLOD();
}

  // 【渲染玩家位置标记】
  renderPlayerMarker() {

    // 从当前状态获取位置信息（兼容未定义的情况）
    const {
      "当前区域": currentRegion,
      "当前地标": currentLandmark,
      "当前坐标": currentCoord
    } = this.currentStatData;

    //console.log(`[渲染日志] 原始坐标：`, currentCoord);
    // 坐标兜底（默认地图中心）
    const coord = currentCoord || { x: 50.0, y: 50.0 };
    // 标记文本（未知区域时显示“未知位置”）
    const markerText = currentRegion === "未知" ? "未知位置" : currentLandmark || currentRegion;

    //const scaledY = coord.y * this.Y_SCALE;

    // 移除旧标记（避免重复）
    const oldMarker = this.mapLocations.querySelector("#map-locations .map-location-marker.current-location");
    if (oldMarker) oldMarker.remove();


    const visualY = coord.y /  GuixuManager.Y_SCALE; // 逻辑y → 视觉y
    const leftStyle = `${coord.x}%`;
    const topStyle = `${visualY}%`;

    // 创建新标记
    const marker = document.createElement("div");
    marker.className = "map-location-marker current-location"; // 用于CSS样式和选择器
    // 定位（基于百分比坐标）
    marker.style.position = "absolute";
    marker.style.left = leftStyle;
    marker.style.top = topStyle;
    marker.style.transform = "translate(-50%, -50%)"; // 中心点对齐
    //console.log(`[渲染日志] 应用的样式：left=${leftStyle}, top=${topStyle}`);
    // 样式内容（可通过CSS自定义）
    marker.innerHTML = `
    <div class="dot"></div>
    <div class="label">${markerText}</div>
  `;

    // 添加到地图容器
    this.mapLocations.appendChild(marker);
  }

  // 【更新玩家状态数据（从_applyUpdateFallback调用）】
  updateStatData(statData) {
    if (!statData) return;
    // 更新缓存的状态
    this.currentStatData = {
      ...this.currentStatData,
      ...statData
    };
    // 如果地图正在显示，实时更新标记
    if (this.mapModal && this.mapModal.style.display === "flex") {
      this.renderPlayerMarker();
    }
  }


  // 计算多边形中心
  getCenterX(points) {
    const xs = points.map(p => p.x);
    return (Math.min(...xs) + Math.max(...xs)) / 2;
  }
  getCenterY(points) {
    const ys = points.map(p => p.y);
    return (Math.min(...ys) + Math.max(...ys)) / 2;
  }

  // 缩放
  zoom(delta) {
    const newScale = this.state.scale + delta;
    if (newScale >= 0.5 && newScale <= 5.0) {
      this.state.scale = newScale;
      this.updateTransform();
      this.updateLOD();
    }
  }

  // 重置视图
  resetView() {
    this.state = { scale: 1.0, x: 0, y: 0 };
    this.updateTransform();
    this.updateLOD();
  }

  // 更新变换
  updateTransform() {
  const viewport = this.mapViewport;
  const cx = viewport.clientWidth / 2;
  const cy = viewport.clientHeight / 2;

  // 变换原点设为视口中心
  this.mapPannable.style.transformOrigin = `${cx}px ${cy}px`;
  // 应用位移和缩放
  this.mapPannable.style.transform = `translate(${this.state.x}px, ${this.state.y}px) scale(${this.state.scale})`;
}

  // 拖拽事件
  bindDragEvents() {
  let isDragging = false;
  let startX, startY;
  let isTouchDrag = false; // 标记是否为触摸拖拽

  // 触摸开始（单指）
  this.mapPannable.addEventListener("touchstart", (e) => {
    if (e.touches.length === 1) { // 仅单指时触发拖拽
      isDragging = true;
      isTouchDrag = true;
      const touch = e.touches[0];
      startX = touch.clientX - this.state.x;
      startY = touch.clientY - this.state.y;
      this.mapPannable.style.cursor = "grabbing";
    }
  });

  // 鼠标开始
  this.mapPannable.addEventListener("mousedown", (e) => {
    isDragging = true;
    isTouchDrag = false;
    startX = e.clientX - this.state.x;
    startY = e.clientY - this.state.y;
    this.mapPannable.style.cursor = "grabbing";
  });

  // 触摸移动（单指）
  document.addEventListener("touchmove", (e) => {
    if (!isDragging || !isTouchDrag || e.touches.length !== 1) return;
    e.preventDefault();
    const touch = e.touches[0];
    this.state.x = touch.clientX - startX;
    this.state.y = touch.clientY - startY;
    this.updateTransform();
  });

  // 鼠标移动
  document.addEventListener("mousemove", (e) => {
    if (!isDragging || isTouchDrag) return;
    this.state.x = e.clientX - startX;
    this.state.y = e.clientY - startY;
    this.updateTransform();
  });

  // 触摸结束
  document.addEventListener("touchend", (e) => {
    if (isTouchDrag) {
      isDragging = false;
      isTouchDrag = false;
      this.mapPannable.style.cursor = "grab";
    }
  });

  // 鼠标结束
  document.addEventListener("mouseup", () => {
    if (!isTouchDrag) {
      isDragging = false;
      this.mapPannable.style.cursor = "grab";
    }
  });
  }

  // 滚轮缩放
  bindWheelZoom() {
    this.mapViewport.addEventListener("wheel", (e) => {
      e.preventDefault();
      const delta = e.deltaY < 0 ? 0.2 : -0.2;
      this.zoom(delta);
    });
  }

  // 双指缩放
  bindPinchZoom() {
  let isPinching = false;
  let initialDistance = 0;
  let initialScale = 1.0;

  // 触摸开始：判断是否双指，记录初始距离和缩放
  this.mapViewport.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => {
    if (e.touches.length === 2) {
      isPinching = true;
      initialDistance = this.getDistance(e.touches[0], e.touches[1]);
      initialScale = this.state.scale;
    }
  });

  // 触摸移动：计算当前距离，更新缩放
  this.mapViewport.addEventListener('touchmove', (e) => {
    if (!isPinching || e.touches.length !== 2) return;
    e.preventDefault(); // 阻止页面默认缩放/滚动

    const currentDistance = this.getDistance(e.touches[0], e.touches[1]);
    const scaleFactor = currentDistance / initialDistance;
    const newScale = initialScale * scaleFactor;

    // 限制缩放范围（与现有zoom逻辑保持一致）
    if (newScale >= 0.5 && newScale <= 5.0) {
      this.state.scale = newScale;
      this.updateTransform();
      this.updateLOD();
    }
  });

  // 触摸结束：重置状态
  this.mapViewport.addEventListener('touchend', (e) => {
    if (e.touches.length === 0) {
      isPinching = false;
    }
  });
  }

// 辅助函数：计算两点间距离
  getDistance(touch1, touch2) {
  const dx = touch1.clientX - touch2.clientX;
  const dy = touch1.clientY - touch2.clientY;
  return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
  }

  // LOD控制
  updateLOD() {
    const scale = this.state.scale;

    const inverseScale = 1 / scale;

    // 同步地标缩放
  document.querySelectorAll('#map-locations .landmark-dot, #map-locations .landmark-label').forEach(el => {
    el.style.setProperty('--landmark-scale', inverseScale);
  });

  // 同步玩家标记缩放
  document.querySelectorAll('#map-locations .map-location-marker.current-location').forEach(marker => {
    marker.style.setProperty('--player-scale', inverseScale);
  });

    // 区域标签
    document.querySelectorAll(".region-label").forEach(label => {
      const isSubRegion = false;
      const config = isSubRegion ?
        {minScale: 2.0, maxScale: Infinity} :
        {minScale: 0.5, maxScale: 5.0};
      label.classList.toggle("hidden", !(scale >= config.minScale && scale <= config.maxScale));
    });

    // 地标
    document.querySelectorAll(".landmark-dot").forEach(dot => {
      const label = dot.nextElementSibling;
      dot.classList.toggle("hidden", !(scale >= 0 && scale <= Infinity));
      if (label) {
        label.classList.toggle("hidden", !(scale >= 1.2 && scale <= Infinity));
      }
    });

    // 【玩家标记随缩放显示/隐藏】
    const playerMarker = document.querySelector(".player-marker");
    if (playerMarker) {
      // 缩放小于0.5时隐藏标签（保持点可见）
      const markerLabel = playerMarker.querySelector("div:last-child");
      if (markerLabel) {
        markerLabel.classList.toggle("hidden", scale < 0.5);
      }
    }
  }
}



const MapEarthTool = {
  // 地球级比例尺配置（常量）
  EARTH_CONFIG: {
    mapScaleKm: 40075, // 地球赤道周长（地图横向对应赤道）
    earthTotalArea: 510072000 // 地球总表面积(km²)，用于校验
  },
  // 计算区域实际面积
  calculatePolygonArea: (pointsData) => {
    let points = [];
    // 兼容不同格式的points数据
    if (pointsData?.outer) {
      points = pointsData.outer;
    } else if (Array.isArray(pointsData) && pointsData[0]?.outer) {
      points = pointsData[0].outer;
    } else if (Array.isArray(pointsData)) {
      points = pointsData;
    }
    if (points.length < 3) return 0;

    // 鞋带公式计算百分比面积
    const area = points.reduce((acc, p1, i) => {
      const p2 = points[(i + 1) % points.length];
      return acc + (p1.x * p2.y - p2.x * p1.y);
    }, 0);
    const percentageArea = Math.abs(area / 2);

    // 获取地图宽高比
    const mapImg = document.getElementById('map-image');
    const aspectRatio = mapImg && mapImg.naturalWidth > 0 && mapImg.naturalHeight > 0
      ? mapImg.naturalHeight / mapImg.naturalWidth
      : 7400 / 3800; // 地图原始宽高比

    // 换算成地球级实际面积
    const { mapScaleKm } = MapEarthTool.EARTH_CONFIG;
    return (percentageArea / (100 * 100)) * mapScaleKm * (mapScaleKm / aspectRatio);
  }
};

const GeometryHelper = {
  /**
   * 判断点是否在多边形内（射线法）
   * @param {Object} point - {x,y} 待判断坐标
   * @param {Array} polygon - 多边形顶点数组 [{x,y},...]
   */
  isPointInPolygon: (point, polygon) => {
    let inside = false;
    const x = point.x;
    const y = point.y;
    for (let i = 0, j = polygon.length - 1; i < polygon.length; j = i++) {
      const xi = polygon[i].x;
      const yi = polygon[i].y;
      const xj = polygon[j].x;
      const yj = polygon[j].y;
      const intersect = ((yi > y) !== (yj > y)) && (x < (xj - xi) * (y - yi) / (yj - yi) + xi);
      if (intersect) inside = !inside;
    }
    return inside;
  },

  /**
   * 将点修正到多边形边缘（超出时拉回最近边缘）
   * @param {Object} point - 异常坐标
   * @param {Array} polygon - 目标多边形顶点
   */
  getClampedPointToPolygon: (point, polygon) => {
    const x = point.x;
    const y = point.y;
    const xs = polygon.map(p => p.x);
    const ys = polygon.map(p => p.y);
    const minX = Math.min(...xs);
    const maxX = Math.max(...xs);
    const minY = Math.min(...ys);
    const maxY = Math.max(...ys);

    // 情况1：点在x范围外 → 修正到x边界，y保持原比例
    if (x < minX || x > maxX) {
      const targetX = x < minX ? minX : maxX;
      const yRatio = (y - minY) / (maxY - minY) || 0.5;
      const targetY = minY + yRatio * (maxY - minY);
      return { x: targetX, y: targetY };
    }
    // 情况2：点在y范围外 → 修正到y边界，x保持原比例
    if (y < minY || y > maxY) {
      const targetY = y < minY ? minY : maxY;
      const xRatio = (x - minX) / (maxX - minX) || 0.5;
      const targetX = minX + xRatio * (maxX - minX);
      return { x: targetX, y: targetY };
    }
    // 情况3：在范围内 → 直接返回
    return { x, y };
  }
};



Object.defineProperty (window, 'GuixuManagerInstance', {
 value: { ...GuixuManager, isInitializing: false }, // 赋值真正实例
 writable: true, // 后续可修改
 configurable: true
 });
  if (window.isGuixuInitTriggered === undefined) {
  window.isGuixuInitTriggered = false; // 仅在全局未定义时初始化
  }


 // 绑定APP_READY事件（简化标记，只依赖全局实例）
 eventOn (tavern_events.APP_READY, async () => {
 if (window.isGuixuInitTriggered) {
 console.log ('[源堡 - 防循环] APP_READY 重复触发，已忽略 ');
 return;
 }

 // 首次触发：标记为已执行，避免重复
 window.isGuixuInitTriggered = true;
 await GuixuManager.init(); // 加 await，确保 init 执行完再处理后续

 // 初始化地图系统实例
 mapSystem = new GeorgeMapSystem();
 console.log('[地图系统] 已在主初始化后实例化');


});








})();
 }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>
